I te māharahara ngā AM o Wēra kei ‘rite rātou ki ngā karetao te āhua'
E tūmatakuru ana ētahi AM i te whakaaro ka huria tō rātou taitara ki te MWP (Mema o te Pāremata o Wēra).
I pupū ake nā ngā marohitanga ki te huri i te ingoa o te whakaminenga ki te Pāremata o Wēra.
Kei te māharahara katoa ngā AM puta noa i te awhe tōrangapū ka whakatakēhia rātou.
I kī tētahi AM Reipa i te māharahara tōna rōpū “he rite te tangi ki te Twp me te Pwp."
Mō ngā kaipānui i waho o Wēra: I te reo Wēra ko te twp he rorirori, ā, ko te pwp he hamuti.
Hei tā tētahi AM Plaid “kāore i te rata” te rōpū katoa, ā, kua whakaputahia ētahi atu whakaaro.
I kī tētahi Welsh Conservative i te “tuwhera” tōna rōpū ki te huringa o te rōpū, engari he āhua rite te MWP ki te Muppet (karetao).
I roto i tēnei horopaki he rite te whakahua o te pū w Wēra ki te whakahua o te u a te Ingarihi o Yorkshire.
Ko te Kōmihana Whakaminenga, e tuhituhi ana i te ture hukihuki i tēnei wā hei whakauru i ngā huringa ki te ingoa, i kī: “Ko te whakatau whakamutunga mō te ingoa mō Ngā Mema o te Whakaminenga ka riro mā ngā mema tonu.”
Nā te Ture o te Kāwanatanga o Wēra 2017 i tuku te mana ki te whakaminenga ki te huri i tōna ingoa.
I te Pipiri, i whakaputaina e te Kōmihana ngā otinga o tētahi whakawhitiwhiti kōrero ā-iwi mō ngā marohitanga i tautokona whānuitia kia kīia te whakaminenga ko te Pāremata o Wēra.
Mō te take o te taitara AM, i pai ki te Kōmihana te ko Ngā Mema Pāremata o Wēra, ngā WMP rānei, engari ko te MWP te mea i tino tautokona i roto i ngā whakawhitiwhiti kōrero ā-iwi.
E ai ki te kōrero kei te whakatakoto atu ngā AM i ētahi kōwhiringa kē, engari ka uaua pea ki te rapu i tētahi wāhi e tau ai ngā whakaaro o te katoa mō te Āpiha Whakahaere, a Elin Jones, ā, ko te tūmanako ka tukuna e ia he ture hukihuki mō ngā huringa i roto i ngā wiki.
Ka uru ki te ture mō ngā whakahoutanga ko ētahi atu huringa ki te āhua o te mahi a te whakaminenga, tae atu ki ngā ture mō te whakakāhore i ngā AM me te hanga o te pūnaha komiti.
Kei ngā AM te pōti whakamutunga mō te pātai e pā ana ki te ingoa mō rātou ina tautohea e rātou te ture.
Ka pōti te iwi o Makerōnia i te tāpaetanga pōti mō te whakarerekē i te ingoa o te whenua
Ka pōti ngā kaipōti ā te Rātapu mēnā kia whakarerekēngia te ingoa o tō rātou whenua ki te “Republic of North Macedonia”.
He mea whakatū te pōti hira hei whakatau i tētahi raruraru wā roa me te whenua paetata o Kirihi, inā he takiwā anō tōna ko Makerōnia te ingoa.
Kua roa a Athens e kī ana mā te whakamahi a taua whenua paetata ki te raki taua ingoa kei te kerēmehia ōna whenua, ā, kua roa e whakahē ana e whakahē ana i ā rātou tono mematanga ki te EU me NATO.
I kī te Perehitini o Makerōnia a Gjorge Ivanov, he kaiwhakahē i te tāpaetanga pōti kia whakarerekēngia te ingoa, kāore ia e aro atu ki te pōti.
Engari, ko ngā kaitautoko i te tāpaetanga pōti, tae atu ki te Pirimia a Zoran Zaev, ko te huri i te ingoa te utu noa o te whakauru ki te EU me te NATO.
Ka Ngū Ngā Pere a Hato Mātene na ngā Uauatanga ki ngā Whare Karakia i Harlem.
“I ngā rā o mua, i kī mai ngā kaumātua he pāparakāuta, he whare karakia i tū ki ia kokonga,” te kī a Mr. Adams.
“I tēnei rā, kua kore ngā mea e rua.”
I kī ia i mārama ki te take i kore atu ngā pāparakāuta.
I kī ia “He rerekē te whakawhanaunga a te tangata” i ēnei rā.
“Kua kore e noho ngā ko ngā pāparakāuta ngā wāhi huihui mō te hapori e auau ai te haere ki reira i ia te wā.”
Mō ngā whare karakia, kei te māharahara ia kāore e rawaka te moni mai i te hokohoko rawa ki tērā e pōhēhētia ana e ngā kaiārahi, “mea rawa ake kua hoki anō rātou ki te āhuatanga i te tuatahi.”
Hei tāna, ka whakakapia pea ngā whare karakia ki ngā whaitua whare noho me ngā poraka whare noho kikī ana i te hunga kāore e āwhina ki te tiaki i ngā wāhi whakaruruhau whakamutunga o te takiwā noho.
Hei tāna, “Ko te tokomaha o te hunga hoko i ngā whare noho i roto i ēnei whare he Pākehā, ka mutu hohoro i a rātou te katinga o ēnei whare karakia i te mea ko te āhua nei kāore te nuinga o ēnei tāngata e kuhu ana ki ēnei whare noho e whakauru hei mema ki ēnei whare karakia.”
He mea hanga ngā whare karakia e rua e ngā whakaminenga Pākehā i mua i te huringa o Harlem hei tāone mangumangu - Metropolitan Community i te tau 1870, a Hato Mātene i te tekau tau i muri mai.
I wehe atu te whakaminenga Wēteriana Pākehā taketake i ngā tau o te 1930.
I riro mai te whare i tētahi whakaminenga mangumangu i te karakia i tētahi wāhi tūtata.
I riro a Hato Mātene i tētahi whakaminenga mangumangu i raro i te maru o John Howard Johnson, nāna i takitaki kia tāparetia ngā kaihokohoko i te Tiriti 125 kāore i tuku mahi, whakatairanga rānei i ngā mangumangu, he tiriti matua mō te hokohoko i Harlem.
I tūkinohia te whare e te ahi i te tau 1939, engari i te wā i te whakariterite te pāriha ki te whakatū anō i te whare, i whakahautia e rātou kia mahia he kariona.
Ko te kōrero a te Minita a David Johnson, tama a Pā Johnson me te piki tūranga o i Hato Mātene, mō ngā kariona ko “ngā pere a te rawakore.”
He ingoa kē atu tō te pūkenga i whakatangi i te kariona i te Hōngongoi: “He taonga ahurea”, ā, “he whakatangi puaki.”
I te mōhio anō te pūkenga a Tiffany Ng o te Whare Wānanga o Michigan, koinei te kariona tuatahi i te ao katoa i whakatangihia e tētahi kai-puoro mangumangu, a Dionisio A. Lind, ā, i neke ia ki tētahi karioana nui ake i te Whare Karakia o Riverside i te 18 tau ki mua.
I kī a Mr. Merriweather kāore i whakakapitia ia e Hato Mātene.
I pā mai i roto i ngā marama kua taha ake i Hato Mātene ko ngā whakahaere uaua e pā ana ki ngā kaihoahoa me ngā kaikirimana, nā ngā reimana o te whare karakia ētahi i heri mai, ā, nā te pīhopatanga o Episcopal ētahi.
I tuhi te pīhopatanga - te poari whakahaere o te pāriha, mai i ngā reimana - ki te wēteri i te Hōngongoi me ngā māharahara ka “ka tukuna atu ngā utu” e te pīhopatanga ki te wēteri, ahakoa kāore te wēteri i roto i ngā mahi tono kaihoahoa me ngā kirimana e tukuna atu e te pīhopatanga.
I amuamu ētahi o te pāriha mō te kore e tuwhera o ngā whakahaere a te pīhopatanga.
I whara he tama 13 tau i te pioke i a e ruku kōura ana i te Karepōnia
I ngaua, ā, i whara he tama 13 tau i te Rāhoroi e tētahi pioke i a ia e ruku kōura ana i Karepōnia i te rā whakatuwhera o te wā ruku kōura, te kī a ngā āpiha.
I pā mai tēnei i te i mua tonu i te 7 a.m. i te wāhi tūtata ki te Beacon’s Beach i Encinita.
I kōrero a Chad Hammel ki a KSWB-TV i San DIego i te ruku ia me ōna hoa mō te hāwhe haora i te ata o te Rāhoroi, ā, kātahi ia ka rongo i te tama e tīorooro ana kia āwhinatia ia, ā, kātahi ka kau atu rātou me tētahi rōpū ki te tango mai i a ia i te wai.
I kī a Hammel i e tuatahi i pōhēhē ia i te umere noa ia nā te mau i tētahi kōura, engari “kātahi ia mōhio i te tīwaha mai ia, ‘kua ngaua ahau!
Kua ngaua ahau!’
Kua pōhahatia katoatia tōna āhei,” te kī a Hammel i tana kitenga i te tama.
“I karanga atu ahau ki te katoa kia puta mai i te wai: ‘He pioke kei roto i te wai!’” te kōrero anō a Hammel.
He mea heri ia mā te waka topatopa ki te Hōhipera Tamariki o Rady i San Diego, ā, kei te taumaha ia.
Kāore i te mōhiotia te momo pioke nāna ia i ngau.
I kī te Kāpene Whakaora a Larry Giles i tētahi whakamārama pānui pāpāho i kitea he pioke i roto i te takiwā i ngā wiki ki mua, engari ko te whakarite i taua wā ehara i te momo pioke mōrearea.
I kī anō a Giles i tino whetuki ngā wharanga o te pārurenga ki te taha o runga o te tinana.
I katia e ngā āpiha te urunga ki te takutai mai i Ponto Beach i Casablad ki Swami i Ecinitas mō te 48 haora mō ngā kaupapa tūhuratanga me te haumaru.
I kī a Giles neke atu i te 135 ngā momo pioke i roto i te takiwā, engari ko te nuinga ehara i te mōrearea.
Kei te whakariterite a Sainsbury’s ki te whakauru ki te mākete rerehua o te UK
Kei te whakataetae a Sainsbury’s ki a Boots, Superdrug me Debenhams me te āhua kauhanga o ngā toa me ngā kaimahi mātanga.
Nā tētahi kōkiri nui ki te mākete rerehua o te £2.8 piriona, e tipu haere tonu ana, ā, me te heketanga o ngā tauhokohoko pūweru me ngā taputapu whare, ka whakamātauria ngā kauhanga rerehua nui ake i ngā toa 11 puta noa i te motu, ā, ka haria ki ētahi toa anō ā tērā tau mēnā ka angitu.
Kua ōrua te haumitanga ki te wāhanga rerehua ki te rapa a ngā hokomaha i ngā huarahi hei whakakī i ngā wāhi tarenga i whakamahia mō ngā pouaka whakaata i mua, ngā ngaruiti me ngā taputapu whare.
I kī a Sainsbury’s ka huaruatia te rahinga o ana tukunga rerehua atu ki te 3,000, tae atu ki ngā momo pērā i a Revlon, Essie, Tweezeman me Dr. PawPaw mō te wā tuatahi.
Ka nui ake te whiwhi wāhi o ngā huinga hua a L'Oreal, Maybelline me Burt’s Bees i te taha o ngā wāhi momo ōrite ki ērā e kitea ana i ngā toa pērā i a Boots.
Kei te whakatārewa anō te hokomaha i tana huinga hua whakapaipai kia noho pai ai te nuinga o ngā hua ki te hunga kaitipu - he mea tēnei e tino tonoa haere e ngā kaihoko tamariki ake.
I tua atu i tēnei, ka whakamātautauhia e te kaihokohoko kakara a Fragance Shop ngā wāhi i whakawātea mai i ngā toa a Sainsbury’s, ko te mea tuatahi i huakina i Croydon, te tonga o Rānana, i tērā wiki, ā, ko te mea tuarua ka huakina i Selly Oak, Birmingham, hei tēnei tau.
Nā ngā hokohoko tuihono me te neke ki ngā hokohoko kai iti i ia rā i ngā toa paetata kua mate ngā hokomaha ki te whakawhere i te tangata kia haere ki a rātou.
I kī a Mike Coupe, te tumuaki o Sainsbury’s, ka ōrite haere te āhua o ngā wāhi hoko ki ngā toa hoko rawa i a ia ka whakapātari ki ngā toa hekeutu a Aldi me Lidl me ngā ratonga nui ake, hua kore-kai hoki.
I whakaurua haeretia e Sainsbury’s ngā wāhi hoko Argos i roto i ngā toa tino maha me te whakauru anō i ngā Habitats maha mai i tana hokotanga mai i ngā kamupene toa e rua i ngā e rua ki mua, me te kī kua piki ake ngā hokohoko kai me te whaihua o ēnei hokotanga.
I hinga te whakamātau o mua a te hokomaha ki te whakahou i ana wāhanga rerehua me te taka rongoā.
I whakamātauria e Sainsbury’s tētahi pātui ngātahi me Boots i ngā tau tōmua o te 2000, engari i mutu te hononga i te pupūtanga o te raruraru mō te āhua o te wehewehe i ngā moni puta mai i ngā toa taka rongoā i roto i ana hokomaha.
Ka puta ake te rautaki hou i muri i te hokotanga a Sainsbury’s i tana pakihi taka rongoā e 281 ngā toa ki a Celesio, te rangatira o ngā toa Lloyds Pharmacy, mō te £125m, i te toru tau ki mua.
Ko te kōrero he wāhanga nui tō Lloyds i roto i te mahere, mā te tāpiri i ngā tūmomo hua tiaki whai rawa, tae atu ki a La Roche-Posay me Vichy i roto i ngā toa e whā.
I kī a Paul Mills-Hicks, te tumuaki arumoni a Sainsbury's: “Kua takahuria e mātou te āhua o ā mātou kauhanga rerehua hei whakarei ake i te wāhi mō ā mātou kiritaki.
I tuku haumi anō mātou ki ngā kaimahi mātanga kia wātea ai ki te tuku tohutohu.
I hangaia ā mātou momo kia hāngai ki ia hiahia, ā, mā ngā wāhi whakapoapoa, haratau hoki kua noho mai mātou hei tino ūnga rerehua e whakapātari ana i ngā āhuatanga tawhito o te hokohoko.
Kei te ‘whakatakariri’ a Peter Jones i muri i te kounu a Holly Willoughby mai i tētahi whakaritenga o te £11 miriona
I te ‘whakatakariri’ te whetū o Dragons Den a Peter Jones i muri i te kounu a te whakaatu pouaka whakaata a Holly Willoughby i tētahi whakaritenga o te £11 miriona me tana pakihi āhua noho kia arotahi ia ki āna kirimana hou me Marks and Spencer me ITV
Kāore a Willoughby i te wātea mō tā rātou momo taputapu kāinga, taonga hoki a Truly.
He pānga tō te pakihi a te tokorua ki te kamupene a Gwyneth Paltrow a Goop.
I whakaputaina e te kaiwhakaatu o This Morning, 37 tau ōna tau, tōna wehenga i runga i a Instagram.
I te whakatakariri te whetū o Dragons Den a Peter Jones ki a Holly Willoughby mō te kounu mai i tā rātou pakihi āhua noho whai hua i mua tonu i te whakaūnga - kia arotahi ia ki āna ake kirimana nui me Marks & Spence me ITV.
I kī ētahi i te “whakatakariri” a Jones i te whākitanga a te wahine pūrotu o te pouaka whakaata i roto i tētahi hui uaua i te Tūrei i te tari matua o ana pakihi i Marlow, Bukinghamshire - neke atu i te £1.5 miriona te wāriu - kua kore ia e wātea ki te whakapau kaha ki tā rāua pakihi taputapu whare, taonga hoki a Truly.
I whakaritea te pakihi ki te pakihi Goop a Gwyneth Paltrow, ā, ko te whakaaro ka huaruatia ngā rawa a Willoughby ki te £11 miriona te wāriu.
I a Willoughby, 37 tau, e kōrero ana i runga i a Instagram mō tana wehenga, i te wehe a Jones i Piritana ki te haere ki tētahi o ōna kāinga hararei.
I kī tētahi: “Ko Truly te tino kaupapa a Holly.
Ko te tikanga koinei tana anamata wā roa mō te rua tekau tau e heke iho nei.
I tino ohorere ngā tāngata katoa ki tana whakatau.
I tino tumeke ngā tāngata i te pānga mai o tēnei i te Tūrei, i te mea kua tata tonu ki te whakarewatanga.
Kikī ana tētahi whare putunga i ngā rawa i te Tari Matua o Marolow, ā, kua reri ēnei kia hokona atu.
E whakapono ana ngā mātanga e hia miriona te utu ki te pakihi o te wehenga o te kaiwhakaatu o This Morning, ko ia hoki tētahi o ngā whetū tino whai hua o Piritana, nā ngā haumi nui ki ngā hua mai i ngā kuihana me ngā kānara ki ngā kākahu me ngā taputapu whare, ā, me te takaware pea anō ki te whakarewatanga.
Koinei pea momotutanga o te taura here hoa i waenga i a rāua.
Kua roa nei a Willoughby, e toru ana tamariki, rāua ko tana hoa tāne a Dan Baldwin e piri tata ana ki a Jones rāua ko tana hoa wahine a Tara Capp mō te tekau tau.
Nā Willoughby i whakatū a Truly i te taha o Capp i te tau 2016, ā, i uru atu a Jones, 52 ōna tau, hei heamana i te Poutūterangi.
Hararei tahi ngā tokowhā nei, ā, 40 ōrau te wāhanga o Jones i roto i te umanga mahi pikitia a Baldwin.
Kua uru a Willoughby hei kanohi mō te pakihi o M&S, ā, ka whakakapi ia i a Ant McPartlin hei kaihautū o te I’m A Celebrity a ITV.
Ko te kōrero a tētahi e tata ana ki a Jones i te pō rā, “E kore mātou e kōrero mō ana take pākihi.”
He kōrero uaua ‘kātahi ka aroha māua ki a māua’
I te kōrero ngahau ia mō ngā whakahē ki a ia mai i te hunga pāpāho mō ana kōrero e ai ki ētahi “kāore e tika mō te Perehitina” me te kōrero pai mō te rangatira o Korea ki te Raki.
He aha i nui ai ngā tukutanga a Perehitini Trump?
Te whakatoi a Trump i roto i tana reo “kaipānui karere”.
“Kāore he paku aha i tukuna e au.”
I kī ia kei te hiahia a Kim kia hui anō rāua i muri i tā rāua hui tuatahi i Hingapoa i te Pipiri i kī a Trump i tutuki te hiahia o taua hui mō te whakakore i ngā pahū karihia a Korea ki te Raki.
Engari kua tārewa ngā whakariterite whakakore pahū karihi.
Neke atu i te toru marama i muri i te hui o te Pipiri i Hingapoa, i kōrero atu te takawaenga kāwanatanga matua a Korea ki te Raki a Ri Yong Ho ki ngā rangatira o te ao i te Whakaminenga Whānui o te U.N kāore te Raki i te kite i tētahi “whakautu hāngai” mai i te U.S. ki ngā nekehanga whakaore tōmua a Korea ki te raki.
Engari kē, i kī ia, kei te mau tonu i te U.S. ngā aukatinga pēpēhi i a rātou.
He pai ake te tirohanga a Trump i roto i tana kauhau huihuinga.
“Ka rawe ā mātou mahi me Korea ki te Raki,” tana kī.
“Kāore tātou i te pakanga ki a Korea ki te Raki.
E hia miriona tāngata ka mate.
Nā, he tino hoahoa māua ināianei.”
I kī ia he tino nui ngā painga i puta i ana mahi hei whakapai ake i ngā whanaungatanga me Kim - te whakamutu i ngā whakamātautau tākirirangi, te āwhina ki te tuku i ngā mau herehere me te whakahoki mai i ngā kōhiwi o ngā pāraeroa o Amerika ki te kāinga.
Me te aha, i tautokona e ia tana aronga rerekē mō te kōrero whanaungatanga me Kim.
“He māmā te noho hei perehitini, tē whakamātautau ai ki te whakauru mai i ngā tāngata 10,000 kei waho ki roto i tēnei taiwhanga kikī, tata ki te 200 noa ngā tāngata e tū mai nā,” te kōrero a Trump, e tohu ana ki te minenga e tū mai ana i mua i a ia.
Anea Kau Ana he Moutere e te Ngaru Taitoko me te Rū Nui i Initonīhia, Tokomaha Rawa Atu Ngā Tāngata i Mate
I muri i te rū o Lombok, i kīia atu ngā whakahaere kāwanatanga-kore kāore rātou i te hiahiatia.
Ahakoa neke atu i te 10 ōrau o te taupori o Lombok i noho kore kāinga, kāore i whakapuakitia he aituā ā-motu, he whakaritenga tōmua mō te tono i ngā āwhina ā-ao.

Ahakoa kei te whakaritea e Save the Children tētahi rōpū hei haere ki Palu, kāore i te mōhiotia mēnā ka taea e ngā kaimahi o tāwāhi te mahi ki reira.
I kī a Mr. Sutopo, te kaikōrero o te tari aituā ā-motu, i tātarihia e ngā āpiha o Initonīhia ngā āhuatanga i Palu ki te kite mēnā ka whakaaetia ngā tari o te ao ki te tautoko i ngā mahi āwhina.
Nā ngā rū e pā haere tonu mai ki Initonīhia, kāore taua iwi i te paku takatū mō ngā āhuatanga kino o te taiao.
Ahakoa kua hangaia ngā whakaruru ngaru taitoko i Aceh, kāore ēnei i te kitea i ētahi atu ākau.
Nā te kore whakapū whakatūpato i te ngaru taitoko i Palu, ahakoa i puta tētahi whakatūpato, tētahi take i matemate atu ai ngā tāngata.
He uaua te nekeneke haere i waenga i ngā moutere maha o Initonīhia, ahakoa te wā.
Ka uaua ake ngā mahi whakaraupapa i roto i ngā aituā tūturu.
Kei te haere atu tētahi kaipuke hōhipera ki Palu, i Lombok e tau ana mō te whakamaimoa i ngā pārurenga o te rū, engari tata ki te toru rā te roa ka tae ki te aituā hou.
Ko te kaupapa nui a Perehitini Joko Widodo o te tana whakahau pōti ko te whakapai ake i te hanganga karukaru o Initonīhia, ā, kua whakapaua e ia he moni nui ki ngā rori me ngā rērawe.
Engari kua roa te kāwanatanga o Mr. Joko e raru ana i te poto o te takarepa o te pūtea i a ka whakamātau kia pōtihia anō ā tērā tau.

Mātakitaki: I whakapau kaha a Daniel Sturridge o Liverpool kia piro ia, ā, ka ōrite ngā tatau ki a Chelsea
I ora i a Daniel Sturridge a Liverpool mai i tētahi hinganga Premier League ki a Chelsea me tana piro i te meneti 89 i tētahi Rāhoroi i Stamford Bridge i Rānana.
I whiwhi a Sturridge i te pōro mai i Xherdan Shaqiri, ā, tata ki te 30 iari tana tawhiti mai i te wāhi piro o Chelsea, ka mutu i muri tana kapa 1-0.
I peia atu e ia te pōro ki tana taha mauī i mua i tana whananga i te pōro ki te taha o te tawhiti o te pou piro.
I rere te pōro ki runga ake o te pāka ka haere ki te kokona matau o te neti.
Nāwai, ka tau te pōro i muri i a Kepa Arrzabalaga, ā, ka tau ki te neti.
“I te ngana ahau ki te tae atu ki taua wāhi, kia whiwhi ahau i te pōro me te aha he rite tonu te pei whakamua haere a ngā kaitākaro pērā i a Shaq i te pōro, ā, ka whakapau kaha ahau ki te whakarite kia nui te wā ki ahau,” te kī a Sturridge ki a LiverpoolFC.com.
“I kite ahau i a Kante e haere mai ana, kotahi taku pānga ki te pōro, ā, kāore noa iho i tino whakaaroarohia e au kātahi ka whanaia atu.”
I mua a Chelsea 1-0 i te wā haurua i muri i te piro a te toki o Belgian a Eden Hazard i te meneti 25.

Kātahi a Kovacic ka pāhi atu me te whiwhi anō i te pōro i te weherua o te whira.
Ā, kātahi ka pāhi whakamuatia atu e ia te pōro, ki a Hazard i roto i te pāka.
Kāore i mau i te hoariri a Hazard, ā, ka rere te pōro ki te neti o tērā taha mā te whana waewae mauī ki muri i a Alisson Becker o Liverpool.

Kei te haere tonu ngā tūhuratanga, inā kua kī ngā pirihimana kei te whakamōhio haere tonu rātou i te whānau o te pārurenga.
Kei te whakamātau he kaitaraiwa tekehi e noho ana i Grayson Mews ki te hoki ki tōna whare noho engari kei te mea atu ngā pirihimana kāore i te whakaaetia te tangata kia puta, kia kuhu rānei i te whare.
Ka nui tōna ohorere i te rongotanga mō te raruraru i pā mai.

Ko te whakapakoko o Cromwell a te Pāremata te tohu whakamahara o nā noa nei i whakakinotia e te tohetohe ‘te raweke hītori’
Ka āhua tika kia mōna i taruweku haere, pērā i tā te iwi Taliban, ngā taonga tuku iho, whakapono maha o Ingarani e ana apataki Puritan.
Engari hei tā te Cromwell Society he “mahi rorirori” te whakaaro o Mri Crick, ā, kei te “whakamātau ia ki te raweke i te hītori.”
I kī a John Goldsmith, heamana o te Cromwell Society: “Kāore e kore ka pupū ake te whakapakoko o Oliver Cromwell i waho o te Whare Kīngi o Westminster hei pārure i roto i ngā tohetohe onāianei mō te whakakoretanga o ngā whakapakoko.
Kāore i whakahautia, i mahia rānei e Cromwell ngā mahi whakakore whakapakoko o mua i roto i ngā pakanga Ingarihi ā-iwi.
Tērā pea ka whakaherea ko tētahi atu Cromwell mō ngā mahi kē a tōna tipuna a Thomas nō te rau tau o mua atu.
He whakaaturanga ngā kōrero whakamārama rawe rawa a Tā William Hamo Thornecroft i ngā whakaaro o te rau tau 19, i roto hoki i ngā mahi a ngā kaituhi hītori i whakapono te nuinga he mea nui tonu kia whakanuitia.
I kī atu a Mr Goldsmith ki The Sunday Telegraph: “Ko te whakaaro a te tokomaha, otirā he maha atu i te wāhanga whakamutunga o te rau tau 19 tēnā i tēnei rā, he kaiwhakangungu a Cromwell i te pāremata mai i ngā āhuatanga o waho, otirā ko te arikitanga.
He tohenga hītori tēnei e haere tonu ana mēnā kei te tika rawa atu te whakamārama.
Ko te mea e tino mōhiotia ana nā ngā pakanga i waenga o te rau tau 17 i ahu i te whanaketanga o tō tātou iwi, e mōhiotia ana ko Cromwell tētahi tangata e whakakanohi ana i tētahi taha o taua tohe.
Me whakanui, me whakamaumahara anō ana whakatutukitanga hei Roera Kaitiaki.”
I Whakamatea e te Poaka tētahi Kaiahuwhenua Hainamana
I whakamatea tētahi kaiahuwhenua e tētahi poaka i roto i tētahi mākete i te puāwanga o Haina, e ai ki ngā pūrongo pānui pāpāho.
I tohua ko te ingoa whānau anake o te tangata ko “Yuan,” i te kitenga kua mate ia kua motukia tōna iatuku, ā, kua toto katoa ia i tētahi iari poaka i te mākete i te porowini o Liupanshui i Guizhou, te pūrongo a te South China Morning Post i te Rātapu.
Ka whakarite tētahi kaiahuwhenua poaka ki te wero i ngā ārainga mate ki ngā poaka i tētahi iari poaka i te 30 o Haratua, 2005 i Xining o te Porowini o Qinghai, Haina.
E kīia ana i haere tahi ia me tana whanaunga mai i te porowini tūtata o Yunnan i te Wenerei ki te hoko i ngā poaka 15 i te mākete.
I te ata o muri mai, ka kitea ia e tōna whanaunga kua mate kē, me te huaki o tētahi kūaha ki te iari poaka i te taha.
I kī ia he tāria ana poaka mā nui i roto i te iari me te toto i tōna waha.
I whakaūtia e tētahi aromatawai whare wā nā te poaka 550 pauna te taumaha i whakamate i te kaiahuwhenua, e ai ki te pūrongo.
Kua toto katoa, kua mutumutu katoa ngā waewae o taku whanaunga,” te kī a te whanaunga, e kīia ana ko “Wu” tōna ingoa whānau, e ai ki te Guiyang Evening News.
I whakaaturia a Yuan e ngā ataata haumarutanga e kuhu ana ki te mākete i te 4.4.40 am o te Tāite e whāngai ana i ana poaka.
I kitea tōna tinana i te haora i muri mai.
Ko te kararehe nāna ia i whakamate ehara nā Yuan, tana whanaunga rānei.
I kī atu tētahi kaiwhakahaere mākete ki te Evening News kua rakaina te poaka kia kaua e whakaeke i ētahi atu, i te wā e kohikohi whakaaturanga ana ngā pirihimana i te wāhi.
E ai ki te kōrero kei te whakariterite te whānau o Yuan me ngā mana o te mākete mō ngā paremata mō tōna matenga.
Ahakoa he tino rerekē tēnei, kua kitea i mua ētahi āhuatanga o te poaka e whakaeke ana i te tangata.
I te tau 2016, i whakaekehia he wahine me tōna hoa tāne e tētahi poaka i tā rāua pāmu i Massachusetts, ā, i whara kino te tāne.
I te tekau tau ki mua, i tāmia he kaiahuwhenua o Wēra e tētahi poaka 650 pauna ki tōna tarakihana, ā, kia tae atu tana wahine ki te pana i te kararehe.
I muri i te kaitanga o tētahi kaiahuwhenua o Oregon e ōna poaka i te tau 2012, i kī tētahi kaiahuwhenua o Manitoba ki a CBC News i te nuinga o te wā ehara te poaka i te kararehe riri engari ki te rongo i te toto he pēnei i te “whakahau”.
“Kei te tākaro kē ngā poaka.
He kinikini kē, he mahira ... kāore i te whakamamae i a koe.
Ko te mea me kē me tika tō whakaute,” tana kī.
Ko te patapataiāwhā te kai ki te puāwanga o te US mai i ngā mahuetanga o Huripari Rosa
E ai ki ngā tohu huarere, kei te ngoikore haere a Huripari Rosa i te wā ka hipa i ngā wai mātao o te takutai raki o Mehiko.
Engari, ka tau mai i a Rosa ngā ua waipuke puta noa i te raki o Mehiko i te puāwanga o U.S. i roto i ngā rā e heke iho.
He 85 mph te kaha o ngā hau o Rosa, he Huripari Momo 1, hei te 5 a.m. wā Rāwhiti i te Rātapu, ā, i te 385 maero i te puāwanga o Punta Eugenia, Mehiko.
Ko te matapae ka neke whakateraki a Rosa hei te Rātapu.
Heoi, kei te puta he pārua i runga ake o Te Moananui-a-Kiwa, ā, ka neke atu ki te Tai Hauāuru o te U.S. I te neke haerenga atu o Rosa ki te kūrae o Baja California ā te Mane hei āwhā pārūrū ka tīmata ki te pei atu i te haukū pāruru hōhonu ki te raki ki te puāwanga o U.S.
Atu ki te 10 īnihi te ua ka puta i a Rosa i ētahi wāhanga o Mehiko ā te Mane.
Ā, ka puta te patapataiāwhā i te pahekotanga o te haukū me te pārua e whakatata mai ana ki te Puāwanga hei ngā rā e heke iho nei.
I te takiwā, ka pā mai te waipuke ohorere mōrearea nā te 1 ki te 4 īnihi o te ua, ngā para e rere ana me ngā horo pea i te koraha.
E 2 ki te 3 īnihi i te haora i ētahi wāhi ka puta i ngā haukū pārūrū hōhonu, otirā i ngā wāhi o te raki o Nevada me Arizona.
Atu ki te 2 ki te 4 īnihi ua e tūmanakohia ana i ētahi wāhi o te Puāwanga, otirā i te nuinga o Arizona.
Ka taea pea ngā waipuke ohorere me te kino haere o ngā āhuatanga nā te marara o te āhua o te ua pārūrū.
Kaua rawa e haere ki te koraha mā raro ina ko te matapae ko ngā ua pārūrū.
Tērā pea ka rere te wai ānō he awa i ngā pākohu, ā, ka pupuhi ngā hau titipārera me te rere o te puehu i ngā rautupu.
He patapataiāwhā ka tau mai ki ētahi wāhi o te takutai o Southern California i te pārua e haere mai ana.
Ka taea pea ngā ua o te īnihi haurua, e taea ai pā mai ai ngā rerenga para iti me ngā rori mania.
Koinei ngā ua tuatahi o te rohe mō te wāhanga tau ua.
Ka whakatata haere atu ētahi ua pārūrū ki Arizona hei te pō o te Rātapu ki te tīmatanga o te Mane, ā, ka whānui haere atu te ua ki ngā wāhi i te pō o te Mane me te Tūrei.
Ka hora te patapataiāwhā ki Kokonga e Whā hei te Tūrei atu ki te pō o te Wenerei.
Ka tino rerekē haere te pāmahana i te Whiringa-ā-nuku puta noa i te U.S. i te makariri haeretanga o te Kōpako Raro, engari ka noho mahana tonu te wāhi pārūrū.
I ētahi wā ka tino rerekē te pāmahana i roto i ngā takiwā.
Ka tētahi tino tauira o ngā rerekētanga nui o ngā pāmahana i waenganui o te U.S. hei te Rātapu.
Tata ki te 20-waeine te rerekētanga o te pāmahana i waenga i a Kansas City, Missouri, me Omaha, Nebraska me St. Louis me Des Moines, Iowa.
I roto i ngā rā e heke nei, ka hiahia te mahana taweke o te raumati ki te tipu haere me te whakawhānui anō.
Kō te matapae mō te nuinga o waenga me te rāwhiti o te U.S. ka mahana te tīmatanga o te Whiringa-ā-nuku me ngā pāmahana o te 80 mai i ngā Mānia o te Tonga ki te Whakarua.
Ka tae pea a New York City ki te 80 waeine hei te Tūrei, tata ki te 10 nui ake tērā o te toharite.
E tohu ana tā mātou matapae wā roa ki ngā tūponotanga nui mō ngā pāmahana nui ake i te toharite mō te taha rāwhiti o te U.S. i te haurua tuatahi o te Whiringa-ā-nuku.
Nui atu i te 20 miriona ngā tāngata i mātakitaki i te whakawātanga o Brett Kavanaugh
Neke atu i te 20 miriona ngā tāngata i mātakitaki i ngā taunakitanga tāuteute a te tautoko Kōti Matua a Brett Kavanaugh me te wahine i tuku whakapae taitōkai mōna i pā mai i ngā tau o te 1980, a Christine Blasey Ford, i ngā whatunga pouaka whakaata e ono.
Heoi, kei te haere tonu te komutunga tōrangapū, i haukotia e ngā kaiwhakapāhō ngā whakaaturanga noa mō te whakaaturanga ohorere i te Paraire: he whakaaetanga i whakaritea e Sen. Jeff Flake o Arizona kia whakahaerehia he tūhuratanga mō te kotahi ki ngā whakapae.
I kī a Ford ki te Senate Judiciary Committee e tino pono rawa atu ia i kōrapua ia e Kavanaugh i a ia i te haurangi, ā, i ngana ia ki te unu i ōna kākahu i tētahi pāti kura tuarua.
I kī a Kavanaugh i roto i tana kauhau manawawera, kei te tino pono rawa atu ia kāore i puta tēnā āhuatanga.
Te āhua nei neke atu i te 20,4 miriona ngā tāngata i pūrongohia e Nielsen i mātakitaki i tērā i te Paraire.
I te tatau te kamupene i te hunga mātakitaki toharite i CBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel me MSNBC.
Kāore i wātea tonu mai ngā whika mō ētahi atu whatunga nā rātou i whakaatu, tae atu ki a PBS, C-SPAN me te Fox Business Network.
Ā, i te nuinga o te wā he uaua ki a Nielsen te ine i ngā tāngata e mātaki ana i rō tari.
Kia mārama ai, he ōrite tērā rahinga hunga mātakitaki ki tētahi kēmu whiringa whāiti, te Academy Awards rānei.
He nui ake te hunga mātakitaki a Fox News Channel, i tino tautoko ngā kaiwhakaatu whakaputa whakaaro i te kopounga o Kavanaugh, me ngā kaimātakitaki toharite o te 5.69 miriona i te wā o te whakawātanga rā katoa, te kī a Nielsen.
I tuarua a ABC me ngā kaimātakitaki 3.26 miriona.
E 3.1 miriona ā CBS, e 2.94 miriona ā NBC, e 2.89 miriona ā MSNBC, ā, e 2.52 ā CNN, te kī a Nielsen.
I te kaha tonu te whaiwhaitia i muri i te whakawātanga.
Ko Flake te tangata nui i roto i ngā whakaaturanga i te Paraire.
I muri i te whakaputanga tauākī a te tari o te kaitōrangapū o te Republican nei e kī ana ia ka pōti ia mō Kavanaugh, i mau ia i runga i ngā kāmera a CNN me CBS i te ata o te Paraire e pokea ana e ngā kaiporotū i a ia e kuhu ana ki tētahi ararewa ki tētahi whakawātanga Komiti Whakawā.
I te titiro whakararo ia mō tētahi wā roa i a ia e waua ana, i whakaaturia matawātia i runga CNN.
“Kei konei ahau e tū ana ki mua i a koe,” te kōrero a tētahi wahine.
“Kei te kōrero pono ia ki te motu?
I kīia atu ia, “he mana ōu engari kāore he mana ō ngā wāhine.””
I kī a Flake i whakaputaina e tana tari he tauākī me te kī, i mua i te katinga o te ararewa, ka nui ake ana kōrero i te whakawātanga a te komiti.
I te whakaaturia matawātia e ngā whatunga taura, pāpāho i ngā haora i muri mai, i te nohotanga a te Komiti Whakawā ki te pōti kia kauneketia te kōharitanga a Kavanaugh ki te Senate whānui mō te pōti.
Engari i kī a Flake ka pōti anake ia i runga i te mōhio kei tirotirohia e te FBI ngā whakapae mō te tangata e kōhiritia ā te wiki e heke iho, e whakahautia ana e te tokoiti o ngā Democratics.
I āhua whakaawetia a Flake i roto i ngā kōrerorero me tana hoa, a Democratic Sen. Chris Coons.
I muri i tētahi kōrerorero me Coons me ētahi atu kaiwhakatau ture i muri mai, ka tukuna e Flake tana whakatau.
He mana nui te kōwhiringa a Flake, i te mea i kitea kāore i rahi ngā pōti a te Republicans kia whakaaetia a Kavanaugh me te kore tūhuratanga.
Nā Perehitini Trump i whakatuwhera i te tūhuratanga a te FBI ki ngā whakapae mō Kavanaugh.

I whakaputaina e ngā āpiha tētahi ataata o te whawhai i waenga i a Sims rāua ko Simpson, ā, i kī a Sims i ngaro i ngaro ana mōhiti i roto i te whawhai.

Ka tuhaina e te puia te pungarehu ki Mexico City
Kua tae ngā pungarehu mai i te puia o Popocatepetl ki ngā takiwā noho o te raki o te tāonenui o Mehiko.
I whakatūpatohia ngā tāngata o Mehiko e te National Center for Disaster Prevention i te Rāhoroi kia kaua e tata atu ki te puia i muri i te rongo i ngā hohenga o te rua puia, ā, 183 ngā haurehu me ngā pungarehu i rēhitatia i roto i te 24 haora.
I te aroturuki haeretia e te pokapū ngā haruru me ngā rū maha.
I whakaaturia e ngā atahanga i runga pāpāho pāpori ngā papanga whāiti o ngā pungarehu e uhi ana i ngā wini motuka o mua i ngā takiwā noho o Mexico City pērā i a Xochimilco.
Kua kitea e ngā kaimātainuku kua nui ake ngā hohenga i te puia e 45 maero (72 kiromita) i te paeroa o te tāone matua mai i te rū 7.1 te nui i ngarue ai te pū o Mehiko i te Mahuru 2017.
Kua roa e hohe ana te puia e mōhiotia ana ko “Don Goyo” mai i te 1994.
Tukituki ai ngā pirihimana me ngā kaikōkiri tino rangatiratanga o Catalan i mua o te huritau o te pōti mana motuhake.
E ono ngā tāngata i hopukia e te ture i Barcelona i te Rāhoroi whai muri i ngā tukitukitanga i waenga i ngā kaiporotū tino rangatiratanga me ngā pirihimana whakahārangi, ā, i te urunga atu o te hunga mano tini ki ngā porotū tāwhai hei tohu i te huritau o te pōti wehewehe i a Catalonia mō te kounutanga.
I te peia atu tētahi rōpū kaikōkiri tino rangatiratanga e ngā pirihimana i a rātou e makamaka ana epaepa ana i ngā hēki ki ngā pirihimana me ngā peita paura, i tutū haere ai ngā puehu pōuri i ngā tiriti, ko ngā tiriti e muia ana e ngā tūruhi i te nuinga o te wā.
I pakaru mai ngā whawhai i muri mai me te whakamahi a ngā pirihimana i ā rātou rākau hei pēhi i ngā whawhai.
He tino roa te wā e karanga haere ana ngā rōpū mana motuhake i te “No forgetting, no forgiveness” me te tuki atu ki ngā kaiporotū uniana e karanga ana rātau “Long live Spain.”
Tekau mā ngā tāngata i whakamaimoatia mō ngā wharanga iti noa mai i ngā porotū, e ai ki te pūrongo a te hunga pāpāho paetata.
Kei te kaha tonu te mānukanuka i roto i te rohe whai i te mana motuhake i te kotahi tau i muri i te tāpaetanga o te 1 o Whiringa-ā-nuku, i kiia e takahi ture e Madrid engari i whakanuitia e ngā kaikōkiri tino rangatiratanga o Catalans.
He tino nui rawa te tahuri o ngā kaipōti kia noho motuhake rātou, ahakoa i iti noa te hunga i pōti, ā, ko te nuinga o te hunga whakahē kāore i pōti.
E ai ki ngā mana o Catalan tata ki te 1000 ngā tāngata i whara i tērā tau whai muri i te whakamātau a ngā pirihimana ki te aukati i te pōti i ngā wāhi pōti puta noa i te rohe i roto i ngā whawhai kino.
I pō takoto te rōpū kaikōkiri tino rangatiratanga i te pō o te Paraire kia kore ai e porotū, hei tautoko i ngā pirihimana.
I haere tonu ngā porotū engari i mate rātou ki te haere mā tētahi atu ara.
Hei tā Narcis Termes, 68 tau, he kaimahi hiko i haere ki te porotū tino rangatiratanga me tana hoa wahine, kua makere atu te pono ka riro mai i a Catalonia tō rātau mana motuhake.
“I tērā tau tētahi wā tino rawe rawa atu mō mātau.
I kite ahau i ngā roimata o ōku mātua e heke ana i runga i te hari i te mea ka āhei rātou ki te pōti, engari kua raru mātou ināianei,” tana kōrero.
Ahakoa i hira te puta o te ihu i ngā potitanga ā-rohe i tērā Hakihea, i uaua te anga whakamua haere tonu a ngā rōpū mana motuhake o Catalan i tēnei nā te maha o ō rātau kaiārahi i whakamanene i a rātau anō, kei rō herehere e tatari ana kia whakawāngia rātou mō tā rātou whakariterite i te tāpaetanga me te whakapuaki i te mana motuhake.
Hei tā Joan Puig, 42 tau, he kaiaka mīhini i hopu i te porotū mā tana waea hei tautoko i ngā pirihimana, he mea takitaki ngā taupatupatu e ngā kaitōrangapū o ngā taha e rua.
“Kei te taumaha haere kē atu,” tana kōrero.
I te Rāhoroi, i whakapuaki a Oriol Junqueras, tētahi o ngā kaiārahi e iwa o Catalan e mau ana ki rō herehere i mua i te whakawātanga mai rā anō i tērā tau, ka tū ia i roto i ngā pōtitanga mō te Pāremata o Uropi ā tērā tau.
“Ko te tū hei kaitono mō ngā pōtitanga o Uropi te āhuatanga pai rawa hei whakahorihori i te pāheketanga o ngā uara manapori me ngā tāmitanga a te kāwanatanga o Pāniora,” tana kōrero.

Nā te piro a Menga ka toa a Livingston 1-0 ki a Rangers
I toa a Livingston i te piro tuatahi a Dolly Menga
I ohorere katoa a Rangers i a Livingston, i piki ake mai i raro, kia pā ai te hinganga tuarua ki a Steven Gerrard i roto i ana kēmu 18 hei kaiwhakahaere i te karapu nō Ibrox.
Ko te piro a Dolly Menga te rerekētanga, ā, ka neke te kapa o Gary Holt ki te tūranga tuarua i te taha i a Hibernian.
Kāore anō te kapa o Gerrard kia toa i waho o te kāinga i roto i te Premiership i tēnei tau, ā, kei te tūtaki rānei ki a Hearts ā te Rātapu, ā, kei muri mai rātou mā te 8 kaute.

Heoi, kua ono tākaro ināianei kāore anō a Livingston kia hinga i roto i te wāhanga, ā, kāore anō te kaiako matua a Holt kia hinga mai i tana whakakapi i a Kenny Millar i tērā marama.
Kāore i ū ētahi whai wāhitanga o Livingston ki ngā manuhiri ngoikore.
Ko te tikanga kei mua noa atu te kapa o Holt i mua i te pirotanga, nā te torotika o ā rātou kōkiri i uaua ai ki a Rangers.

I mauri tau te haukāinga ki te tuku i a Rangers ki te tākaro i mua i a rātou i runga i te mōhio ka whakararuraru i a rātou te manuhiri mai i ngā wāhi whakarite.
Ā, nā tēnei āhua i piro ai rātou.

Atu ki taua wā, i a Rangers te nuinga o te pōro i uaua ki a rātou te wāhi i te pae whakangungu o te haukāinga, ka mutu kāore noa i tino raruraru a Liam Kelly.

I ū haere tonu mai ngā whakawhiti ki te pāka o Livingston me te pare haere tonu atu, ā, kāore i arohia atu ngā tono whiu - whai muri i te rutu a Halkett ki te piki a Glenn Middleton, me tētahi mō te pā ringa o te pōro.

Alasdair Lamont a BBC Scotland i te Tony Macaroni Arena

Kua tino rerekē rawa atu te āhua o tā rātou purei me ngā kaitākaro mai i te hokinga atu ki te taumata o runga, engari mihi ka tika ki a Holt mō tana whakakotahi mai i te kapa mai ka tae atu ia.

Kua mate he kaieke pahikara i te tukinga me tētahi waka i Rānana.

Te whare herehere o Long Lartin: E ono ngā āpiha i whara i ngā tīrangorango
E ono ngā āpiha i whara i tētahi tutūtanga i tētahi whare herehere whakatiki tāne, te kī a Āpiha Whare Herehere.
I pakaru mai te raruraru i HMP Long Lartin i Worcestershire i te takiwā o te 09:30 BST i te Rātapu, ā, kei te haere tonu.
Kua heria mai ngā āpiha mātanga “Huripara” ki te whakatikatika i te raruraru, e waru ngā mauhere kei roto i tēnei kei roto i tētahi peka kotahi.

E Whakatuma Ana a Huripari Rosa i a Phoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake City Me Te Waipuke Ohorere (Ka Hua Pea Ko Ngā Wāhi Tauraki)
He tino rerekē te kite i tētahi pārua pārūrū i Arizona, engari te āhua nei ka pā mai tētahi ā te tīmatanga o te wiki e heke iho i te neke haerenga atu o te toenga o te kaha o Huripari Rosa ki te Koraha ki Puāwanga, e pā mai ai ngā waipuke ohorere.
Kua whakaputakētia e te Ratonga Huarere ā-Motu ngā whakatūpato waipuke ohorere mō te Mane me te Tūrei mō te uru o Arizona atu ki te tonga me te rāwhiti o Nevada, te paeroa o California me Utah, tae atu ki ngā tāonenui o Phoenix, Flagstaff, Las Vegas, me Salt Lake City.
Ko te tikanga ka haere torotika te ara o Rosa mā Phoenix hei te Tūrei, ka tata haere atu hei te pō o te Mane me te ua.
I kī te Ratonga Huarere ā-Motu o Phoenix i roto i tētahi tīhau “tekau anake ngā huripari pārūrū i mau tonu te tūranga āwhā pārūrū, pārua rānei i roto i te 200 maero o Phoenix mai i te tau 1950!
He huripari a Katrina (1967) i roto i te 40 maero o te paenga AZ.”
E matapae ana te tauira a te Pokapū Huripari ā-Motu e 2 ki te 4 īnihi te ua, me ngā rahinga tūhāhā atu ki te 6 īnihi i roto i te Mogollon Rim o Arizona.
Ko te tikanga ko ētahi atu wāhi o te Koraha ki Puāwanga ko te pū o Rockies me te Peihana Nui he 1 ki te 2 īnihi ki konei, me ngā rahinga tūhāhā ka taea atu ki te 4 īnihi
Mō ērā kei waho o te mōrea waipuke ohorere, tērā pea he mānawatanga pea ngā ua o Rosa i te mea kei te tauraki te roa.
Ahakoa he take tino taumaha te waipuke, he mea pai ētahi o ēnei ua i te mea kei te pā ngā āhuatanga tauraki ki te Puāwanga i tēnei wā.
E ai ki te U.S. Drought Monitor, neke atu i te 40 ōrau o Arizona kei raro i ngā āhuatanga tauraki nui, te wāhanga teitei rawa tuarua,” te kī a weather.com.
Tuatahi, e haere atu ana te ara o Huripari Rosa ki uta i Baja California i te kūrae o Mehiko.
E 385 maero a Rosa, kei te kaha huripari tonu i te ata o te Rātapu me ngā hau kaha o te 85 maero i te haora, i te taha tonga o Punta Eugenia, Mehiko me te haere whakateraki i te 12 maero i te haora.
Kei te pā te āwhā ki ngā wai mahana i Te Moananui-a-Kiwa, nō reira kei te kaha kē te heke.
Nā, ko te matapaetia ka tae ki Mehiko me te kaha āwhā pārūrū hei te ahiahi, pō rānei o te Mane.
Tērā pea he tino kaha te ua i ētahi wāhi o Mehiko, e mono mōrea ai ki te waipuke nui.
“Ko te matapae mai i te 3 ki te 6 īnihi ngā rahinga ua mai Baja California atu ki te māuru o Sonora, ā, atu ki te 10 pea ka taea,” te kī a weather.com.
Kātahi ka haere a Rosa i Mehiko hei āwhā pārūrū i mau i te tae atu ki te paenga o Arizon i ngā haora moata o te Tūrei hei pārua pārūrū, ā, kātahi ka ahu atu mā Arizona atu ki te tonga o Utah hei te pō o te Tūrei.
“Ko te mōrea nui e tūmanakohia ana mai i a Rosa, ana mahuetanga rānei ko te patapataiāwhā i Baja California, te māuru o Sonora me te Koraha ki Puāwanga o te U.S.,” te kī a te Pokapū Huripari ā-Motu.
Ko te tūmanako ko ngā waipuke ohorere me ngā rerenga para e matapaetia ana i ēnei he mōrea ki te ora tangata i ngā koraha, me ngā horo i ngā pae maunga.

E kī ana a Trump mō Kavanaugh ‘i whara ia i te weriweri me te riri’ o te Rōpū Democratic
“Ki te pōti mō Kaiwhakawā Kavanaugh kei te pōti ki te whakakāhore i ngā mahi aroha kore me te mōrihariha a te Rōpū Democratic,” te kī a Trump i tētahi huihuinga i Wheeling, West Virginia.

E hia rau tāngata i mate i te rū me te ngaru taitoko i Initonīhia, ā, e piki haere ana te kaute

Me huarua e te U.S. ngā pūtea A.I
I te nui haere ake o ngā mahi hinengaro hori a Haina, me huarua e te U.S. te rahinga e whakapaua ana e ia ki ngā rangahau i roto i taua wāhi, te kī a te kaihaumi me te tohunga AI a Kai-Fu Lee, i mahi ia mā Google, Microsoft me Apple i mua.
Ka puta ake ngā kōrero nei i muri i ngā whakapuakina a ngā wāhanga rerekē o te kāwanatanga o te U.S. mō te AI, ahakoa kāore he rautaki AI ōkawa a te U.S.
Ahakoa, i whakaurua e Haina tana mahere i tērā tau: ko tōna whāinga kia noho ia ki te tūranga 1 o te auahatanga AI i mua o te 2030.
“He tīmatanga pai te huarua i te tahua rangahau AI, ina kei muri rā anō ētahi atu o ngā whenua i te U.S., ā, kei te rapu mātou i te wāhitanga whai ake i roto i te AI,” te kī a Lee.
Mā te huarua i ngā pūtea ka huarua anō i ngā tūponotanga ka puta te whakatutukitanga AI nui whai ake i te US., te kī a Lee ki te CNBC i roto i tētahi uiui i tēnei wiki.
Ko Lee, he pukapuka tāna ko “AI Superpowers: China, Silicon Valley and the New World Order" i whakaputaina i tēnei marama e Houghton Mifflin Harcourt, te CEO o Sinovation Ventures, i haumi ki tētahi o ngā kamupene AI rongonui rawa i Haina, Face++.

I āhukahuka a Lee i ngā whakataetae hangarau kāwanatanga o te U.S. o mua pērā i te Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge, ā, i pātai ia āhea te mea whai ake, kia pai ai te āwhina ki te tohu i ngā matakite whai ake.
I te nuinga o te wā me kaha ake ngā mahi a ngā kairangahau o te U.S. kia riro mai ai ngā takuhe, te kī a Lee.
“Ehara i te mea kei te tangohia mai e Haina ngā pūkenga mātauranga mātāmua; ko ngā rangatōpū kē,” te kī a Lee.
I tuku mahi a Pukamata, Google me ētahi atu kamupene hangarau i ngā manutaki mai i ngā whare wānanga ki te mahi i te AI i ngā tau kua tata kua hipa.
I kī a Lee mā ngā rerekētanga ki ngā kaupapahere hekenga ka āwhina anō i te U.S. ki te whakapakari ake i ana mahi AI.
“Ki ahau nei me tuku noa ngā kāri kākāriki ki te hunga whai PhD i roto i te AI,” tana kī.

Ko tā te National Natural Science Foundation o Haina he tuku pūtea ki te hunga kei ngā whakanōhanga mātauranga e ōrite ana ki te āhua o te tuku pūtea a te National Science Foundation me ētahi atu whakahaere kāwanatanga ki ngā kairangahau o te U.S., engari he iti ake te kounga o ngā mahi mātauranga i Haina, te kī a Lee.

Kua pōti te iwi o Makerōnia i roto i tētahi tāpaetanga pōti mō te huri i te ingoa o te motu, kāore rānei
I pōti te iwi o Makerōnia i roto i tētahi tāpaetanga i te Rātapu mēnā me whakarerekē tō rātou ingoa ki te “Republic of North Macedonia,”mā tēnei ka tau te wenewene tūroa me Kirihi nā rātou i aukati i ngā tono mematanga ki te Uniana o Uropi me NATO.
E kī ana a Kirihi, kei a ia tētahi porowini e kīia ana ko Macedonia, e tohu ana te ingoa o tana kiritata ki te raki i tētahi kerēme ki tōna rohe, ā, nāna i aukati i tō rātou whakaurunga ki NATO me te EU.
I tatū he whakaaetanga i waenga i ngā kāwanatanga e rua e ai ki te ingoa hou e marohitia ana, engari e tohe ana ngā hoariri mana kotahitanga ka whakararua e te whakarerekētanga te tuakiri mātāwaka o te taupori matua Slavic o Makerōnia.

“I tae mai ahau i tēnei rā ki te pōti mō te anamata o te motu, mō te hunga rangatahi o Makerōnia kia noho wātea rātou i raro i te maru o te Uniana o Uropi ina he haumaru ake mō tātou katoa,” te kī a Olivera Georgijevska, 79, i Skopje.

Engari ko te hiahia o ngā kapa whakataetae a Scherzer ko te tākaro ki a Colorado Rockies, engari ia mēnā ka taea tonu te uru o ngā Rockies ki ngā whiringa whāiti, ā, kei mua rātou mā te tākaro kotahi ki a Los Angeles Dodgers i te NL West.
I riro i ngā Rockies tētahi tūranga tuarua i te iti rawa, i toa 5-2 ki ngā Nationals i te pō o te Paraire, engari kei te whai tonu rātou kia riro mai i a rātou te toa o te wāhanga mō te wā tuatahi.
“Ahakoa kāore he hua o te tākaro, ko te mea kē ka tākaro i roto i tētahi wairua rawe i konei i Denver nā te marea, ā, kei te tākaro tērā atu kapa ki tētahi taumata teitei rawa i pā ahau i tēnei tau.
He aha te take kāore ahau e hiahia ana ki te tākaro i roto i tērā?”
Kāore anō kia whakaputaina e ngā Nationals ko wai ka tīmata, engari ko te rongo kōrero ka tukuna ko Scherzer te kaiepa i taua āhuatanga.
Koinei te tīmata 34 mō Scherzer, ā, i te whakaharatau noa iho ana epa i te Tāite, ā, ka epa ia i tana rā whakatā noa i te Rātapu.
He 18-7 te kaiepa ringa matau o Washington me tētahi 2.53 ERA me ngā poi mīere 300 i roto i ngā pāeke 220 2/3 i tēnei tau.
Ka huihui atu a Trump ki West Virginia
I kōrero huna te Perehitini mō te āhuatanga e pā ana ki tana kōwhiri i a Brett Kavanaugh ki te Kōti Matua me te kōrero anō mō te hiranga o te haere ake o ngā Republican ki te pōti i ngā pōtitanga wā weherua.
“Kei te mōrea ā tātou mahi katoa ā te Whiringa-ā-rangi.
E rima ngā wiki mai i tētahi o ngā pōtitanga hira rawa i roto i ō tātou ao.
Koinei tētahi o ngā mea nui, nui -- kāore i te oma engari kei te omaoma haere kē ahau ki ngā wāhi katoa ki te whawhai mō ngā kaitono tino rawe,” tana kī.
Ka haere tonu a Trump, “Kei te kite koe i tēnei rōpū weriweri, wāwāhi tahā, ngā Democrats, e kitea ana e pā ana i tēnei wā.
Ka mutu kei te ngana rātou ki te muru i te mana ahakoa pēhea, ka kite koe i te weriweri me te maniheko.
Kāore he aha ki a rātou ko wai ka whara i a rātou, ka takahia e rātou kia riro mai i a rātou te mana me te rangatiratanga, koinā tō rātou hiahia ko te mana me te tino rangatiratanga, nō reira me ngana tātou.”
Kei te ngana ngā Democratics ki te “ātete me te ārai.”
“Nā, ka kite koe i ngā rā e whā kua huri,” tana kī, ko tana kōrero mō ngā Democrats he “riri, he weriweri me te maniheko me te take.”
He kōrero ia mō te Senate Judiciary Committee e whakaraupapa ana i te Democratic Sen. Dianne Feinstein mā tōna ingoa, ā, e whakatakēhia ia mai i te marea.
“Kei te maumahara ki tōna whakautu?
Nāu i tuku te tuhinga?
Ā, ā, he aha.
Kāo, ā, kāo, taihoa - kāore i pai te kōrero a te tinana - te kōrero ā-tinana weriweri katoa kua kite ahau.”
Kua kore a Labour i te rōpū whakaaro whānui.
Kāore i te rata ki te hunga kōrero i ō rātou whakaaro
I te pōtitanga o ngā kaiwhakaaraara o Momentum i roto i tōku ake rōpū kia wahangū ahau, kāore i ohorere.
Ina, ko au te tētahi o ngā MP o Labour i tēnei wā kia kīia kāore au i te hiahiatia - mō te whakaputa noa i ō mātou whakaaro.
I pērā anō te āhua ki taku hoa pāremata a Joan Ryan i te mea i tino whakahē ia i ngā mahi takahi i ngā Hūrae.
Mō te āhuatanga ki ahau, i whakahē te mōtini rauwene i ahau mō taku i whakahē i a Jeremy Corbyn.
Mō te hiranga o tētahi kaupapahere ōhanga takohanga, mō te haumarutanga ā-motu, mō Uropi, arā, he ōrite ngā take i whakahē ai a Jeremy ki ētahi atu rangatira o mua.
Ko te pānui mō te hui a Nottingham East Labour i te Paraire i kī “ko tō mātou hiahia kia tuwhera, kia whai hua ngā hui”.
Mō te nuinga o ōku tau e waru hei MP Labour mō te rohe, i tino pērā ngā hui GC i ngā pō o ngā Paraire.
Engari i tēnei rā, kua kore e pērā te wairua o ngā hui, ā, ko te oati o ngā tōrangapū “atawhai ake, ngāwari ake” kua warewaretia, mēnā rā i koinei i te tuatahi.
Mārama ana te kite ināianei kāore i te whakaaetia ngā whakaaro rerekē i roto i te pāti Labour, ā, ka whakawātia ia whakaaro mēnā e rata ana ki ngā kaiārahi o te rōpū.
I tīmata tēnei i muri tonu mai i te urunga o Jeremy hei kaiārahi, i te tūmanako ētahi o aku hoa i pōhēhē ahau i ōrite ō mātou whakaaro tōrangapū ka huria ōku whakaaro me te whai i ngā kaupapa kāore rawa ahau i tautoko - ahakoa mō te haumarutanga ā-motu, mō te mākete kotahi mō EU.
Ina kōrero ahau ki te marea - ka mutu kāore he aha he aha aku kōrero - ka whai mai ko ngā kupu tāwai i runga pāpāho pāpori mō te whakawātea mema, te whakahē, te whakahorihori i ngā tōrangapū o waenganui, e kī mai ana kia ahau kāore he wāhi mōku i roto i te rōpū Labour.
Ka mutu, ehara ko noa iho e pēneitia ana.
Arā, e mōhio ana ahau he waimarie ake ahau i ōku hoa i te mea ko ngā werowero i ahau e pā ana ki te tōrangapū.
Ka mīharo ahau ki te ngaiotanga me te manawanui o aua hoa e pēhia ana e ngā kupu whakaparahako ā-ira tangata, kaikiri hoki i ia rā engari kāore rātou e piko.
Ko tētahi o ngā āhuatanga tino pōuri o tēnei wā tōrangapū ko te kaha o te tūkinotanga kua whakaaetia.
I kī a Jeremy Corbyn i tērā wiki me hāpai e te rōpū Labour tētahi ahurea manawa nui.
Ko te āhua tūturu kua kore e whakaaetia e tātau ngā whakaaro whānui, ā, whai muri i ia mōtini “kore tautoko”, te huringa rānei o ngā ture tīpakonga ka whāiti haere ake te rōpū.
He nui ngā tohutohu i homai ki ahau i roto i ēnei tau e rua e āki ana i ahau kia tuohu tōku māhunga, kia kaua e kaha ki te kōrero, ā, ki te pērā “ka pai noa iho”.
Engari ehara koinā te take i uru mai ai ahau ki ngā mahi tōrangapū.
Mai rā anō i tuku urunga atu ki Labour i ngā tau 32 tau ki mua i te wā i te kura ahau, i whai i tēnei nā te kore i aro mai o te kāwanatanga o Thatcher ka pākarukaru haere tōku akomanga, ko tāku e whai ana he taunaki kia pai ake ngā ratonga tūmatanui mō te hunga e tino hiahia i ēnei - ahakoa hei kaikaunihera ā-takiwā, hei minita kāwanatanga rānei.
Kāore au i huna i aku tōrangapū, tae atu ki te pōtitanga whakamutunga.
Ko te tikanga kāore he tangata i Nottingham East i rangirua mō aku kaupapa kaupapahere me ngā wāhi i te taupatupatu ki ngā kaiārahi onāianei.
Ki te hunga nā rātou i hāpai i te mōtini i te Paraire, ko tāku noa i te wā e anga atu ana motu ki te Brexit ka whakamamae nei i ngā kāinga, pakihi me ā tātou ratonga tūmatanui, kāore au i te mōhio he aha te hiahia ki te moumou wā, kaha hoki mō tōku pono ki te kaiārahi o te rōpū Reipa.
Engari ko taku tino kōrero kē ehara ki a Nottingham Momentum, ki te iwi o taku rohe pōti kē, ahakoa he mema Labour, kāore rānei: Ka tū whakahī ahau ki te mahi mā koutou me taku kī taurangi ahakoa ngā kōrero whakatuma ki te whakawātea i ahau mai i te tū mō te rōpū, ngā āhuatanga tōrangapū rānei e kore au e whakarere i ngā mea e whakapono ana ahau he pai mō koutou katoa.

Ayr 38 - 17 Melrose: Kei te tūnga tuatahi a Ayr, ā, kāore anō i hinga
E rua ngā piro i mua o te mutunga i whakatītaha i ngā kaute whakamutunga, engari kāore he māharahara ka tika kia toa Ayr i roto i ngā takaro Tennent’s Premiership o te rā ngahau rawa atu.
Kei runga rātou i te papatoa i tēnei wā, ko rātou anake te kapa o te tekau kāore anō kia hinga.
I te mutunga, nā te kaha ake o tā rātou whakangungu, i te taha hoki o rātou ki te whakatutuki i ngā whai wāhitanga, e puta ai te kapa hau kāinga, ā, ka tika kia hari te kaiako a Peter Murchie.
“I whakamātauhia mātou i roto i ā mātou kēmu atu ki tēnei wā, ā, kāore anō kia hinga, nō reira me hari ahau,” tana kī.
I kī a Robyn Christie o Melrose: “Me mihi ki a Ayr, i pai ake tā rātou whakatutuki i ngā whai wāhitanga i a mātou.”
I puta a Ayr ki mua i te piro a Grant Anderson i te meneti 14, ka whiti te whana turuki a Frazier Climo, engari nā tētahi kāri kōwhai ki te kaitākaro o Kotirana a Rory Hughes, i tukuna e ngā Warriors mō tēnei kēmu, i whiwhi piro ai a Jason Baggot engari kāore i ū te whana turuki.
I nui ake ngā kaute a Ayr mā te whana whiu a Climo i mua tonu i te wā weherua, i whiwhi piro ia, ā, ka whiti i a ia te whana turuki o tētahi poro takitahi kia puta ai a Ayr ki te 17-5 i te wā weherua.
Engari i pai te tīmata a Melrose i te wāhanga tuarua me te piro a Patrick Anderson, i whiti i a Baggot te whana turuki, ka iti ake te wehenga ki te rima kaute.
I hikina te kēmu mō tētahi wā roa nā tētahi wharanga nui ki a Ruaridh Knott, i kawea atu, ā, mai i te tīmatanga, i kōkiri whakamua a Ayr mā tētahi piro ki a Stafford McDowall, i whiti i a Climo te whana turuki.
Ka whiwhi kāri kōwhai te kāpene rīwhi a Blair Macpherson, ā, ka whiwhi piro anō a Melrose, ā, kāore i whiti te whana turuki a Bruce Colvine, i muri i tētahi wāhanga e kaha te pēpēhi tētahi i tētahi.
I hoki mai te kapa hau kāinga, engari i te tukutanga o te kāri kōwhai ki a Struan Huchinson mō te rutu i a Climo me te kore pōro, mai i te āpititū whiu, i piro a MacPherson mai i muri o te mōro a Ayr.
I whiti te whana turuki a Climo, pērā anō i muri tonu i te tīmatanga o te wāhanga tuarua, i muri tonu i te hopu a Kyle Rowe i te whanau pouaka a David Armstong ka pāhi atu ki a Gregor Henry ka riro i a ia te piro tuarima mō te kapa hau kāinga.

Kua rite te whetū o Still Game a Ford Kieran ki te neke atu ki te ahumahi manaaki i muri tonu i te kitenga i runga tōna ingoa i tētahi kamupene whare hoko kai whai raihana.
E 56 ōna tau, ā, ko ia te kaiwhakaatu o Jack Jarvis i te whakaaturanga BBC hira, he kaituhi ngātahi, kaiwhakaatu ngātahi hoki te taha o tōna pātui pukuhohe pūmau a Greg Hemphill.
I whakapuakina e ngā tokorua ko te rārangi whakaaturanga e heke iho te mea whakamutunga o te whakaaturanga, ā, ko te āhua nei kei te whakarite a Kiernan mō tōna ao i muri i a Craiglang.
E ai ki ngā rārangi pūkete whaimana, ko ia te tumuaki o Adriftmorn Limited.
Kāore te kaiwhakaatu i hiahia ki te kōrero mō te karere, engari i kī tētahi tangata a te Scottish Sun i te hiahia a Kiernan ki te whakauru ki te “ahumahi whare hoko kai momoho.”
‘Nō tātou te maoana’: e manako ana te whenua tuawhenua a Poriwia ka huakina anō e te kōti he ara ki Te Moananui-a-Kiwa
E tūtei ana ngā hēramana i tētahi takuahi tauamana i La Paz.
Ka rere i ngā whare tūmatanui tētahi haki kahurangi.
Kua pania ngā pokapū tauamoana mai i te Roto o Titicaca ki te Amazon ki te pepeha: "The sea is ours by right.
To recover it is a duty."
Puta noa i te whenua tuawhenua o Poriwia, kei te mau tonu ki ngā mahara o te ākau i ngaro ki a Hiri i tētahi pakanga nui o te rau tau 19 - me te kōingo nui ki te whakatere anō i Te Moananui-a-Kiwa.
Ka nui rawa te tūmanako i tēnei wā, ina e tāria ana e Poriwia te whakatau a te kōti ā-ao ā te 1 o Whiringa-ā-nuku whai muri i te rima tau e whiriwhiria ana.
“Kei a Porowia te anga whakamua, he wairua whakakotahi, āio hoki, ā, e tūmanako ana i tētahi putanga pai,” te kī a Roberto Calzadilla, he takawaenga nō Poriwia.
He maha ngā tāngata o Poriwia ka mātaki i te whakatau a te ICH i runga mata nui puta noa i te motu, ko te tūmanako ka hinga te taraipiunara i te Hague ki te taha o te kerēme a Poriwia - whai muri i ngā kōrerorero pakari - e herea ana a Hiri ki te whakarite e āhei ai a Poriwia ki tētahi putanga ā-kāwanatanga ki te moana.
He nui ngā āhuatanga kei runga i te whakatau a te Mane mō Evo Morales, te perehitini tangata whenua - ka tukituki ia kia pōtihia anō ā tērā tau.
“Kua tata tonu te hoki ki Te Moananui-a-Kiwa,” tana kī i te mutunga o Hereturikōkā.
Engari e whakapono ana ētahi kaitātari kāore pea e whakaaetia e te kōti te hiahia o Porowia - ka mutu kāore pea e tino rerekē ake ngā āhuatanga mēnā ka whakaaetia.
Kāore he mana o te rōpū UN kei Hōrana ki te tuku i ngā whenua o Hiri, me te kī anō kāore e whakatauhia he putanga o ngā kōrerorero.
I te mea ka puta mai te whakatau a te ICJ i te ono marama anake i muri i te tāpaetanga o ngā tautohe whakamutunga e tohu ana tēnei kēhi “ehara i te mea uaua,” te kī a Paz Zárate, he mātanga ture ā-ao nō Hiri.
Ā, kāore pea i tautoko i te take a Poriwia, engari i raru pea nā ngā taua kua hipa.
“He mea haukoti te take o te āhei atu ki te moana e te kāwanatanga o Poriwia,” te kī a Zárate.
Kua ngaro te whakaaro pai o Hiri i ngā kōrero whakaaraara a Morales, tana whakapae.
He wā tōna ka kōrerorero haere a Poriwia me Hiri, engari he uaua te whakahaere i aua kōrero i muri i tēnei.
Kāore anō ngā whenua e rua kia tuku takawaenga kāwanatanga ki ō rāua anō whenua mai i te tau 1962.
I whakahēhia e te perehitini o mua a Eduardo Rodríguez Veltzé, te māngai o Poriwia ki te Hague, i te whakaaro he mea rerekē te hohoro o te whakatau a te kōti.
Ka puta ki a Poriwia ā te Mane “tētahi whai wāhitanga whakaharahara hei whakatuwhera i tētahi wā hou mō ngā whanaungatanga me Hiri” me tētahi whai wāhitanga ki te “whakamutu i ngā wenewene o ngā tau 139 mō ngā painga ngātahi tētahi ki tētahi,” tana kī.
I whakahē a Calzadilla i te whakamahia e Morales - tētahi o ngā perehitini e tino kaingākautia ana o Amerika Rātini - te take mō te moana hei kaupapa tōrangapū māna.
“E kore a Poriwia e tuku i tana mana āhei atu ki Te Moananui-a-Kiwa,” tana kī,
“He whai wāhitanga te whakatau hei whakaatu me waiho ngā rā o mua ki reira.”
E kī ana a Korea ki te Raki kāore e tukuna ana pahū karihi ki te kore ia e pono ki a US
I kī te Minita o Tāwāhi o Korea ki te Raki a Ri Yong Ho e kore tōna whenua e tuku i ana pahū karihi mēnā kāore ia i te pono ki a Washington.
I te kōrero a Ri i te Rāhoroi ki Te Whakaminenga Whānui o Te Kotahitanga o Ngā Whenua o Te Ao.
I tono ia ki te Hononga o Amerika kia tutuki i a ia ana oati i puta i tētahi hui taumata i Hingapoa i waenga i ngā rangatira o ngā whenua nei.
Ka puta ana kōrero i mua i te tīmata anō a te Hēkeretari o te Motu a Mike Pompeo i ngā kōrero takawaenga mō te pahū karihi mai i te toru marama i muri i te hui i Hingapoa me Kim Jong Un o Korea ki te Raki.
E kī ana a Ri he “wawata noa iho” ka hinga te Raki i ngā tāpare me te whakahē a te U.S. ki te whakapuakanga e whakamutu ana i te Pakanga o Korea.
Kei te māharahara a Washington ki te whakaae ki te whakapuakanga me te kore e tīmata a Pyongynga ki te tuku i ana pahū karihi.
Kei te hiahia a Kim me te Perehitini o te U.S. a Donald Trump i tētahi hui taumata tuarua.
Engari ko te whakaaro whānui kāore a Pyongayng i te pono mō te tuku i ana putunga pahū karihi e ai ki tērā iwi koinei ana te āhuatanga hei whakaū i tā rātou noho haumaru.
Kei te whakariterite a Pompeo ki te haere atu ki Pyongyang ā tērā marama mō tētahi hui taumata Kim-Trump tuarua.
E whakaatu ana ngā hoahoa kākahu ngā mea hou rawa mō ngā pōtae e haere ana ki tētahi Tiriti Matua tūtata ki a koe
Mēnā e hiahia ana koe ki te whakahou anō i ō pōtae, te ārai noa rānei te rā, kāore i tua atu i ēnei.
I huraina e ngā kaihoahoa a Valentino rāua ko Thom Browne i ngā pōtae nui rerekē mō tā rātou kohinga SS19 mō te ara hīkoi i whakamīharo i te huihuinga i te Wiki Hoahoa Kākahu o Parihi.
E tino pīrangitia ana ngā pōtae tino hakorea i tēnei raumati, ā, kua tukuna e ēnei kaihoahoa ā rātou mahinga whakamīharo ki te ara hīkoi.
Ko te mea tino i tino whererei a Valention ko te pōtae kiwi kōmā tino rerekē e whakarākeitia ana me tētahi pehe whānui rite ki te huruhuru i karapoti i ngā māhunga o ngā whakakite kahu.

I whakaatuna anō e Thom Browne tētahi tīpakonga rerekē o ngā ārai kanohi - i tae mai i mua i a Halloween.
He maha ngā ārahi kanohi karakara i tuituia ngā ngutu, ā, i rite rawa ki a Hannibal Lectre tēnā i tētahi pūweru rangatira.
Ko tētahi i hangaia mai i ngā kia ruku moana tae atu ki te ngongohā me ngā mōwhiti, ā, ko tētahi atu he rite ki tētahi koeke ahikirīmi i rewa.

E matapae ana ngā kaimātaki hoahoa kākahu tērā pea kei te haere atu ngā pānati ki ngā tiriti matua tūtata ki a koe.

Ko te pāhi rawhia karaka pakapaka, whai rawhia me tētahi kīwei kirikau mā, te tino taonga a te kohinga a Jacquemus' La Riviera SS19 i te Wiki Hoahoa Kākahu o Parihi.
