John Edward: He mea waiwai ngā pūkenga reo mō ngā kirirarau ā-ao
Kei te ū tonu ngā kura motuhake o Kotirana ki ngā taumata mātauranga tiketike, ā, i pērā anō i te 2018 me ngā otinga whakamātautau hirahira, e whakaūhia ano e ngā angitu takitahi, takitini hoki i roto i ngā hākinakina, toi, puoro, me ētahi atu umanga hapori.
Neke atu i te 30,000 ngā ākonga puta noa i Kotirana, e whakakanohitia ana ēnei kura e te Scottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS), he nanao atu kia taumata tiketike te whakarato ki ā rātou ākonga, mātua hoki.
E whai ana ngā kura motuhake ki te whakapakari i ā rātou ākonga ki te whai mātauranga atu anō, teitei ake hoki, ki te whai i tā rātou ara mahi me tō rātou wāhi hei kirirarau ā-ao.
Hei rāngai mātauranga e taea ana e te waihanga me te whakatinana tētahi marautanga kura hāngai, kei te mātou kei te whāia tonu ngā reo onāianei hei kaupapa hira, e hiahiatia ana i roto i ngā kura.
I kī a Nelson Mandela: “Mēnā ka kōrero koe ki tētahi tangata i roto reo e mārama ana ia, ka ū tērā ki tōna hinengaro.
Ki te kōrero koe ki a ia i roto i tōna ake reo, ka haere ū tērā ki tōna ngākau.”
He whakamaharatanga kaha tēnei kia kaua tātou e whirinaki ana ki te reo Ingarihi anake ina hiahia ana ki te tuitui taura here me te pono me te hunga nō whenua.
Mai i ngā otinga aromatawai o tēnei tau, kei te tātou kei runga rawa ngā reo i ngā tūtohi wāhanga me ngā auau hipa i roto i ngā kura motuhake.
E 68 ōrau o ngā ākonga i whai i ngā reo o iwi kē i whiwhi tētahi māka A Teitei ake.
Ko ngā raraunga, i kohia mai i ngā kura SCIS 74, i whakaatu e 72 ōrau o ngā ākonga i whiwhi i tētahi māka A Teitei ake mō reo Manarini, ā, he 72 ōrau o te hunga i te ako i te reo Tiamana, 69 o te hunga i te ako i te reo Wīwī me te 63 ōrau o te hunga i te ako i te reo Pāniora i whiwhi i te A.
E whakaatu ana tēnei kei te tautoko ngā kura motuhake i Kotirana i ngā reo o iwi kē hei pūkenga hira ka hiahiatia ana e ngā tamariki me ngā taiohi ā tōna wā.
Ko ngā reo onāianei, pērā i te kōwhiri kaupapa, he ōrite te mana ki ngā kaupapa STEM (pūtaiao, hangarau, pūkaha me te pāngarau) i roto i ngā marautanga kura motuhake me ētahi atu wāhi.
I kitea e tētahi rangahau a te UK Commission for Employment and Skills i te 2014 ko ngā pūtake a ngā kaituku mahi mō te whakakī i ngā tūranga wātea, 17 ōrau i kī nā te kuaretanga reo te kaupapa.
Nō reira kei te hira haere ake te whai i ngā pūkenga reo hei whakapakari i te hunga taiohi mō ā rātou ara mahi anamata.
Nā te nui haere ake o ngā whai wāhitanga mahi e hiahia ana i ngā reo, he mea waiwai ēnei pūkenga i te ao whānui.
Ahakoa te ara mahi ka kōwhiria e te tangata, mēnā i ako ia i tētahi reo tuarua, kei runga ake ia ā tōna wā nā te whai i tētahi pūkenga pūmau pērā i tēnei.
Nā te mōhio ki te whakawhitiwhiti kōrero me te hunga nō iwi kē kua whakaihuwaka te tangata whai reo kē ki mua i ētahi atu kaitono mahi.
E ai ki tētahi pōti a YouGov o ngā tāngata pakeke neke atu i te 4,000 i te UK i te tau 2013, 75 ōrau ō rātou kāore i matatau ki te kōrero i tētahi reo o iwi kē, ā, ko te reo Wīwī anake te reo i te mōhiotia i eke ki te ōrau mamati-rua, he 15 ōrau.
Koinei te take he hira te whakapau kaha ki te whakaako reo ināianei mō ngā tamariki o ēnei rā.
Mā te whai i ngā reo maha, otirā ngā reo o ngā ōhanga whanake, ka āhei ake ngā tamariki ki te rapu mahi whaitake.
I roto i Kotirana, he rerekē ngā reo e whakaakona ana e ia kura.
He maha ngā kura ka arotahi ki ngā reo hou tauhira ake, ā, ko ētahi ka whakaako i ngā reo e kī ana he hira ake mō te UK ina titiro atu ki te 2020, pērā i te Manarini, Hapanihi hoki.
Ahakoa te kaingākau o tō tamaiti, ka nui tonu ngā reo hei kōwhiri i roto i ngā kura motuhake, me ngā kaiako e mātau ana i roto i tēnei wāhanga.
E pūmau ana ngā kura motuhake o Kotirana ki te tuku i tētahi taiao ako e pakari ai ngā tamariki me te whai i ngā pūkenga e hiahiatia ana kia angitu ai rātou, ahakoa ngā āhuatanga o te ao anamata.
Kāore e taea te whakahē i tēnei wā, i roto i tētahi taiao pakihi ao whānui, ka noho hira tonu ngā reo ki te anamata o te reo, nō reira me whakaata tēnei i roto i te mātauranga.
Āe rā, ko te whakarite tika mō ngā reo onāianei ko “ngā pūkenga whakawhitiwhiti kōrero ā-ao”.
Ka tukuna tonu e ngā kura motuhake tēnei kōwhiringa, kanorautanga me te hiranga mō ngā taiohi o Kotirana.
Ka tika tonu.
Ko John Edward te Tumuaki o te Scottish Council of Independent Schools
Ka tākaro a LeBron i tana tākaro tuatahi mō Lakers ā te Rātapu i San Diego
Kua tata te mutu o te tatari a ngā kaitautoko e hiahia ana ki te kite i a LeBron e tākaro ana i tana tākaro tuatahi mō Los Angeles Lakers.
Kua puta te kōrero a te kaiako o ngā Lakers a Luke Walton ka tākaro a James i te kēmu whakamātautau tuatahi ā te Rātapu ki a Denver Nuggets i San Diego.
Engari kāore i te mōhiotia e hia ngā meneti ka tākaro ia.
“Ka nui atu i te kotahi, ā, ka iti iho i te 48,” te kōrero a Walton kei runga i te paetukutuku whaimana a te Lakers.
I puta te tīhau a te kairīpoata o ngā Lakers a Mike Trudell he iti noa ngā meneti ka tākaro a James.
Whai muri i te parakitihi i tēnei wiki, i uia a James mō ana whakaritenga mō te hōtaka o ngā kēmu whakamātautau e ono a ngā Lakers.
“Ehara i te mea me whai kēmu whakamātautau ahau i tēnei wāhanga o taku ara tākaro kia takatū ai ahau,” tana kī.
Te Wā Huihuinga i West Virginia a Trump, Hōngere YouTube
Ka tīmata ngā huihuinga whakahau a te Perehitini Trump i tēnei pō i Wheeling, West Virginia.
Koinei te tuatahi o ngā huihuinga e rima a Trump kua whakaritea i roto i te wiki, tae atu ki ngā wāhi whakahoahoa pērā i a Tennessee me Mississippi.
Kei te tārewa tonu te pōti mō tana kōwhiri ki te whakakī i te tūranga wātea o te Kōti Matua, kei te whai a Trump ki te whakaemi tautoko mō ana pōtitanga wā weherua e heke iho ina ko te mōrea ki ngā Republicans kei ngaro te mana whakahaere i te Congress ina tukuna ngā pōti ā te Whiringa-ā-rangi.
He aha te wā o te huihuinga a Trump i West Virginia i tēnei pō, ā, me pēhea te mātakitaki tuihono?
Kua whakaritea te huihuinga a Trump i Wheeling i West Virginia mō te 7 p.m. ET i tēnei pō, Rāhoroi, Mahuru 29, 2018.
Ka taea te huihuinga a Trump i West Virginia te mātaki tuihono mā te roma matawā i runga i a YouTube.
Ko te tikanga ka kōrero a Trump i te whakawātanga i tēnei wiki mō te kaikōhari ki te Komiti Matua a Brett Kavanaugh, e tohea nā ngā whakapae mahi whakaito, ā, e tārewa ana te pōti whakaū mō te Senate mō te wā atu ki te wiki i te wā e tūhuratia ana te take e te FBI.
Engari ko te whāinga matua o tēnei whakatū huihuinga maha nei ko te āwhina i ngā Republicans i mua i ngā pōtitanga o te Whiringa-ā-rangi kia whiwhi tautoko ai.
Nō reira, i kī te rōpū whakahau a Perehitini Trump ko ēnei huihuinga e rima i tēnei wiki ko te “whakaihiihi i ngā kaitūao me ngā kaitautoko i te wā ngana ana ngā Republicans ki te tiaki me te whakawhānui i tō rātou tokomaha i roto i te Senate me te House of Representatives,” e ai ki a Reuters.
“He mea nui rawa te mana whakahaere i a Congress mō tana kaupapa, ā, ka haere te Perehitini ki ngā wāhanga whenua maha rawa ka taea i a tātou e kuhu nei ki te wāhanga whakahau toritori rawa,” te kī a tētahi kaikōrero nō te rōpū whakahau o Trump ki a Reuters, ā, kāore ia i hiahia kia mōhiotia ia.
I whakaritea mō Wesbanco Arena i Wheeling, ka emi mai pea ngā tautoko ki te huihuinga ā te pō nei mai i “Ohio me Pennsylvania, ā, kia whāia mai e te hunga pāpāho o Pittsburg,” te kī a te West Virginia Metro News.
Hei te Rāhoroi te wā tuarua i tēnei marama kua tae a Trump ki West Virginia, te wāhanga whenua i toa mai i ngā piro neke atu i te 40 ōrau i te 2016.
Kei te ngana a Trump ki te āwhina i a te kaitono o te Republican Senate o West Virginia a Patrick Morrisey, kei muri ia i roto i ngā pōti.
“Ehara tēnei i te tohu pai mō Morrisey kua haere mai nei te perehitini ki te hāpai i ana pōti,” te kī a Simon Haeder, he mātanga tōrangapū i West Virginia University, e ai ki a Reuters.
Te Kapu Ryder 2018: He kaha te whawhai a te Kapa USA kia ora tonu ai rātou mō ngā tākaro takitahi ā te Rātapu
Whai muri i ngā wāhanga tākaro e toru i runga ake tētahi taha, ko ngā tokowhā o te ahiahi o te Rāhoroi te mea tika pea mō tēnei Kapu Ryder.
Taketake ake nō te ao hākinakina te āhuatanga o te huri o te tai e tino whakapono ana ngā kaitākaro, ā, kātahi tika rawa atu mō ngā whakataetae pērā i ēnei.
Nō reira kei hea te ia o te tai e haere ana i tēnei wā?
“E ono piro rātou i mua e haere ana, ā, e whā ināianei, nō reira kei muri pea te ia o te tai i mātou,” te kī a Jordan Spieth i tana wehenga atu mō te rā.
Kei mua a Uropi, āe rā, e whā ā rātou piro ki mua, ā, tekau mā rua atu anō hei tākaro.
Hei tā Spieth, kei te anga whakamua ngā Amerikana ka mutu kei te kite hua rātou i roto i a rātou, otirā i te āhua o te tākaro o Spieth rāua ko Justin Thomas i tākaro tahi mō te katoa o te rā, ā, e toru ā rāua piro mai i te whā.
Ka kino kē a Spieth mai i te tī ki te kākāriki, ā, ko ia te tino manutaki.
Kātahi ka tino kaha rawa atu ngā umere i a e haere ana, ka tika i a ia tētahi tīpao hira kia ōrite ai i te kēmu tuawhā, ina i muri rāua ko Thomas mā te rua.
Ko tana tīpao i toa ai i a rātou te kēmu i te 15 i pērā anō te kaha o te umere, i mōhio ai koe kei roto tonu te kapa o Amerika i tēnei whakataetae.
“Me tino ūpoko pakaru koe me te whakaaro noa iho mō tāu ake tākaro,” te kī a Spieth.
Koinei anake te mea kei ēnei tākaro e toe ana ināianei.
18 ngā kaupeka kia tū rangatira ai.
Ko ngā kaitākaro anake he nui ake ngā piro i a Spieth rāua ko Thomas i roto i ngā rā e rua nei ko Francesco Molinari rāua ko Tommy Fleetwood, te tino kōrero o te Kapu Ryder.
Ko te tokorua rerekē engari e arohatia ana o Uropi, kua whā ngā toa mai i te whā, ā, tē taea te hapa.
Ko “Moliwood” anake te tokorua kāore i whiwhi aketahi i te ahiahi o te Rāhoroi, engari i karo anō rāua i ngā aketahi i te ata o te Rāhoroi, te ahiahi o te Paraire me te iwa mutunga o te ata o te Paraire.
Nā taua tākaro, me te āhua o te rere o ō rāua kaha atu, mai hoki i tēnei marea manioro e whakaatu ana ko rāua ngā kaitākaro hei turaki a te Rātapu, ā, kāore he kaitākaro hira rawa hei toa i te whakataetae pea mō Uropi i te tōnga o te rā ki a Le Golf National i tua atu i a Fleetwood, Molinari rānei.
Ko te mea pai rawa ko rāua tahi ki ngā kaupeka rerekē.
Engari he moata rawa te kōrero mō te toa o Uropi.
Kāore i tino raru a Bubba Watson rāua ko Webb Simpson ki a Sergio Garcia, te toa pōrowhā o te ata, i te taha ia i a Alex Noren.
Nā tētahi aeha me ngā akerua e rua i te iwa o mua i uru te Pāniora me te Huirangi ki te raruraru kāore nei rāua i puta.
Engari ā te Rātapu, kāore he tangata hei āwhina i a koe i tō raru.
He tino mīharo te mātaki i ngā pōrowhā me ngā tokowhā ki te mātakitaki kia pātata tonu nā ngā whakawhitiwhiti i waenga i ngā tokorua, ngā tohutohu ka tukuna, kāore e tukuna hoki me te āhua o rerekē inamata o tētahi rautaki.
He pai ake te tākaro ā-kapa a Uropi atu ki tēnei, ā, kei mua rā anō rātou e haere ana i te rā whakamutunga engari i kitea i tēnei wāhanga tokowhā kei te kaha a USA ki te whawhai, ā, i te pōhēhē ētahi, otirā i Amerika, kāore i a rātou tērā.
Kei mua a Uropi 10-6 i te rā mutunga o te Kapu Ryder.
Kei mua rā anō a Uropi i te rā whakamutunga o te Kapu Ryder i muri i ngā kēmu pōrowhā me te tokowhā i te Rāhoroi, ā, he 10-6 tā rātou tatau ki Te Hononga o Amerika.
Nā te tokorua whakahihiri a Tommy Fleetwood rāua ko Francesco Molinari i ārahi mā ngā toa e rua ki a Tiger Woods kia eke ai ā rāua tatau ki te whā i tēnei wā i te Le Golf National.
I runga ake te kapa Uropi o Thomas Bjorn, e ngana nei ki te pupuri i te taonga i riro atu i ngā tau e rua ki mua i Hazeltine, i te kapa o Amerika i miere i te ata i te kēmu pōrowhā, ka toa 3-1.
I kaha ake te ātete a te U.S. i roto i ngā tokowhā, ā, e rua ngā kēmu i a toa rātou, engari kāore tonu i tata atu.
Me whiwhi te kapa o Jim Furyk i ngā piro e waru mai i ngā kēmu takitahi 12 a te Rātapu kia mau tonu i te taonga.
Ko Fleetwood te pūhou o Uropi tuatahi ki te toa i ngā piro whā piritata, ā, ko rāua tahi ko Molinari, i tapaia ko “Molliwood” whai muri i tētahi mutunga wiki whakaharahara, te tokorua tuarua ki te toa i ngā piro e whā mai i ā rātau kēmu e whā tuatahi i roto i te hītori o te Kapu Ryder.
I haukerekerehia e rāua a Woods rāua ko Patrick Reed i roto i ngā pōrowhā i rawe tā rāua mahi tahi ki te haukerekere i a Woods me te pūhou o Amerika a Bryson Dechambeau mā te 5&4.
I uaua ngā tākaro e rua a Woods i te Rāhoroi, ā, i kitea ētahi mahi whakamīharo āna engari kua 19 mai i ngā kēmu 29 kua hinga ia i roto i ngā pōrowhā me ngā tokowhā, ā, e whitu piritata.
I hoki mai a Justin Rose, i whakatā ia mō ngā pōrowhā o te ata, ki te taha o Henrik Stenson i roto i ngā tokowhā ki te hinga i a Dustin Johnson rāua ko Brooks Koepka 2&1 - kei te tūranga kotahi me toru rāua i te ao.
Engari kāore i rere pai i te katoa o te wā mō Uropi i tētahi rā paki, hau angiangi i te puāwanga o Parihi.
I whakatakotohia e te Jordan Spieth, e toru ana toa, me Justin Thomas te pae taumata mō ngā Amerikana me ngā piro e rua i te Rāhoroi.
I riro toa i a rāua tētahi kēmu uaua 2&1 ki a Jon Rahm o Pāniora me Ian Poulter i roto i ngā pōrowhā, ā, i hoki mai ia ki te turaki i a Poulter rāua ko Rory McIlroy 4&3 i roto i ngā tokowhā whai muri i tana hinganga i ngā kaupeka e rua tuatahi.
E rua anake ngā wā i roto i te hītori o te Kapu Ryder kua hoki mai he kapa mai i ngā piro e whā ki muri i roto i ngā kēmu takitahi, ahakoa me ōrite noa te kapa o Furyk kia mau tonu i a rātou te taonga.
Engari, whai muri i te noho tuarua mō ngā rā e rua, te āhua nei he uaua rawa pea mō rātou te hoki mai anō a te Rātapu.
Ka kī a Korea ki te Raki e ‘kore rawa’ e tuku i a rātou pahū karihi ki te rātou he pono
I kī atu te minita take tāwāhi o Korea ki te Raki ki Te Kotahitanga o Ngā Whenua o te Ao i te hōhonu kē atu te kore pono ki Te Hononga o Amerika nā ngā tārepa, ā, e kore tērā whenua e tuku i ana pahū karihi i raro i aua āhuatanga.
I kī atu a Ri Yong Ho ki Te Whakaminenga Whānui o te UN he “nui ngā whakaritenga whakaaro pai” kua oti i a Korea ki te Raki i te tau kua hipa, pērā i te whakamutu i ngā whakamātautau pahū karihi, pahūtuku hoki me te kī taurangi kia kaua e whakaemi pahū karihi me ngā hangarau karihi.
“Engari, kāore mātou i te kite i te urupare ōrite mai i te U.S.,” tana kī.
“Ki te kore e pono ki te U.S. kāore he tautoko i tō mātou whakamarutanga ā-motu, ā, i raro i aua āhuatanga e kore rawa mātou e tuku tuatahi i ā mātou pahū karihi.”
Ahakoa i tuaruahia e Ri aua amuamu anō a Korea ki te Raki mō te ātete a Washington ki tētahi ara ka “āta whakaurua mai” mō te whakawātea i ngā pahū karihi e utua ai Korea ki te Raki i a ia ka whai i taua ara, te āhua nei he hira tāna tauākī i te mea kāore i whakahētia tā rātou whakakorenga o ngā pahū karih pērā i te kī a Pyongyang i mua.
I kōrero a Ri mō tētahi tauākī ngātahi i tukuna e Kim Jong Un rāua ko Donald Trump i te hui taumata tuatahi i waenga i tētahi Peretini o te U.S. me tētahi rangatira o Korea ki te Raki i Hingapoa i te Pipiri 12, i te kī oati a Kim ka whai ia i te ara ki te “whakakore i ngā pahū karihi o te kūrae o Korea” me te kī taurangi a Trump ka whakapūmautia e ia te whakamarutanga o Korea ki te Raki.
E rapu ana a Korea ki te Raki i tētahi whakamutunga ōkawa ki te Pakanga o Korea 1950-53, engari ko te kī a te Hononga o Amerika me mātua tuku rātou i ā rātou pahū karihi i te tuatahi.
I whakahē anō a Washington i ngā tono ki te whakamāmā i ngā tārepa ā-ao kei runga i a Korea ki te Raki.
“Kei te ū tonu te U.S. ki te “whakakorenga o ngā pahū karihi” i te tuatahi me te whakapiki i te kaha o ngā pēhitanga kia eke ai tā rātou kaupapa mā tētahi āhuatanga ringa ū, me te whakahē hoki ki te “whakapuakanga o te mutunga o te pakanga,”” te kī a Ri.
“Ko te whakaaro ka tuohu mātou i ngā tarepa hē pōhēhē tērā nō te hunga kuare ki a mātou.
Engari ko te raruraru kē kei te hōhonu kē atu tō mātou hotohoto nā ngā tāpare pūmau.”
Kāore a Ri i kōrero mō ngā whakaritenga mō tētahi hui taumata tuarua i waenga i a Kim rāua ko Trump i kōrerohia e te rangatira o te U.S. i Te Kotahitanga o Ngā Whenua o Te Ao i tēnei wiki.
I kōrero kē te minita mō ngā hui e toru i waenga i a Kim me te rangatira o Korea ki te Tonga a Moon Jae-in i ngā marama e rima kua hipa me te kī anō: “Mēnā ko te rōpū i roto i tēnei take o te whakakorenga o ngā pahū karihi o Korea ki te Tonga, ā, kaua ko te U.S., e kore rawa e kōmutu pēnei te whakakorenga o te kūrae o Korea.”
Ahakoa tērā, he tino rerekē te wairua o te kōrero a Ri ki tērā tau, i tana kī atu ki te Whakaminenga Whānui o te U.N. kāore e kore ka whakatika atu ngā tākirirangi a Korea ki te Tonga ki te whenua o te U.S whai muri i te kī a "Mr Evil President" Trump he “tangata tākirirangi” a Kim kei te whai ki te whakamate i a ia anō.
I tēnei tau i Te Kotahitanga o Ngā Whenua o te Ao, he nui ngā kōrero a Trump, i whakatuma ki te “tino whakakore atu” i a Korea ki te Raki i tērā tau, e mihi ana ki a Kim mō tōna māia ki te whai i te ara ki te whakakore i ngā pahū karihi, engari i kī he nui tonu ngā mahi hei mahi ā, me noho tonu ngā tāpare kia kore atu ngā pahū karihi a Korea ki te Raki.
I te Wenerei, i kī a Trump kāore he wātaka āna mō tēnei, “Mēnā e rua tau, toru tau, rima marama rānei - kāore he aha.”
Ko te tohe a Haina rāua ko Rūhia me utu te Kaunihera Whakamaru o te U.N. i a Pyongyang mō ngā mahi kua oti i a rātou.
Engari, i kī atu te U.S. Secretary of State a Mike Pompeo ki te Kaunihera Whakamaru o te U.N. i te Tāite: “Me haere tonu ngā whakaūnga o ngā tāpare a te Kaunihera Whakamaru, ā, kia kaua e miere kia kite rā anō tātou i te whakakorenga tūturu, whakamutunga, whakaūnga hoki o te whakakorenga o ngā pahū karihi.”
I whānui te whakaae a te Kaunihera Whakamaru kia whakapikihia ngā tāpare ki a Korea ki te Raki mai i te tau 2006 hei kōtē atu i ngā pūtea mō ngā kaupapa pahū me te pahūtuku karihi a Pyongyang.
I tūtaki a Pompeo ki a Ri i te rāhaki o ngā hui a te Whakaminenga Whānui a te U.N me te kī i muri mai ka haere anō ia ki Pyongyang ā tērā marama ki te whakarite i mō te hui taumata tuarua.
E toru ngā haerenga atu o Pompeo ki Korea ki te Raki i tēnei tau tonu, engari kāore i tutuki pai tana haerenga whakamutunga.
I te wehenga mai i Pyongyang i te Hōngongoi i kī ia kei te anga whakamua, engari i ētahi haora i muri mai i whakahētia ia e Korea ki te Raki mō ana “tono whakawetiweti.”
I kī oati a Korea ki te Raki i tētahi hui me Moon i tēnei marama ka turakina tētahi wāhi pahūtuku me tētahi whare karihi menā ka whai anō te Hononga o Amerika i ēnei “whakaritenga ōrite.”
I kī ia i kī atu a Kim ki a ia ko “ngā whakaritenga ōrite” e rapu ana ia ko ngā whakapūmau whakamaru mai i kī oati a Trump i Hingapoa me te neke haere ki te whakaū i ngā whanaungatanga me Washington.
Kei te whai ngā ākonga o Havard i tētahi akoranga mō te nui o te whiwhi whakatā
I tētahi akoranga hou i Te Whare Wānanga o Harvard i tēnei tau kua tahuri ngā ākonga paetahi katoa kia nui ake te moe hei kaupare atu i te ahurea whakamārōrō e tipu ana i roto i te whai mātauranga mā te inu kawhe ‘kia mahi ai i te pō roa.’
I kitea e tētahi tangata mātauranga i te whare wānanga matua o te ao kāore noa iho ngā ākonga i te mōhio ki ngā mea tino waiwai mō te tiaki i a rātou anō.
I hangaia te akoranga e Charles Czeisler, ahorangi o ngā rongoā moe i te Harvard Medical School, ā, e whakapono ana ia koinei te mea tuatahi pēnei i te U.S.
I uru mai te whakaaro ki a ia kia tīmataria te akoranga i muri i te tuku kōrero mō te pānga o te iti rawa o te moe ki te ako.
‘I te mutunga i haere mai tētahi kōtiro ki ahau ka kī mai: ‘He aha te take kātahi anō ahau ka mōhio mō tēnei, i taku tau whakamutunga?’
I kī ia kāore he tangata i kōrero atu ki a ia mō te hiranga o te moe - i ohorere ahau i tēnei,’ i kī ia ki The Telegraph.
Ko tēnei akoranga, i whakahaerehia mō te wā tuatahi i tēnei tau, he whakamārama ki ngā ākonga mō ngā mea waiwai mō te āwhina a ngā ritenga moe pai i ngā mahinga mātauranga me te hākinakina, me te whakapai ake i tō rātou oranga whānui.
I kī a Paul Barreira, te ahorangi mate hinengaro o Harvard Medical School me te tumuaki whakahaere o ngā ratonga hauora o te whare wānanga, i whakatau te whare wānanga ki te whakauru mai i te akoranga i te kitenga he tino iti rawa te moe a ngā ākonga i te wiki.
Kei roto i ngā akoranga kotahi haora ko ngā mahinga pāhekoheko.
I tētahi wāhanga he atahanga kei reira o tētahi rūma moe, e pāwhiri ai ngā ākonga i ngā kapu kawhe, ārai, hū hākinakina me ngā pukapuka ka kīia mai mō ngā pānga o te kawhe me te awatea, ā, he pēhea te pānga o te mahinga hākinakina nā te iti rawa o te moe, me te hiranga o tētahi ritenga wā moe.
I tētahi atu wāhanga, ka kōrerohia atu ngā kaiwhakauru he pēhea te pānga o te iti o te moe ki ngā hē manawa, ikura roro, pāpouri me te mate pukupuku.
Ko te mahere o te whare wānanga, me ngā ata pāhekoheko, ka whakatenatena i ngā kaiwhakauru kia whakaaroaro mō ā rātou ritenga o ia rā.
‘E mōhio ana mātou kāore e rerekē ngā whanonga o ngā ākonga i tēnei wā tonu.
Engari e whakapono ana mātou me āhei rātou ki te mōhio - pērā anō i tō tāua āhei ki te mōhio mō ngā pānga hauora o te kai paipa,’ te kī a Ahorangi Czeisler.
I kī ia ko te ahurea o te whakamanamana i mahi i te pō roa’ kei te mau tonu, me te aha kua hē kē atu i ngā hangarau hou me ngā taumahatanga nui ake te raruraru o te iti o te moe a ngā ākonga.
Ko te whakarite kei te nui te moe, ā, he kounga hoki, te ‘te mea whaitake’ a te ākonga ki te pēhi atu i ngā taumahatanga, rūhātanga me te auhi, tana kī - me te ārai i te mōmona haere, ina ki te iti rawa te moe uru te hiakai ki te roro, ā, e noho haere tonu ai te tangata.
I āwhina a Raymond So, 19 ōna tau nō Karepōnia e ako ana i te mātauranga matū me te koiora tinana, i āwhina i a Ahorangi Czeisler ki te waihanga i te akoranga, ā, i whai ia i tētahi o ngā akoranga i tērā tau i tana tau tuatahi i Havard.
I kī ia i tuwhera ōna karu me te whakahihiri i a ia ki te puta whānui tēnei akoranga ki te takiwā katoa o te wānanga.
E manako ana ia, ko te mahi whai ake ko te tono ki ngā ākonga paerua katoa kia whai i tētahi akoranga ōrite i mua i te uru ki te whare wānanga nei.
Ko te whakahau a Ahorangi Czeisler kia whakaritea e ngā ākonga he pūoho mō te hoki ki te moe me te oho hoki, ā, kia tūpato ki ngā pānga kino o te ‘rama kikorangi’ ka puta i ngā mata hiko me ngā rama LED, ka whakararu i te karaka o tō tinana, e uaua ai te parangia e te moe.

I tau mai anō te pōuritanga ki a Rangers i wāhi kē i te hinganga 1-0 o te kapa o Steven Gerrard nā te piro a Dolly Menga i Livingston.

I piro a Menga i te whitu meneti i mua i te wā weherua, ā, kore i pātata te kapa o Rangers ki te whiwhi piro.
Ahakoa ka taka a Rangers ki te tūranga tuaono, ka piki a Livingston ki te tuatoru, ā, kei muri noa iho i a Hibernian rerekētanga piro.
Kei reira anō pea ētahi atu raruraru mō Rangers i muri i te wharanga o te māhunga o te kairota a Calum Spence i whiutanga o tētahi taputapu ki a ia mai i te taha o ngā manuhiri.

Engari i mau tonu a Holt ki tana kapa tīmata nā rātou i tango i tētahi piro mai i a Hearts i tērā wiki, ka mutu kei te hari pea ia i tana āhua o te poke a tōna kapa tino koi i tō rātou hoariri.
Ahakoa i a Rangers te nuinga o te pōro engari i whaikiko ake te whakamahi a Livingstone i te pōro i te wā i a rātou.
Ko te tikanga i piro rātou i te meneti rua meneti i te pānga tuatahi o Menga kia puta a Scott Pittman ki te pou piro o Allan McGregor's engari i kotiti kē atu ki te pōro ki te taha.

I kaha mai anō a Rangers engari i te wawata noa iho rātou kāore i ū te pono mō te āhua o tā rātou purei i te rauna tuatoru.
I tino whakapono a Alfredo Morelos me tuku he whiu māna i te rua mā rima meneti i tō rāua tukinga ko Steven Lawless engari kāore i aro atu te kaiwawao a Steven Thomson ki ngā pīra a te tangata o Koromopia.
E rua noa iho ngā whana hāngai i te wāhanga tuatahi engari kāore i uaua ki te tautopenga a Liam Kelly te pare atu i te tukirae a Lassana Coulibaly me te whana koretake a Ovie Ejaria.

I uaua anō ki a Rangers te pupuri i ngā tākaro whakarite a Jacobs.

Engari i nuka tonu a Livingston i ngā manuhiri ki te tākaro i te momo kēmu e pai ana ki a rātou, me te haukoti a Lithgow rāua ko Halkett i ia whana pōro roa.
I te tata te piro anō a te kapa o Holt i ngā wāhanga whakamutunga engari i pakari a McGregor ki te aukati atu i a Jacobs i mua i te kotiti atu o te tukirae a Lithgow mai i te kokonga.

Almanac: Te kaiwaihanga i te Geiger Counter
Nā, he whārangi mai i tā mātou "Sunday Morning" Almanac: Mahuru 30, 1882, 136 ki mua i tēnei rā, ā, HAERE TONU... te rā i whānau mai ai te kaiahupūngao a Johannes Wilhelm "Hans" Geiger i Tiamana.
I hangaia e Geiger tētahi tikanga mō te kimi me te ine i te iraruke, ka hangaia he taonga mai i tēnei e mōhiotia ana ko te Geiger Counter.
He poupou nō te pūtaiao mai i taua wā, he poupou anō te Geiger Counter nō te ahurea puoro, arā nō te whitiāhua o te 1950 “Bells of Coronado,” ko ngā kaiwhakaatu mātanga pūtaiao kaupoai a Roy Rogers rāua ko Dale Evans:
Tangata: “He aha tērā?”
Rogers: “He Geiger Counter, whakamahia ai ki te kimi i ngā ōpapa iraruke, pērā i te konukarihi.
Ina whakamaua e koe ēnei kaweoro, ka rongo koe i ngā pānga o ngā rāpoi ngota e puta ana i te iraruke i roto i ngā ōpapa”
Evans: "Kei te tino pahū kē!"
I mate a “Hans” Geiger i te tau 1945, i mua paku tonu i tana huritau 63.
Engari kei te ora tonu te tenenga i mau nei i tōna ingoa.
Ka taea e te kano ārai mate pukupuku hou tātau te pūnaha ārai mate te ako ki te ‘kite’ i ngā pūtau nauhea.
Ka taea e te kano ārai mate pukupuku te pūnaha ārai mate te ako ki te ‘kite’ i ngā pūtau nauhea me te patu atu
Ka ako te ārai mate kano i te pūnaha ārai mate kia mōhio ki ngā pūtau nauhea i roto i te whakamaimoatanga
Kei roto i tēnei ko te tango i ngā pūtau ārai mate mai i tētahi tūroro, e rawekehia ana i roto i tētahi taiwhanga
Kātahi ka ‘kitea’ pūmua noa ki ngā mate pukupuku maha, ā, ka weroa atu anō
Kei te puta he hua i tētahi kano ārai mate whakamātautau ki ngā tūroro me ngā tūmomo mate pukupuku.
I kite tētahi wahine i whakamaimoatia ki te kano ārai mate, e ako ana i te pūnaha ārai mate kia mōhio ki ngā pūtau nauhea, i te koretanga o tana mate pukupuku wharekano mō ngā marama neke atu i te 18.
Kei roto i tēnei tikanga ko te tango i ngā pūtau ārai mate mai i te tūroro, ka rāwekeweke i roto i te taiwhanga kia ‘kite’ ai i tētahi pūmua noa ki ngā mate pukupuku maha e kīia ana ko HER2, ā, ka wero anō i ngā pūtau.
I kī te Ahorangi a Jay Berzofsky, o te US National Cancer Institute i Bethesda, Maryland: “E kī ana ā mātou otinga he kano ārai mate tino whai kiko tonu.”
Ko tā te HER2 he “kōkiri i te tipuranga o ngā momo mate pukupuku maha,” tae atu ki ngā mate pukupuku ki te ū, wharekano, pūkahukahu, kōpiro hoki, te whakamārama a Ahorangi Berzofsky.
I momoho anō tētahi atu ara ōrite o te tango i ngā pūtau ārai mate mai i ngā tūroro me te “ako” me pēhea te whai i ngā pūtau mate pukupuku i roto i te whakamaimoa i tētahi momo mate totomā.

Kāore i Pai

Nā, mēnā i te māharahara ahau mō te kaikiri kua wehe noa atu ahau i Amerika,” tana kī.

I whakawetihia ahau e rātou!

Kei te whakahē te kaiwhakaatu rongonui o Game of Thrones a Kit Harington ki ngā tautānetanga kino

HIV/Aids: Ko te pūrongo a Haina 14% te pikitanga o ngā kēhi hou
Kua puta i a Haina te kōrero 14% te pikitanga o te maha o ana kirirarau e pāngia e te HIV me te Aids.
Neke atu i te 820,000 e pāngia ana i roto i te whenua, te kī a ngā āpiha hauora.
Tata ki te 40,000 ngā kēhi hou i pūrongohia i te hauwhā tuarua i te 2018 anake.
Ko te nuinga o ngā kēhi hou i whakawhitia mā te ai, he rerekētanga tēnei mai mua.
Mai i rā anō i mua, i tere te hōrapa o te HIV i ētahi wāhanga o Haina nā nga huaranga toto i whakapokea.
Engari kua iti haere ake te hunga i whiwhi i te HIV mā tēnei āhuatanga, ā, kua tata ki te kore, te kī a ngā āpiha hauora Hainamana i tētahi hui i te porowini o Yunnan.
Engari, i ia tau, kua piki te rahinga o te hunga e pāngia ana e te HIV me te Aids i Haina mā te 100,000 tāngata.
He raru nui te whakawhitinga o te HIV mā te ai i roto i te hapori LGBT i Haina.
I whakakorehia ngā whiu taihara mō te takatāpui i Haina i te 1997, engari kei te kaha tonu te aukatitanga o te hunga LGBT.
Nā ngā uara tuku iho o te motu, e ai ki ngā rangahau tata ki te 70-90% o ngā tāne e ai ana i te tāne ka mārena i te wāhine.
He maha ngā whakawhitinga o ngā tahumaero i ahu mai i ngā whakamaru ai koretake i roto i ēnei whanaungatanga.
Mai i te tau 2003, i oati te kāwanatanga o Haina kia whānui te āhei atu ki ngā rongoā HIV i roto i tētahi kaupapa ki te whakarite i te raru.

I whakahorihori te U.S. Rep. a Maxine Waters i te Rāhoroi i ngā whakapae nā tētahi o ana kaimahi i pōhi ngā mōhiohio whaiaro o ngā kaihanga ture Repulican U.S. e toru ki ngā whārangi Wikipedia mō ngā kaihanga ture.

I puta tuihono ēnei mōhiohio i te Tāite, he mea pōhi e tētahi tangata tē mōhiotia i runga o Capitol Hill i te wā o tētahi whakawātanga a te rōpū Senate mō ngā whakapae taitōkai ki te kaikōhari ki te Kōti Matua a Brett Kavanaugh.
I puta te tukunga kōrero i muri i te uiui a ngā kaihanga ture e toru i a Kavanaugh.
Ko ngā pae kōroke pērā i a Gateway Pundit me RedState i kī ko te wāhitau KI e tautuhi ana i te puna o ngā pōhi e pā hono ana ki te tari o Watters” me te tuku i ngā mōhiohio o tētahi kaimahi a Waters, te pūrongo a te Hill.
“He tino teka tēnei whakapae poka noa, he rūkahu,” te kōrero a Waters.
“Kāore rawa atu taku kaimahi - i whakaaturia tōna tuakiri, ngā mōhiohio whaiaro, me te noho raru o tōna haumaru nā ēnei whakapae tinihanga, teka hoki - i tuku i ēnei mōhiohio.
He tino teka tēnei whakapae poka noa, ka mutu he rūkahu.”
I tere te whakahē i te tauākī a Waters i runga ipurangi, ā, tae atu ki te hekeretari pāpāho o mua o te White House a Ari Fleischer.
“He riri kei roto i tēnei whakakāhoretanga,” i tuhia e Fleischer.
“E tohu ana tēnei kāore i a ia te momo āhua tika hei Mema Uepū.
Mēnā ka whakapaetia te tangata mō tētahi mahi rā nāna i mahi, kaua rawa ia e riri.
Kaua rawa ia e whāuraura.
Kaua rawa ia e werowero i te kaupapa a te kaiwhakapae.
Me mauri tau, me āio.
I puta a Fleischer ki te whakataurite i te urupare a Walters ki ngā whakahē a ngā Democrats i a Kaiwhakawā Kavanaugh, i whakapaetia ia e ētahi te hunga whakahē i a ia i te kaha rawa riri i ngā whakawātanga o te Tāite.
I puta anō ngā whakaaro o Omar Navarro i runga Tīhau, he kaitono Repuplican ia e whakamātau ana ki te turaki i a Waters i roto i ngā pōtitanga wā weherua.
“He nui mēnā kei te tika,” tana tīhau.
I roto i tana tauākī, i kī a Waters i whakamōhiotia atu tana tari ki “ngā mana tōtika me ngā mana whakaū i te ture mō ēnei whakapae tinihanga.
“Ka mātua whakarite mātou ka kitea te hunga hara, ā, ka riro mā te ture rātou e aki mō ā rātou mahi kino, whakaraerae hoki ki aku kaimahi katoa.”
He aro take i a Johnny English Strikes Again - te tāwhai hangarau pūrahorua a Rowan Atkinson
Kua tikanga ināianei te rapu i ngā tohu mō Brexit i roto i ngā kiriata hōu me ngā kōrero mō Piritana, ka mutu e hāngai ana ki tēnei whakaoranga o te whai raihana toha o te pukuhohe hohenga a Johnny English - i tīmata mai i te tau 2003 me Johnny English ka hoki mai anō i te 2011 me Johnny English Reborn.
Ko te pūhohe whaiaro e whakatakē ana i tō tātou koretake te whai wāhitanga hoko ki tai hōu o te motu?
Heoi, kua whakahōutia te raihana o te kanohi ruru, hangenge a Johnny English ki te taka ki te hē mō te wā tuarua - e tohu ana tōna ingoa he pukuhohe whānui i hangaia mō ngā whenua mātakitaki pikitia kāore e kōrero Pākehā.
Ko ia hoki te pūrahorua muna māhunga wai ahakoa tana ngana kia koi ia he āhua rite ia ki a Clouseau, me Mr Bean me taua tangata i whakatautau i te rangi kotahi o Chariots of Fire i te whakatuwheratanga o te Orimipia 2012 i Rānana.
I takea mai hoki ia i te tangata haere me te tangata ā-ao muna i whakatautauhia e Atkinson i mua i roto i ngā pānui hokohoko a Barclaycard, he raruraru katoa i mahue mai i a ia.
Kei reira ētahi wā hira ruarua nei i roto i te whakaaturanga JE hou.
Ka rawe ki ahau te whakatata haere o Johnny English ki te waka topatopa me te mau i ngā kākahu pukupuku o nehe me te paopao o ngā maitai topatopa ki tōna pōtae mārō mō te wā poto.
Ka kitea ngā pūmanawa o Atkinson ki te whakaari i te pukuhohe, engari āhua koretake me te pāpaku te āhua whakakata, ina kua kaha ngā momo kiriata “pono” pērā i a 007 me Mission Impossible ki te whakauru mai i te pukuhohe.
Te āhua nei kei te hāngai te pukuhohe ki ngā tamariki kaua ki ngā pākeke, ā, mōku ake kua kore e auaha, e tōtika ngā haerēre tino rerekē a English pērā i ngā kiriata ngū a Atkinson i roto i te kiripuaki a Bean.
Ko te kaupapa o te wā ināianei kei te tino raruraru a Piritana Nui.
Kua uru poka noa tētahi mūrere-tāurungi ki te kōtuinga pūrahorua tino matatapu o Piritana, e whakaatu ana i ngā ko wai ngā pūrahorua katoa o Piritana kei te mahi, ā, kua ohorere katoa te āpiha kei te mahi - he wāhanga iti mō Kevin Eldon.
Koinei te raruraru whakamutunga mō tētahi pirimia whakahīhī, taukumekume, kei te kaha te whakahē i a ia e te ao tōrangapū: He tino kaha a Emma Thompson ki te whakataurite i a ia ki tētahi kiripuaki e rite nei ki a Teresa-May engari he iti rawa te matū i roto i te tuhituhinga hei whai māna.
Ko te kōrero a ana kaitohutohu ki a ia kua noho mōrea ia pūrahorua ia, ā, me whakahoki mai tētahi mai i te ahungarua.
Arā, ko te whakahoki mai i a Johnny English, he tumuaki ia ināianei i tētahi kura whakahirahira, engari kei te ako i ētahi kaupapa kei waho i te marautanga me pēhea te mahi hei pūrahorua: kei konei ētahi wāhi whakakatakata, i a English e tuku ana i tētahi momo wānanga pūrarohorua e rite ana ki te School of Rock.
Ka tonoa a English kia hoki ki Whitehall mō tētahi whakamāramatanga ohorere me te hono atu anō ki tana hoa pātui mamaeroa a Bough, e whakatautauhia ana e Ben Miller.
Kua mārena a Bough ināianei, he kaiārahi wakataua ruku, ki tētahi wahine whakaparana e whakatautahia ana e Vicki Pepperdine.
Nō reira kua hoki mai te tokorua pērā i a Batman rāua ko Robin e rite nei ā rāua hapa nui e mahi nei mā te Secret Service a te Kuini, ka tūtaki ki te kiripuaki ātaahua o Olga Kurylenko a Ophelia Bulletova.
Nō reira, kei te riro ngā whakaaro o te pirimia i a tangata whairawa nui o te ao hangarau e kerēme ana ka taea e ia te rongoā ngā raruraru rorohiko o Piritana: te tangata kino a Jason Volta, te tangata kino nei a Jake Lacy.
Ka tīmata ngā mahi manuware a English rāua ko Bough: ka whakataruna rāua hei weita, i tahuna e rāua tētahi whare hoko kai Wīwī; he mahi whakahārangi i a rāua e eke whānako atu ki te wakarā whai rawa o Volta; ka tīrangorango katoa i a English i a ka whakamahi i tētahi maupane Ao Mariko hei whakaharatau i a ia ki ngā āhuatanga i roto o te whare o Volta.
Ka tino whakapau kaha rawa atu mō te wāhanga whakamutunga, engari ahakoa te ngāwari me te tūperepere, he tino hāngai ki ngā āhuatanga pouaka whakaata o te tamariki.
He āhua ngāwari noa.
Ā, pērā i ētahi atu kiriata Johnny English ka whakaaro ahau: he aha te take kāore e taea e te ahumahi whitiāhua o Piritana tuku tētahi tūranga whitiāhua ki a Rowan Atkinson e tino whakamana ana i ōna pūmanawa?
E whakahē ana a Labour kei te hanga mahere ia mō ngā tāngata o Piritana kia huri ki tētahi wiki mahi mō ngā e whā engari kia utua mō ngā rā e rima
Kei te whiriwhiri te Rōpū Labour o Jeremy Corbyn ki te whiriwhiri i tētahi mahere tino rerekē e mahi ai ngā tāngata o Piritana i ngā rā e whā o te wiki - engari ka utua mō ngā rā e rima.
E ai ki te kōrero kei te hiahia te pāti kia tukuna e ngā rangatira o ngā kamupene i ngā penapena ka hua ake i te hurihanga hinengaro hori (AI) ki ngā kaimahi mā te tuku i tētahi rā whakatā ki a rātou.
Ka whiwhi ngā kaimahi i tētahi mutunga wiki toru rā - engari ka ōrite tonu te utu.
I ngā puna kōrero ka ‘hāngai’ te whakaaro ki te kaupapa ōhanga a te rōpū, ā, me te whakarite ka tautoko te motu i ngā kaimahi.
Kua tautokohia te neke ki tētahi wiki mahi whā rā e te Trades Union Congress e whai hua ai ngā kaimahi mai i te ōhanga hurihuri.
I kī atu tētahi puna kōrero matua o te Rōpū Labour ki te Sunday Times: ‘E tūmanakohia ana ka whakaputaina tētahi arotake kaupapahere i mua i te mutunga o te tau.
‘Kāore e wawe te whakatinanahia engari he manako te wiki mahi whā rā e ū ana ki te ara a te rōpū mō te whakataurite i te ōhanga e tītaha ana ki te kaimahi me te rautaki ahumahi whānui o te rōpū.’
Ehara ko te Rōpū Labour te rōpū tuatahi ki te tautoko i tētahi whakaaro pērā, ā, i oati ana te Rōpū Green i tētahi wiki mahi whā rā i tana whakahau pōtitanga whānui i te tau 2017.
Engari, kāore te manako nei i te tautoko whānuitia e te katoa o te Rōpū Labour.
I kī tētahi kaikōrero Rōpū Labour: ‘Ehara te wiki mahi whā rā i te kaupapahere at erōpū, ā, kāore i te whiriwhiria e te rōpū i tēnei wā.’
I whakamahia e te Chancellor apitihana a John McDonnell i te hui a Labour i tērā wiki ki te wherawhera i tana matakitenga mō tētahi hurihanga manawa pāpori i roto i te ōhanga.
I kī a Mr McDonnell ka ūpoko pakaru ia ki te tango mai i te mana mai i ‘ngā tumuaki kanohi-kore’ me te ‘hunga hao’ i ngā umanga whaipainga.
I roto i ngā mahere a te tumuaki mātāmua apitihana kāore pea e hoki te katoa o te punga a ngā kaipurihea kamupene wai i te mea ka whakaritea pea e te kāwanatanga Labour ‘ngā tangohanga’ i runga i te whakatau kei te hē.
I whakaū anō ia ki te whakauru i ngā kaimahi ki ngā poari kamupene me te waihanga i Ngā Tahua Rangatiratanga Whakaurunga kia tukuna i te 10 ōrau o ngā tūtanga umanga rāngai-tūmatanui ki ngā kaimahi, ka whiwhi pea i ngā moni hua ā-tau atu ki te £500.
Ka kōrero atu a Lindsey Graham me John Kennedy ki a “60 Minutes” mēnā ka taea e te tūhuratanga a te FBI ō rāua whakaaro
Nā te tūhuratanga a te FBI ki ngā whakapae mō Kaiwhakawā Brett Kavanaugh kua tōmuri te pōti whakamutunga mō tana kōharitanga ki te Kōti Matua mā te kotahi wiki i te iti rawa, ā, ka puta te pātai mēnā ka taea e ngā kitenga te whakahau ngā kaihanga ture Republican te kukume mai i ā rātou tautoko.
I tētahi uiui ka whakaaturia ā te Rātapu, i pātai atu te kairīpoata “60 Minutes” a Scott Pelley ki ngā Senator Republican a John Kennedy rāua ko Lindsey Graham mēnā ka kitea te FBI tētahi mea hei huri i ō rāua whakaaro.
I te tuwhera ake ngā whakaaro o Kennedy i tana hoa o South Carolina.
“Me kī, āe,” te kī a Kennedy.
“I kī ahau i mua i te whakawātanga, i kōrero ahau ki te Kaiwhakawā Kavanaugh.
I waea atu ahau ki a ia whai muri i te putanga o tēnei whakapae, ka kī atu, ‘Kei te hara koe?’
I niwha, mārō, tapatahi ia.”
Engari, te āhua nei kua kōhatu kē te pōti a Graham.
“Kua tau ōku whakaaro mō Brett Kavanaugh, ā, ka mutu mā tētahi whakapae tino nui e huri ai,” tana kī.
“Tākuta Ford, kāore au i te mōhio i aha, engari kei te mōhio ahau ki tēnei: I kaha te whakahē a Brett,” te kī anō a Graham, e kōrero ana mō Christine Blasey Ford.
“Me te aha kāore i taea e ngā tāngata katoa i whakahuatia e ia te whakamana.
Kua 36 tau te tawhito.
Kāore ahau i te kite e rerekē ana.”
He aha te Global Citizen Festival, ā, i Tutuki He Hua ki te Whakaheke i te Rawa Kore?
I tēnei Rāhoroi ka whakahaerehia e New York te Global Citizen Festival, he huihuinga puoro ā-tau e whai ana i ngā kaiwaiata tino rongonui me tētahi umanga tino rawe; te whakamutu i te rawa kore i te ao katoa.
Koinei te tau tuawhitu, e huihui mai ai te tini me te mano ki te Global Citizen Festival i te Great Lawn i Central Park ki te pārekareka ki ngā kaiwaiata pērā i a Janet Jackson, Cardi B me Shawn Mendes, engari me te hāpai anō i te whāinga o te huihuinga ki te whakamutu i te tino whai rawa i mua o te 2030.
Ko te Global Citizen Festival, i kī i te tau 2012, he whānuitanga o te Global Citizen Festival, he rōpū taunaki e manako ana ki te whakamutu atu i te rawa kore mā te whakarahi ake i te maha o te hunga e pakanga ana i tēnei.
Hei whiwhi i tētahi tīkiti koreutu mō te huihuinga (engari ia mēnā kei te hiahia koe ki te utu i tētahi tīkiti VIP), i mate te hunga haere ki te konohete ki te whakatutuki i ētahi mahi, “mahinga” rānei pērā i te mahi tūao, te īmēra ki tētahi rangatira nō te ao, te tuku waea, te whai rānei i ētahi atu tikanga whaitake hei āwhina ki te hāpai i te whāinga ki te whakamutu i te rawa kore.
Engari i pēhea nei te momoho o te Global Citizen Festival i roto i te 12 tau e toe ana ki te whakatutuki ana i tana whāinga?
Ko te whakaaro o te utu i ngā tāngata me tētahi konohete koreutu tūturu hei whakahau i ngā tāngata kia maranga ake, ko taua āhuatanga anō rānei o te “pāwhiritanga” - ko te whakaaro o ngā tāngata kei te tino whai kiko rātou mā te waitohu i tētahi petihana tuihono, te tuku rānei i tētahi tīhau?
Mai i te tau 2011, e kīia ana te Global Citizen kua hopukia e Global Citizen ngā “mahinga” 19 miriona mai i ana kaitautoko, e whakahau ana i ētahi whāinga rerekē.
E kīia ana nā ēnei mahinga i āwhina i ngā rangatira o te ao ki te whakapuaki i ō rātou paiherenga, kaupapahere hoki e neke atu ana i te $37 piriona ka whai pānga ki ngā ao o ngā tāngata neke atu i te 2.25 piriona hei te 2030.
I te tīmatanga o te 2018, e kī ana ngā rōpū 390 ngā paiherenga me ngā whakapuaki mai i ana mahi, he $10 piriona iti te rawa kua tohaina kēhia, kua kohia rānei.
E kī ana te rōpū i whai pānga tōtika ngā pūtea ki ngā tāngata tata ki te 649 miriona puta noa i te ao.
Ko ētahi o ngā paiherenga hira ko The Power of Nutrition, he pātuitanga kaihaumi me ngā kaiwhakatinana i te U.K. e pūmau ana ki te “āwhina i ngā tamariki kia tipu ki te whakatutuki i ō rātou pūmanawa,” e oati ana ki te tuku i te $35 miriona ki Rwanda hei āwhina ki te whakamutu i te kore kai i taua whenua whai muri i te whiwhitanga o ngā tīhau neke atu i te 4,700 mai i Ngā Kirirarau o te Ao.
“Mā ngā tautoko a te kāwanatanga o te U.K., ngā kāwanatanga ā-motu, me Ngā Kirirarau o te Ao pērā i a koe, ka taea te whakarite i te tūkino pāpori o te kore kai ki roto i ngā pukapuka hītori,” te kōrero a te māngai o The Power of Nutrition a Tracey Ullman ki te marea i tētahi konohete i Rānana i te Paengawhāwhā 2018.
I kī anō te rōpū whai muri muri i ngā tūmahi nui atu i te 5,000 e tono ana i te U.K. kia whakapai ake i ngā kai mā ngā māmā me ngā tamariki, i whakaputaina e te kāwanatanga he pūtea mō tētahi kaupapa, te Power of Nutrition, ka tae ki ngā wāhine me ngā tamariki 5 miriona me ngā wawaotanga kai tika.
I te urupare ki tētahi o ngā FAQs kei tana paetukutuku e pātai ana “he aha koe e whakaaro ai ka taea e tātau te rawa kore nu te whakakore atu?”
I whakautu te kirirarau o te ao: “He huarahi roa, uaua hoki - i ētahi wā ka hinga pore mātou, ka hinga mātou.
Engari, pērā anō i ngā kaupapa tika ā-iwi nui, ārai-kaikiri rānei i mua, ka tutuki mātou, i te mea ka kaha ake tātou i roto i te kotahitanga.
Ko Janet Jackson, the Weeknd, Shawn Mendes, Cardi B, Janelle Monáe ētahi o ngā kaiwaiata kei te tū i te huihuinga o tēnei tau i Te Āporo Nui, ā, ko te Deborra-Lee Furness rāua ko Hugh Jackman ngā kaihautū.
Ka whakamahi pea te US i te Taua Moana hei “whakapā” kia raru ngā hoko ki tai pūngao a Rūhia - Hekeretari ā-Motu
Ka taea e Washington “mēnā e tika ana” te whakamahi i tana Taua Moana hei ārai i te tae atu o ngā pūngao a Rūhia ki ngā mākete, tae atu ki Waenga Rāwhiti, te kōrero a te Hekeretari ā-Motu o te US a Ryan Zinke, e ai ki te Washington Examiner.
E whakapae ana a Zinke ko te kaupapa ake o te whakauru atu o Rūhia ki Hiria - otirā i haere i runga i te tono a te kāwanatanga ake o reira - he hōpara i ngā mākete pūngao hōu.
“E whakapono ahau ko te kaupapa ake kei Waenga Rāwhiti rātou ko te whakariterite i ngā pūngao pērā anō i tā rātou mahi i Uropi ki te Rāwhiti, taha tonga o te puku o Uropi,” tana kī.
Ka mutu, e ai ki te āpiha, kei reira anō ētahi āhuatanga hei whakarite i tēnei.
“Kei Te Hononga o Amerika te kaha, me tō tātou Taua Moana, ki te whakarite kei te tuwhera ngā ara moana, ā, mēnā e hiahiatia ana te whakapā hei whakarite e kore ā rātou pūngao e tae ki te mākete,” tana kī.
I te kauhau atu a Zinke ki te hunga i tae atu ki tētahi huihuinga e whakahaerehia ana e te Consumer Energy Alliance, he rōpū huamoni-kore e kī ana rātou ko rātou te ‘reo o te kiritaki pūngao” i te US.’
I whakataurite ia i te whakarite a Washington i a Rūhia me Irāna, e kī ana ia he āhua rite tonu ēnei.
“Ko te kōwhiringa ōhanga mō Irāna me Rūhia, me kī he whakamahi i te mana me te whakakapi i ngā kora,” tana kī, me te kōrero mō Rūhia “kotahi anake tōna kaha” e whirinaki ana te ōhanga ki ngā koranehe.
Ka puta ngā tauākī nei i te wā e whai ana te kāwanatanga o Trump ki te whakapiki i te kapuni wē ki Uropi, e whakakapi ana i a Rūhia, te kōwhiringa utu iti ake mō ngā kiritaki o Uropi.
Mō tērā, ka whakamātau ngā āpiha o te kāwanatanga o Trump, tae atu ki te Perehitini o te US a Donald Trump, ki te mirimiri i a Tiamana kia puta mai i te kaupapa “hē” o te kaupapa paipa o Nord Stream 2, e ai ki a Trump, i noho “whakarau” a Berlin mā Moscow.
Kua roa a Moscow e kī ana ko te paipa Nord Stream 2 $11 piriona, ka huarua i te kaha o te paipa onāianei ki te 110 piriona mita pūtoru, he kaupapa ōhanga kē.
E tohe ana te Kremlin ko te whakahē kaha a Washington ki te kaupapa he take ōhanga kē, ā, he tauira hao.
“E whakapono ana ahau he ōrite o tātau whakaaro ehara te pūngao i te taonga pēhi, ā, ko te tikanga me āhei ngā kiritaki ki te kōwhiri i ngā kaiwhakarato,” te kī a te Minita Pūngao o Rūhia a Aleksandr Novak whai muri i tētahi hui me te Hekeretari Pūngao o te US a Rick Perry i Moscow i te Mahuru.
I tino rara a Tiamana ki tū a te US, i whakaū anō i tana pūmau ki te kaupapa.
Kua tono te whakahaere matua a Tiamana mo te ahumahi te Federation of German Industries (BDI), kia kaua e whakauru mai ki te kaupapahere pūngao a te EU me ngā whakaaetanga takirua i waenga i a Berlin me Moscow.
“Ko te raruraru nui ki ahau ko te whakararuraru a tētahi kāwanatanga kē ki tā mātau putunga pūngao,” te kī a Dieter Kempf, ūpoko o te Federation of German Industries (BDI) whai muri i tētahi hui i waenga i te Upoko o Tiamana a Angela Merkel me te Perehitini o Rūhia a Vladimir Putin.
Ka “Āta Tirohia” e Elizabeth Warren Te Tū Mō Te Perehitini hei te 2020, te kī a te Senator o Massachusetts
I kī te Senator o Massachusetts a Elizabeth Warren i te Rāhoroi ka “āta tirohia” e ia te tū mō te perehitini whai muri i ngā pōtitanga wā weherua.
I te wā o tētahi hui hōro tāone i Holyoke, Massachusetts, i kī a Warren ka whakaaro ia ki te tū.
“Koinei te wā mō te wahine ki te haere ki Washington ki te whakatika i tō tātou kāwanatanga pakaru, ka mutu me noho he wahine hei ūpoko,” tana kī, e ai ki The Hill.
“I muri i te 6 o Whiringa-ā-rangi, ka āta whakaaroaro ahau ki te tū hei Perehitini.”
I kōrero a Warren mō Perehitini Donald Trump i te wā o te hui i te hōro tāone, kei te “ārahina e ia te whenua ki ara hē.
“Ka nui rawa te māharahara i roto i ahau mō ngā mahi a Donald Trump ki tā tātau manapori,” tana kī.
I whakahē a Warren i a Trump me tana kaikōhari ki te Kōti Matua a Brett Kavanaugh.
I roto i tētahi tīhau i te Paraire, i kī a Warren “āe rā me whai tātau i tētahi tūhuratanga FBI i mua i te pōtitanga.”
Engari, e ai ki tētahi rangahau pōti i whakaputaina i te Tāite, ko te maha o ngā tāngata i te rohe pōti o Warren kāore i te whakaae kia tū ia ā te 2020.
Rima tekau mā waru ōrau o ngā kaipōti o Massachusetts “ko te tikanga” ka pōti i kī kia kaua te kaihanga ture e tū, e ai ki te rangahau pōti a te Suffolk University Political Research Center/Boston Globe.
Toru tekau mā rua i tautoko i a ia kia tū.
He nui ake te tautoko a te rangahau pōti kia tū te Kāwana o mua a Deval Patrick, 38 ōrau e tautoko ana kia tū ia, ā, 48 ōrau i whakahē i tana tū.
Ko ētahi atu ingoa Democratic e mōhio whānuitia ana i kōrerohia mō te tū pea ā te 2020 ko te Perehitini Tuarua o mua a Joe Biden me te Senator o Vermont a Bernie Sanders.

I hopukina ia, ā, ka hāmenetia mō te whakarekereke ā-whare i te pō o te Mane
“Ko ngā taumahatanga e pēhi nei i taku tama mai i tana hokinga mai, kei te mōhio ahau e mārama ana ki ētahi whānau mō ngā pānga o te PTSD me ngā wharanga ki ngā hōia i tō rātou hokinga mai,” tana kōrero atu ki te whakaminenga i tētahi huihui mō Donald Trump i Tulsa, Oklahoma.
Ko te kōrero a Palin mō tana hoputanga ko “te arewhana i roto i te rūma” me te kōrero anō mō tana tama me ētahi atu ika-ā-whiro, “kua rerekē rātou i te hokinga mai, kua mārō ake, me te whaaaro ake mēnā kei te whakautehia rātou mō ā rātou ko ō rātou hoa hōia me ngā hōia rererangi, me ētahi atu hōia a Tū, i whakapau kaha mō te motu.”
I hopukia ia e te ture i te Mane i Wasilla, Alaska, ā, ka hāmenetia mō te whakarekereke ā-whare ki tētahi wahine, te raweke i tētahi pūrongo o te whakarekereke ā-whare me te mau pū i a e haurangi ana, e ai ki a Dan Bennett, he kaikōrero mō Ngā Pirihimana o Wasilla.
18 ngā wāhanga whenua me D.C kei te tautoko i te wero ki te kaupapahere whakarurutanga hōu.
Tekau mā waru ngā wāhanga whenua me te Takiwā o Columbia kei te tautoko i tētahi wero ā-ture ki tētahi kaupapahere hōu a te U.S. e whakahē ana i te whakarurutanga ki ngā pārurenga e rere ana i ngā whakarekereke kēnge, ā-whare rānei.
I tāpaehia e ngā māngai mai i ngā wāhanga whenua 18 me te takiwā i tētahi whakarāpopototanga hoa o te kōti i te Paraire i Washington hei tautoko i tētahi wero ki te kaupapahere rapu whakarurutanga, te pūrongo a NBC News.
Kāore anō kia whakaaturia te ingoa whānui o te kaiwhakapae i roto i te kēhi Grave ki a ki a Sessions i tāpaehia e te American Civil Liberties Union i te Hereturikōkā e whakahē ana i te kaupapahere kāwanatanga.
I kī ia i tūkinohia ia e tana hoa “me ana tama kino o ngā kēnge,” engari i whakahētia e ngā āpiha o te U.S. tana tono whakarurutanga i te 20 o Hōngongoi.
I puritia ia i Texas.
Ko te kōrero a te rōia a te wāhanga whenua e tautoko ana i a Grace mō Te Kaiwhakaora, Honotura me Kuatamāra, he tino nui ngā kaitono whakaruru ki te U.S., he whenua ēnei e pēhia ana e ngā raruraru nui e pā ana ki ngā kēnge me te whakarekereke ā-whare.
I takahuria e te kaupapahere whakarurutanga hōu a te U.S. te whakatau a te Board of Immigrant Appeals e tuku ana i ngā kaiheke kore-mana e rere ana i ngā whakarekereke ā-whare ki te tono mō te whakarurutanga.
I kī te Rōia Matua a te Takiwā o Columbia a Karl Racine i roto i tētahi tauākī i te Paraire ko tā kaupapahere hōu “he whakaririka i ngā te ture o ngā tau maha o te wāhanga whenua, kāwanatanga me te ao.”
“E herea ana e te ture kāwanatanga kai whakawāngia ia kerēme whakarurutanga mō ngā meka ake me ngā āhuatanga o te kerēme, ā, e takahi ana i tērā i taua mātāpono,” te kōrero a te whakarāpopototanga a te hoa o te kōti.
I tohe ngā rōia i roto i te whakarāpopototanga ko te kaupapahere e whakahē ana i te urunga mai o ngā kaiheke he patu i te ōhanga o te U.S., e kī ana ko te nuinga ka uru hei rakahinonga, ā, ko rātou “ngā kaimahi e hiahiatia ana.”
I whakahautia e te Kōti Matua a Jeff Sessions kia whakamutua te tukua a ngā kaiwhakawā hekenga i ngā whakarurutanga ki ngā pārurenga e rere ana i ngā whakarekereke ā-whare, kēnge hoki i te Pipiri.
“E wātea ana te whakarurutanga ki te hunga e wehe ana i tō rātou whenua tipu nā te whakawhiunga, wehi rānei nā te take mātāwaka, whakapono, iwi tūturu, he mema rānei nō te rōpū, whakaaro tōrangapū rānei,” te kī a Sessions i tana whakapuakitanga i te kaupapahere i te 11 o Pipiri,
Ehara i te mea he whakamauru te whakarurutanga i ngā raruraru katoa -- ahakoa ngā raruraru nui katoa -- kei runga i ngā tāngata i ia rā puta noa i te ao.

“I ia meneti kua kawea mai e te waka tūroro ngā tūpāpaku.
He tino iti rawa te wai mā.”
I kitea ngā kainoho e hokihoki ana ki ō rātou kāinga, e wherawhera ana i ā rātou rawa kua kī i te wai, e ngana ana ki te tohu i ngā mea e taea ana.
E hia ngā tāngata i whara i te rū nui 7.5, ā, kua tino kī rawa ngā hōhipera .

“Kāore i whai wā ki te whakaora i a rātou anō.

Kāore au i te mōhio i ahatia rāua tahi ko taku tamaiti.
E tūmanako ana ahau kei te pai rāua.”
E whakapae ana te māngai kāwanatanga o te U.S. kei te ‘whakaweti’ a Haina mā ngā ‘pānui hapainga’
I te kotahi wiki i muri i te whakaputanga a tētahi nūpepa whaimana o Haina i tētahi pānui whā whārangi i roto i tētahi nūpepa o te U.S. e kōrero ana mō ngā painga taharua o te tauhokohoko ki te U.S.-Haina, i tuku whakapae te māngai o te U.S. ki Haina i a Beijing mō te whakamahi i ngā nūpepa o Amerika hei hora i ana whakaaro.
I kōrero te Perehitini o te U.S. a Donald Trump i te Wenerei kua taha ake nei mō te pānui a te China Daily i roto i te Des Moines Register - te nūpepa e tino hokohokotia ana i Iowa - i muri i te whakapae i a Haina mō te whakararuraru i ngā pōtitanga uepū o te U.S. i te Whiringa-ā-rangi, ā, kei te whakahē a Haina ki tēnei whakapae.
Ko te whakapae a Trump i te whakararuraru a Beijing i ngā pōtitanga o te U.S., e ai ki ngā kōrero a ngā āpiha o te U.S. ki a Reuters, e tohu ana tēnei i tētahi wāhanga hōu i roto i tētahi whakahau a Washington e kaha ana ki te pēhi i a Haina.
Ahakoa he tikanga noa mō ngā kāwanatanga o tāwāhi ki te tuku pānuitanga hei hāpai i ngā tauhokohoko, kei te nui kē atu te taupatupatu tauhokohoko i waenga i a Beijing me Washington, ā, e whakatauhia ana e rāua tahi ngā utu here ki ngā hoko ki uta tētahi ki tētahi.
Ko te kaupapa o ngā utu here rautipu a Haina i te tīmatanga o te taupatupatu tauhokohoko he patu i ngā kaitukurawa i ngā wāhanga whenua pērā i a Iowa e tautoko ana i te Rōpū Republican o Trump, te kī a ngā tohunga Haina me te U.S.
I kī a Terry Branstad, te māngai kāwanatanga o te U.S. ki Haina me te kāwana wā roa o mua Iowa, he takiwā tuku i ngā rawa ahuwhenua ki Haina, i whara i a Beijing ngā kaimahi, kaiahuwhenua me ngā pakihi o Amerika.
I tuhi a Branstad i roto i tētahi tuhinga whakaaro ki te Des Moines Register i te Rātapu, “kua kaha kē atu tā rātou whakaweti ināianei mā te whakaputa i ngā pānui hapainga i roto i ā tātou nūpepa wātea.”
“I a rātou e tuku ana i ā rātou kōrero hapainga, kei te whai te kāwanatanga o Haina i te tikanga tuku iho o Amerika i te mana ki te whakaputa kōrero me ngā nūpepa wātea mā te whakauru i tētahi pānuitanga utu ki te Des Moines Register,” te tuhi a Branstad.
“Engari i tētahi wāhi hoko nūpepa i tētahi tiriti i konei i Beijing, he iti noa ngā kōrero whakahē, ka mutu kāore koe e kite i ngā whakaaro rerekē o te iwi o Haina mō te hekenga ōhanga o Haina, ina kei raro te hunga pāpāho i ngā tohutohu a te Chinese Community Party,” tana tuhi.
I kī anō ia “i karo tētahi o ngā nūpepa rongonui o Haina i tana tono ki te whakaputa” i tana tuhinga, ahakoa kāore ia i kōrero ko tēhea te nūpepa.
Kei te Whakakaikiri te Rōpū Republican i Ngā Kaipōti Wāhine i Mua i Ngā Pōti Wā Weherua Nā te Take Mō Kavanaugh, te Whakatūpato a Ngā Kaitātari

Tē taea aua mea te whakahoki,” ko te kōrero a Grant Reeher, he ahorangi mātauranga tōrangapū i Maxwell School o Te Whare Wānanga o Syracuse, ki The Hill mō tētahi tuhinga i whakaputaina i te Rāhoroi.
I kī a Reeher kāore ia i te whakapono ka taea e te whakahau takamuri a Senator Jeff Flake (R-Arizona) kia tūhuratia e te FBI te whakarata ngā kaipōti e whakatakariri nei.

I te ata o te Paraire, i karanga ngā kaiporotū “November is coming!” i a rātou e porotū ana i te kauhanganui o te Senate i runga i te whakatau a ngā Republican e whakahaere ana i te Komiti Whakawā kia anga whakamua tonu te kōhari i a Kavanaugh ahakoa te kōrero taunaki a Tākuta Christine Blasey Ford,te pūrongo a Mic.

Whai muri i te whakahau a Flake, kei te tūhura te FBI i ngā whakapae i tēnei wā i whakaarahia e Ford me tētahi atu kaiwhakapae kotahi atu anō i te iti rawa, a Deborah Ramirez, te pūrongo a The Guardian.
I tukuna e Ford ana kōrero taunaki ki mua i te aroaro o te Komiti Whakawā i raro oati i tērā wiki mō te whakapae i whakaitohia ia e Kavanaugh i a ia haurangi ana, 17 ōna tau i taua wā.

Kei te Whakarite te Kaihanga o te World Wide Web ki te Waihanga i Tētahi Ipurangi Hōu Hei Whakataetae ki a Google me Pukamata
Kei te whakarewahia e Tim Berners-Lee, te kaihanga o te World Wide Web, tētahi umanga hōu hei whakataetae ki a Pukamata, Amazon me Google.
Ko te kaupapa hōu a te hautipua hangarau, a Inrupt, he kamupene ka whakawhānui ake mai i te pūhara pūtake tuwhera a Berners-Lee, a Solid.
Mā Solid, ka tukuna ngā kaiwhakamahi ki te kōwhiri ki hea rokiroki ai ā rātou raraunga, ā, he aha ngā mōhiohio e āhei atu ana ngā tāngata.
I tētahi uiui tauwhāiti me Fast Company, i te raweke noa a Berners-Lee ko te koronga o Inrupt ko te “whakahaere i te ao.”
“Me tutuki tērā ināianei,” tana kī mō te kamupene hōu.
“He wā hītori hira tēnei.”
“E whakamahia ana e te taupānga ngā hangarau a Solid kia āhei ngā tāngata ki te waihanga i tā rātou ake “toa raraunga tuihono whaiaro,”, he POD rānei.
Ka taea te whai ngā rārangi hoapā, ngā rārangi hei-mahi, maramataka, puna puoro me ētahi atu utauta whaiaro, ngaio hoki.
He pērā i a Google Drive, Microsoft Outlook, Slack me Spotify e wātea ana ēnei katoa ki te pūtirotiro kotahi i ngā wā katoa.
Ko te mea ahurei o ngā raraunga tuihono whaiaro kei te kaiwhakamahi te tikanga he aha ngā momo mōhiohio ka taea te toro atu.
E kī ana te kamupene mō tēnei ko “te whakamanatanga whaiaro mā ngā raraunga.”
Ko te huatau mō Inrupt, hei tā te CEO o te kamupene a John Bruce, mā te kamupene hei heri mai i ngā rawa, te tukanga me ngā pūkenga tōtika kia wātea mai ai a Solid ki te katoa.
Kei roto i te kamupene i tēnei wā ko Berners-Lee, Bruce, he pūhara haumarutanga i hokona mai e IBM, ētahi kaimahi kaiwhakawhanake i tīkina hei mahi i runga i te kaupapa, me tētahi hapori kaitūao kaihanga waehere.
E tīmata ana tēnei wiki, ka taea e ngā kaiwhakawhanake hangarau puta noa i te ao te waihanga ā rātou ake taupānga kua wetea mai mā te whakamahi i ngā utauta e wātea ana ki te paetukutuku a Inrupt.
I kī a Berners-Lee kāore rātou ko tana rōpū i te kōrero ki a “Pukamata me Google mēnā āe rānei, kāo rānei ka whakauru mai e rātou ngā rerekētanga nui e takahuria ā rātou tauira pakihi katoa i te pō.
“Kāore e mātou i tono mō tā rātou whakaaetanga.”
I tētahi pōhi i Medium i whakaputaina i te Rāhoroi, i tuhi a Berners-Lee ko te “uaratanga o Inrupt he tuku ngoi ahumoni me tētahi pūnaharauropi hei āwhina ki te tiaki i te pono me te kounga o te tukutuku hōu i hangaia ki Solid.
I te tau 1994, i takahuria e Berners-Lee te Ipurangi i tana whakatū i te World Wide Web Consortium i te Massachusetts Institute of Technology.
I ngā marama kua taha ake, he reo whai mana a Berners-Lee i roto i te tautohetohe kia noho herekore te tuwhera o te tukutuku.
Tae noa ki te whakarewatanga o Inrupt, ka noho tonu a Berners-Lee hei Kaiwhakaū me te Whakataka o te Director of World Wide Web Consortium, te Web Foundation me te Open Data Institute.
“Kei te tino ngākau rorotu ahau mō te wāhanga whai ake o te tukutuku,” te kī anō a Berners-Lee.
Bernard Vann: Kua whakanuia te minita Rīpeka a Wikitōria o te WW1
Kua whakanuia te minita o te Hāhi Mihinare kotahi anake i whiwhi i te Rīpeka a Wikitōria hei kairiri i tōna tāone ake i te kotahi rau tau ki muri.
I tohua a Lt Col Minita Bernard Vann ki te tohu i te 29 o Mahuru 1918 i te upokotaua i Bellenglise me Lehaucourt.
Engari, nā tētahi kaipupuhi huna ia i whakamate i ngā rā e whā i muri mai, ā, kāore i mōhio i riro mai i a te hōnore hōia teitei rawa o Piritana.
I huraina tētahi kōhatu whakamaharatanga e ana mokopuna tāne e rua i tētahi whakatūtū i Rushden, Northamptonshire, i te Rātapu.
I kī tētahi o ana mokopuna, a Michael Vann, he “tohu tino rawe” ka huraina te kōhatu i ngā tau kotahi rau pū ki muri mai i te mahi whakaharahara a tōna koroua.
E ai ki te London Gazette, i te 29 o Hepetema 1918 i ārahina e Lt Col Vann tana hokowhitu kua whakawhiti i te Canal de Saint-Quenti “i roto i te kohu, ā, e puhipuhita ana i mai i ngā pū repo me ngā pū hurihuri.”
I kōkiri ia i te mura o te ahi me te “tino māia” i ārahi ia i te pae kōkiri i mua i tana poke i tētahi pū repo ko ia anake me te whakamate i tētahi tokotoru.
I whakamatea a Lt Col Vann i tētahi kaipupuhi huna Tiamana i te 4 o Whiringa-ā-nuku, 1918 - neke atu i te kotahi marama i mua i te mutunga o te pakanga.
I kī a Michael Vann, 72 ōna tau, mō ngā mahi a tōna koroua “he āhuatanga tērā e kore nei e eke i a ahau engari ka noho whakaiti.”
I whakatakotohia anō e rāua ko tana tungāne a Tākuta James Vann tētahi rīhi i muri i te whakatūtū, i ārahina e Brentwood Imperial Youth Band.
I kī a Michael Vann he “hōnore nui mōna te whakauru ki te whakatūtū” me tana kī anō “e whakaarihia ana te māia o tētahi toa tūturu e ngā tautoko a ngā tāngata tokomaha.”
I oho haere tonu ngā kaiwhai MMA i te pō ki te mātakitaki te Bellator 206, engari i whiwhi kē rātou i a Peppa Pig
Whakaarohia tēnei, i oho haere tonu koe ki te mātakitaki i te Bellator 206 kikī ana i te tangata engari kīhai koe i āhei ki te mātakitaki te wāhanga matua.
I roto i te pire mai i San Jose ko ngā whawhai 13, tae atu ki ngā mea e ono kei te kāri matua, ā, e whakaaturia ana i te pō i te UK i runga Channel 5.
I te 6am, i te wā e whakarite ana a Gegard Mousasi rāua ko Rory MacDonald ki te whawhai mātātahi, ā, i tumeke ngā kaimātakitaki i te UK i te huringa o te whakaaturanga ki a Peppa Pig.
Kāore i rata ki ētahi i te mea i oho haere rātou mō ētahi haora i te pō ki te mātakitakii te whawhai.
Ko te kōrero a tētahi kaiwhaiwhai i runga Tīhau mō te whakawhititanga ki te pakiwaituhi tamariki he “mahi kino rawa atu.”
“E ai ki ngā ture kāwanatanga i te 6 a.m. kāore i tika tērā whakaaturanga nō reira i whakawhitia ki ngā whakaaturanga mā ngā tamariki, te kī a Dave Schwartz, te perehitini tuarua o ngā tauhokohoko me ngā whakawhitiwhititanga, i te pātaitanga mō te whakaaturanga.
""Peppa te poaka, āe."
I kī te perehitini o te kamupene Bellator a Scott Coker ka whakariterite mō ā rātou whakaaturanga kia uru ai ngā kaimātakitaki o te UK ā muri ake.
“Ki ōku whakaaro mō te whakaatu anō, ka taea e mātou whakatika,” te kī a Coker.
“Engari, he ono ko te karaka i te o te Rātapu tēnei, ā, tē taea e mātou tēnei whiriwhiri hei te Rātapu kē i tō mātou wā, ā, he Mane te wā ki a rātou.
Engari kei te mahia e mātou.
Me whakapono mai, i te whakawhititanga atu, he maha ngā patowaea i te haere atu me te hoki, ā, ka mutu kāore i te pai.
I te ngana mātou ki te whakatika, i pōhēhē kē mātou he hapa hangarau kē.
Engari kāhore, he take kāwanatanga kē.
E oati ana ahau e kore e pā mai anō tēnei āhuatanga.
Ka noho noa iho ngā whawhai e rima kaua ki te ono - pērā i te whakahaere ināianei - i kaha mātou kia nui ake ngā tukunga ki ngā kaiwhaiwhai, ā, i neke kē tā mātou mahi i tērā.
He āhuatanga whakarapa tēnei.”
Desert Island Discs: I ‘raro iho’ ngā whakaaro o Tom Daley mō anō nā tōna hokakatanga
I kī te kairuku Oromipia a Tom Daley i raro iho ōna whakaaro mōna anō i a ia e pakeke mai ana nā tōna hōkakatanga - engari tērā i puta ai tōna ihu
I kī ia, 24 ōna tau, nō tana taenga kē ki te tuarua i kite ia “kāore i te rite ngā tāngata katoa ki a ia.”
I a kōrero ana ki te Desert Island Discs tuatahi a Radio 4 e whakaaturia ana e Laruen Laverne, i kōrero ia mō ngā tika takatāpui kia whai “tūmanako” ai ētahi atu.
I te mea he matua ia kāore ia i tino aro atu ki te wikitōria i ngā whakataetae Oromipia.
Kei te whakatā te kaihautū ake o te whakaaturanga wā roa nei, a Kirsty Young, mō ētahi marama nā tōna māuiui.
I runga ia i te whakaaturanga tuatahi a Laverne, i kī a Daley he “iti iho ia” i ētahi atu i a ia e tipu ake ana nā te mea “kāore i tika te hiahia i te tāne me te wahine.”
I kī ia: “Atu ki tēnei rā, nā aua whakaaro iti iho, whakaaro rerekē mōku, koinei ngā āhuatanga i tino whai kaha ahau kia puta ai tōku ihu.
I te hiahia ia ki te whakaatu i “tōna mana,” kāore ia i hiahia kia pōuri ngā tāngata katoa ki a ia i te mōhiotanga mō tana hōkakatanga.
Kaihāpai LGBT rongonui te kaiwhiwhi mētara rauwhero Oromipia, ā, i whakamahia e ia tana whakataetae i Ngā Whakataetae Hoa Whenua o te Ao i Ahitereiria ki te tono i ngā whenua atu anō kia whakakorehia te hara o te takatāpui.
I whakaputahia e ia ōna whakaaro i te mea i waimarie ia ki te noho herekore, ā, ko tana kia whai “tūmanako” ētahi atu i a ia.
I kōrero te toa tātoru o te ao mō tana whakaipo ki tētahi tāne - te kaihanga kiriata o te US a Dustin Lance Black, i tūtaki rāua i te tau 2013 - "i tino ohorere rawa atu ahau."
I mārena a Daley i te kaiwhiwhi tohu Oscar, he 20 te pakeke i a ia, i tērā tau engari kī ia kāore he raruraru mō te rerekē o ō rāua taipakeke.
"Ina haere pā mai ngā taumahatanga nui i a koe e tai ana" - i haere ia ki ana whakataetae Orimipia tuatahi i a ia e 14 tau, ā, ka mate tana pāpā i ngā tau e toru e whai ake - i kī ia he uaua mōna te kimi i tētahi atu tangata e ōrite ana ngā tau i pērā anō te pā mai o ngā piki me ngā heke.
I te Pipiri i noho mātua ngā tokorua nei, ko Robert Ray Black-Daley tā rātou tama, ā, i kī a Daley i tino rerekē rawa atu "ōna whakaaro".
"Mēnā i pātai mai koe ki ahau i tērā tau, ko te kaupapa nui "Me whiwhi mētara kōura ahau," tana kī.
"Mōhio koe, arā atu anō ngā āhuatanga hira i tua atu i te wini mētara kōura Oromipia.
Ko Robbie taku mētara kōura Oromipia."
Kei tana tama te ingoa o tōna pāpā a Robbie, i mate i te tau 2011, 40 ōna tau whai muri i te kītanga kei te mate pukupuku ki te roro ia.
I kī a Daley kāore i whakaae tana pāpā ka mate ia, ko tētahi o ana pātai whakamutunga ki ahau mēnā kua riro mai i ahau ana tīkiti mō Rānana 2012 - i te mea i te hiahia ki te noho ki te pae o mua.
"Kāore ahau i kaha ki te kī atu 'kāore i konei ā taua wā ki te noho i te pae mua e pā", tana kī.
"I te pupuri ahau i tana rangi i tana hā whakamutunga, ka mutu nō te mutunga rā anō o tana whakangā, ā, nō te matenga i mōhio ahau ehara ia i te kiriūka," tana kī.
I te tau o muri mai i whakataetae a Daley i ngā whakataetae Orimipia 2012, ā, i riro i a ia te rauwhero.
"I te mōhio ahau koinei te mea i moemoeātia e au mai anō i te tīmatanga - ki te ruku i mua i tōku ake iwi i tētahi Whakataetae Orimipia, kāore he wairua i tua atu i tēnei," tana kī.
I puta anō tana kōwhiringa waiata tuatahi i tēnei - Proud nā Heather Small – i pā ki tōna whatumanawa i a ia e whakapakari ana mō te Orimipia, ā, ka rere tonu te ihi i roto i a ia.
Kei runga a Desert Island Discs i a BBC Radio 4 ā te Rātapu i te 11:15 BST.
Kua whakatahahia a Mickelson mō te Kapu Ryder ā te Rāhoroi nā tōna ngoikore
Ka eke i a Phil Mickelson o Amerika i tētahi rekoata ā te Rātapu i a ia tākaro i roto i tana tākaro Kapu Ryder 47, engari me tino piki ake te āhua o tana tākaro kia kore ai e miere tana tohu nui.
E tākaro ana ia i roto i te whakataetae ia rua tau mō te wā 12, he rekoata tēnei, ā, i whakatahahia ia e te kāpene a Jim Furyk mō te tākaro pōrowhā me te tokowhā ā te Rāhoroi.
Engari, kāore ia i te tākaro, ā, ko ia tētahi o ngā tino kaitākaro o te Hononga o Amerika, he e rima ana toa whakataetae matua, e wehea ana tana rā ki te tautoko i te kapa me te whakapakari i tana kēmu i te papa haupōro i runga i te tūmanako ka tika i a ia ana hapa.
Ehara ia i te kaihahau torotika rawa, pērā anō i te wā e toa ana ia, ehara te tangata nei, 48 ōna tau i te tino hāngai ki te papa haupōro o Le Golf National, e raruraru ana ngā hahau kotiti i roto i ururua roa.
Me te aha, i tua atu i te whakapāhunu o te papa haupōro, kei te tākaro a Mickelson, i te kēmu tuaiwa ā te Rātapu ki te Toa torotika o te Whakataetae o Piritana a Francesco Molinari, kei te taha ia i te pūhou a Tommy Fleetwood me tō rātou wikitōria i ā rātou kēmu e whā katoa i tēnei wiki.
Mēnā ka tino pai te tīmata a ngā Amerikana, kei muri rātou mā te whā piro ina tīmata ana i ngā kēmu 12, ka noho hira pea te tākaro a Mickelson.
Kei te pono a Furyk ki tana tangata, engari kāore pea e taea e ia he kōrero i tua atu i tērā.
"I tino mārama ia ki tāna mahi i tēnei rā, i papaki ia i taku tuarā ka awhi i ahau me te kī mai ka reri ia āpōpō," te kī mai a Furyk.
"Kei ngākau titikaha ia ki a ia anō.
He Tino Whakaihuwaka ia, ka mutu ia he nui ana tautoko i ēnei kapa i mua, me tēnei wiki.
Kāore pea au i whakaaro ake e rua anake ana kēmu.
I pōhēhē ahau ka nui atu i tēnā, engari i pērā, ā, koirā te āhuatanga i whiriwhiria e mātou.
Kei te hiahia ki te tākaro, pērā anō i te katoa."
Ka hipa a Mickelson i te rekoata a Nick Faldo mō ngā kēmu Kapu Ryder maha rawa i tākarohia i te Rātapu.
Ka tohu pea tērā i te mutunga o āna tākaro Kapu Ryder kāore nei pea i kātata ki ngā tiketiketanga o ōna ake taumata takitahi.
E 18 ngā toa o Mickelson, 20 ngā hinganga, ā, e whitu ngā hāwhe, engari i kī a Furyk he maha ngā painga ki te kapa mai i a Mickelson.
"He tangata pukuhohe ia, he hākiki ia, he koi, he pai ki a ia te raweke i ngā tāngata, ka mutu he tino tangata ia mō te kapa," tana kōrero.
"I pārekareka anō pea ki ngā kaitākaro tamariki ake te werowero i a ia i tēne wiki, ā, he ngahau tērā te kite atu.
He nui atu anō takoha i tua atu i te tākaro."
E mōhio ana te kāpene o Uropi a Thomas Bjorn ka tere kore atu tō rātou anga whakamua nui
Kei a Thomas Bjorn, te kāpene o Uropi, ngā wheako ka uaua rawa atu tō haere i te korenga atu o tō anga whakamua i te rā whakamutunga o ngā tākaro takitahi o te Kapu Ryder.
I tīmata te tākaro a te Tenemaka i te kēmu i te 1997 i Valderrama, i mua te kapa e kāpenehia ana e Seve Ballestoros mā te rima piro ki ngā Amerikana engari i toa tonu rātou mā te wehenga tino iti rawa, 14½-13½.
"Ka whakamaumahara haere tonu i a mātou anō i mua rā anō mātou i Valderrama; he nui te anga whakamua i Brookline, ā, ka mīere, me Valderram, i toa mātou, engari i waimarie, te kī a Bjorn, e whakaaturia ana, whai muri i te mātakitaki i te Rōpū o te tau 2018 e toa ana 5-3 i te Paraire me nanahi kia puta ō rātou ihu 10-6 i Le Golf National.
Nō reira mā te ahau e tohu, me te kapa katoa anō kia mutu tēnei tākaro.
Ka ūpoko pakaru koe āpōpō.
Haere ki te tākaro ka mahi i ngā mahi tika.
Kāore anō i mutu kia riro i a koe ngā piro ki te papa.
Mēnā he whāinga tā mātou, ko te wikitōria i tēnei taonga, ā, e mau ana ngā whakaaro ki reira.
Kua roa ahau i kī ana, e arotahi ana ahau ki ngā kaitākaro 12 o tō mātou kapa, engari kei te tino mōhio mātou he aha kei tērā taha e tū ana – ngā tino kaitākaro toa katoa o te ao."
Ka nui taku hari mō te āhua o te tākaro a ēnei kaitākaro i runga i tētahi papa haupōro uaua, te kī a Bjorn: "E kore ahau e kaute i aku pīpī.
He maunga tiketike kē hei kake āpōpō.
Ko ngā tākaro takitahi āpōpō, ā, he āhuatanga rerekē tēnā hei mahi.
He rawe te tākaro i te taha o tētahi hoa i te wā e pai ana te haere, engari i a koe e tākaro takitahi ana, kei te tino whakamātautauhia koe hei kaihahau.
Koirā te karere hei whakaputa māu ki ngā kaitākaro, kia whakaputa koe i tō tino toa āpōpō.
Ināianei, ka mahue i a koe tō hoa, a, kua haere ia ki te whakaputa i tōna tino toa āpōpō."
Hāunga a Bjorn, e tūmanako ana a Jim Furyk kia pai ake te tākaro takitahi a ana kaitākaro i ngā takitahi tēnā i ngā takirua, engari anō a Jordan Spieth rāua ko Justin Thomas, i riro i a rāua ngā piro e toru mai i te whā.
Kua pā a Furyk ki ngā taha e rua o aua hurihanga nui i te rā whakamutunga, i roto ia i te kapa i toa i Brookline, ā, i hinga rātou ki a Uropi i tākaro e kīia ana ko te "Merekara i Medinah."
E maumahara ahau ki ia kupu," i tana whakautu ki te pātai mō te āhua o te ārahi a te kāpene a Ben Crenshaw i te tau 1999, i ana kaitākaro i te rā whakamutunga.
"E 12 ngā kēmu hira āpōpō, engari ko te hiahia kia tere te tīmata pai pērā i Brookline, pērā i Medinah.
Ina rere te ia ki tētahi taha, ka uaua mō aua tākaro i waenganui.
Ka whakaritea e mātou tō mātou kapa e ai ki tērā me te whakauru atu i ngā tāngata e tika ana ki a mātou, e ngana ana kia puta ngā āhuatanga whakamīharo āpōpō."
Kua riro mā Thomas e ārahi i te urupare āpōpō, ā, ka tākaro ia ki a Rory McIlroy i roto i te kēmu matua, ā, ko Paul Casey, Justin Rose, Jon Rahm, Tommoy Fleetwood me Ian Poulter ētahi atu o ngā Uropi kei te wāhanga o runga ake.
"Koinei te raupapa o ngā kaitākaro i whakaingoatia e au i te mea e kapia ana ngā wāhi katoa," te kī a Bjorn mō ana tīpakonga takitahi.
Kua huakina anō te wakatauā hou o Tiamana
Ko te tikanga i whakahautia te wakatauā hou rawa o te Taua Moana o Tiamana i te 2014 hei whakakapi i ngā wakatauā o te wā o te Pakanga Mātao, engari kāore e taea atu hei tērā tau rā anō i te tōmua rawa nā ngā pūnaha hē me te nui haere o ngā utu, te kī a te hunga pāpāho o reira.
Kua hikina te whakahautanga o te "Rheinland-Pfalz," te waka matua o ngā momo wakatauā Baden-Wuerttemberg hōu rawa, mō te wāhanga tuatahi o te tau 2019, e ai ki te nūpepa Die Zeit e kōrero ana mō tētahi kaimahi hōia.
Ko te tikanga i uru mai te waka ki te Tauā Moana i te 2014 engari nā ngā raruraru i muri i te tukutanga i raru ai tēnei kaupapa hao nui.
Ko ngā momo waka Baden-Wuerttemberg e whā i otahia e te Tauā Moana i te tau 2007 ka whakakapi i ngā waka tauā Bremen tawhito.
E ai i ngā whakamārama kei roto tētahi pū repo tino kaha, ngā momo pahūtuku pupuhi-wakarere, pupuhi-kaipuke hoki me ētahi hangarau konihi, pērā i te hihiani iti rawa, ngā waitohu pōkākā me te hou mataaho.
Ko ētahi atu āhuatanga hira ko te roa ake o te wā i waenga wā tautiaki - ko te tikanga ka taea ngā waka tauā te whakatere mō te wā atu ki te rua tau mai i ngā tauranga o te hau kāinga.
Engari, nā pā mai tonu mai o ngā takamuritanga ka noho tawhito te āhua o ngā wakatauā hangarau hōu rawa - e kīia ana ka taea e Tiamana tōna aha te whakaatu i tāwāhi - ā te wā ka whakaurua mai hei whakamahi, te kōrero a Die Zeit.
I puta whānuitia te rongokōrero mō te waka tauā F125 raruraru nei i tērā tau, i te whakahētanga a te Tauā Moana o Tiamana i te waka, ā, ka whakahokia atu ki te iari waka o Blohm & Voss i Hamburg.
Koinei te wā tuatahi i whakahokia e te Waka Tauā tētahi waka ki tētahi kaihanga waka i muri i te tukutanga atu.
Kāore i te tino mōhiotia he aha i whakahokia atu ai, engari i ai ki te hunga pāpāho o Tiamana he maha ngā "maha me ngā pūmanawa me ngā pūmārō", ā, nā tēnei kāore he take o te wakatauā mēnā ka tukuna ki te pakanga.
He mea nui hoki ngā hapa pūmanawa ina e whakahaerehia ana ngā waka Baden-Wuerttemberg e ngā hēramana 120 - he haurua tēnei o ngā tāngata e hiahiatia ana ki te whakahaere i ngā momo waka tauā Bremen.
Me te aha, i kitea he tino taumaha rawa atu te waka, ā, he whakaheke i te mahinga me te whakatiki i te kaha o te Tauā Moana ki te tāpiri i ngā whakapaitanga ā muri ake.
Ko te whakapae he huarua ake te taumaha o te "Rheinland-Pfalz" 7,000 tana ki ngā momo waka tauā ōrite e whakamahia ana e ngā Tiamana i te Pakanga Tuarua o te Ao.
I tua atu i ngā pūmārō hapa, he raruraru anō te utu mō te kaupapa katoa o te waka - tae atu ki te whakangungu i ngā kaumoana.
Ko te kōrero kua tae atu ki te €3.piriona($3.6bn) - he pikitanga mai i te €2.2 piriona i te tīmatanga.
Kātahi ka tino hira rawa atu ngā raruraru o ngā waka tauā hōu rawa nā runga i ngā whakatūpato o nā noa nei kei te iti haere atu te kaha o te tauā moana o Tiamana.
I tēnei tau, i kī a Hans-Peter Bartels, te rangatira o te komiti ārai hoariri o te pāremata o Tiamana, kei te "itiiti haere atu ngā waka pakanga" o te Tauā Moana."
I kī te āpiha nā wai i hē kātahi ka hē kē atu, i te mea i whakawāteahia atu ngā waka tawhito engari kāore waka hōu hei whakakapi.
Ko tana pōuri kāore i taea ngā momo waka tauā Baden-Wuerttemberg te whakauru mai ki te Waka Tauā.
Ka whakarongo te National Trust ki te ao muna o ngā pekapeka
Ko te whāinga o ngā mahi rangahau hōu e whakahaerehia ana i tētahi kāinga i Ngā Pae Maunga o Kotirana he tūhura i te āhua o te whakamahi a ngā pekapeka i te whenua mō te aruaru kai.
Ko te tūmanako mā ngā kitenga ka mōhiotia ngā whanonga o ēnei whāngote rere ahurei me te āwhina ki te ārahi i ngā mahi atawhai ā muri ake.
Ka whaiwhai te rangahau a ngā tohunga pūtaiao a te National Trust mō Scotland i ngā pekapeka noa me te soprano pipistrelles, tae atu ki ngā pekapeka taringa parauri roa me te Daubenton i Inverewe Gardens i Wester Ross.
Ka whakatakoto haerehia ngā pūrere tāhopu i ngā wāhi hira puta noa i te whenua hei whaiwhai i ngā mahi a ngā pekapeka puta noa i te wāhanga tau.
Ka whakahaerehia anō e ngā kaimahi me ngā kaitūao a NHS i ngā rangahau mātai pūkoro mā ngā pūoko ā-ringa.
Mā ngā tātaritanga oro mātanga o ngā tāhoputanga katoa ka whakatau i te auautanga o te karanga a ngā pekapeka, ā, he aha ngā mahi a tēnā momo, a tēnā momo.
Kātahi ka whakaputaina e tētahi mahere wāhi noho me te pūrongo hei waihanga i tētahi pikitia tirohanga whenua taipitopito ā-whata o ngā whanonga.
E tūmanako ana a Rob Dewar, te kaitohutohu atawhai ao tūroa mō te NTS ka whakaatu ngā otinga ko ēhea o ngā wāhi o te wāhi noho he tino hira ki ngā pekapeka, ā, he pēhea te whakamahi a tēnā pekapeka, a tēnā pekapeka.
Ka āwhina ēnei mōhio ki te whakatau i ngā i ngā painga o ngā mahi whakahaere wāhi noho pērā i te waihanga tahora, ā, me pēhea te tiaki i ngā ngahere mō ngā pekapeka me ētahi atu momo hāngai.
Kua tino iti haere te nuinga o ngā taupori pekapeka i Kotirana me te UK i roto i te rau tau o mua.
Kei te noho mōrearea mai i ngā mahi hanganga, whanaketanga hoki e whai pānga ana ki ngā nohonoho me te kore wāhi noho.
He mōrea anō ngā kapohau me ngā rama, tae atu ki ngā pepa hopu ngaro me ētahi matū papanga hangahanga, ā, me ngā konihi a ngā ngeru mōkai.
Ehara ngā pekapeka i te kāpō.
Engari, nā ngā ritenga aruaru i te pō he tōtika ake ngā taringa i ngā karu mō te aruaru kai.
Ka whakamahia tētahi tikanga pāoro-wāhi mātanga hei kimi i ngā ngārara me ngā tauārai i te ara rere.
He mea nui ki te NTS, ko tana kawenga he tiaki i ngā whare neke tuku iho neke atu 270, ngā māra hira 38 me te 76,000 heketea whenua puta noa i te motu.
Tekau ana tohunga matatau, e whakahaere ana i ngā rangahau, ngā tirotirotanga nohonoho me ētahi whakaora.
Kua whakatūhia hoki tētahi whenua rāhui tuatahi i Kotirana kua wehea mai mō ngā pekapeka anake i te kāinga o Threave i Dumfries me Galloway, ā, koinei te kāinga o ngā momo pekapeka e waru o Kotimana mai i te tekau.
I kī te kaiwhakahaere o te kāinga a David Thompson koinei te wāhi tika mō ngā pekapeka.
"I konei i Threave he tino pai tēnei wāhi mō ngā pekapeka," hei tana.
"Kei konei ngā whare, ngā rākau tawhito me ngā wāhi noho pai katoa.
Engari he nui tonu ngā āhuatanga mō ngā pekapeka kāore i te mōhiotia, nō reira ko ngā mahi ka mahia i konei me ētahi atu whenua ka āwhina kia nui ake te mōhio ki ngā mea e hiahiatia ana kia momoho."
I āta kōrero ia mō te hira o te tirotiro mō ngā pekapeka i mua i tana whakahaere i ngā mahi tautiaki i ngā whare i te mea kei tūpono noa te tūkino i tētahi nohonoho kōhanga e taea ana pea te whakamate i ngā uwha me ngā pūhou atu ki te 400, ka ngaro pea te taupori paetata katoa.
E tiakina ana ngā pekapeka, ā, he takahi ture te patu, te whakatāwheta, whakapōrearea rānei, te tūkino rānei i ngā nohonoho.
Kei te whakatenatena a Elisabeth Ferrel, te āpiha o Kotirana mō te Bat Conservation Trust, i te iwi whānui kia āwhina mai.
I kī ia: "He nui ngā mea hei ako mō ngā pekapeka me te maha o ā tātou momo, kāore noa tātou i te mōhio kei te pēhea ngā taupori nei."
Ka whakahē a Ronaldo ki ngā whakapae pāwhera, kei te whakarite ngā rōia ki te hāmene i te moheni o Tiamana
E kī ana a Cristiano Ronaldo mō ngā whakapae pāwhera mōna he "rongokōrero teka", e kī ana ia "kei te hiahia rātou ki te hāpai i a rātou anō" mā te whakamahi i tōna ingoa.
Kei te whakarite ana rōia ki te hāmene i te moheni rongokōrero o Tiamana a Der Spiegel, nāna i whakaputa ngā whakapae.
Kua whakapaetia te poumua o Potukara me Juventus nāna i pāwhera tētahi wahine o Amerika, ko Kathryn Mayorga tōna ingoa, i tētahi rūma hōtera i Las Vegas i te tau 2009.
E ai ki te kōrero he $375,000 i utua te wahine e ia kia noho wahangū ia mō te raruraru, te pūrongo a Der Spiegel i te Paraire.
I tana kauhau i roto i tētahi ataata Instagram Live ki ana kaiwhai 142 miriona whai muri i te puta o ngā whakapae, i kaha te whakahē a Ronaldo, 33 ōna tau, me te kī he "rongokōrero teka."
Kāo, kāo, kāo, kāo.
Ko ā rātou kōrero i tēnei rā, he rongokōrero teka," te kī atu a te toa tārima o te Ballon d'Or ki te kāmera.
"Kei te hiahia rātou ki te hāpai i a rātou anō mā te whakamahi i tōku ingoa.
He mahi noa tēnei.
