Kei te hiahia rātou kia rongonui rātou mā te whakahua i tōku ingoa, engari he pērā i ērā mea.
He tangata hari ahau, ka mutu kei te pai," te kī anō a te kaitākaro, e menemene ana.
Kei te whakarite ngā rōia a Ronaldo ki te hāmene i a Der Spiegel mō ngā whakapae, me tā rātou kī "he pūrongo mō ngā whakapae e kore e whakaaetia mō te āhuatanga ki te tūmataitinga," hei tā Reuters.
I kī te rōia a Christian Schertz ka rapu paremata te kaitākaro mō "ngā makeretanga matatika ki tētahi rahinga hāngai ki te nui o te hara, ā, ko tētahi o ngā takahitanga nui rawa o ngā tika whaiaro i ēnei tau nei."
E whakapaetia ana i pā mai tēnei āhuatanga i te Pipiri 2009 i tētahi rūma hōtera i te Palms Hotel me te Casino i Las Vegas.
Whai muri i te tūtaki i tētahi whare whakangahau, e ai ki te kōrero i hoki a Ronaldo rāua ko Mayorga ki te rūma o te kaitākaro, e ai ki te whakapae i pāwheratia te wahine e ia, e ai ki ngā pepa i tāpaetia i te Clark County District Court i Nevada.
E whakapae ana a Mayorga i tau ia ki ōna pona i muri i raruraru e whakapaetia ana ka kī atu ki a ia he "99 ōrau" he "tangata pai" ia, ā, nā te "kotahi 'ōrau" ia i hē ai."
Hei tā ngā pepa i whakaae a Ronaldo i ai rāua, engari i whakaae tahi rāua.
E whakapae anō a Mayorga i haere ia ki ngā pirihimana, ā, ka tangohia ngā whakaahua o ana wharanga i tētahi hōhipera, engari i whakaae ia ki tētahi whakataunga i waho o te kōti i te mea "i mataku ia i te rautipunga", me tana māharahara ka whakamōrarotia tūmatanuitia ia."
I kī ia, 34 ōna tau, kei te whai ia ki te takahuri i te whakataunga i te mea kei te pā mai tonu te whetuki ki ia nā taua āhuatanga.
Kua tata kē ia ki te whakauru ki a Real Madrid mai i a Manchester United i te wā o te pāwhera e whakapaetia ana, ā, i tēnei raumati i neke ia ki ngā toa o Itāria a Juve mō tētahi whakaaetanga €100.
Brexit: Ka 'āwhiti te UK mō ake tonu atu' i te rironga o ngā kaihanga waka
Ka 'āwhiti te UK mō ake tonu atu' mēnā ka ngaro tana tūranga hei whakaihuwaka mō te mahi waka whai muri i a Brexit, te kī a te Hekeretari Pakihi a Greg Clark.
I kī anō ia e "māharahara ana" i te kī atu a Toyota UK ki te BBC ki te wehe mai a Piritana i te EU me te kore whakaaetanga ka hikina e ia ngā mahi waihanga mō tētahi wā i te wheketere i Burnaston, tūtata ana ki Derby.
"Me whiwhi whakaaetanga tātou," te kī a Mr Clark.
I kī te kaihanga waka Hapanihi ka ngaro pea ngā tūranga mahi nā te pānga o ngā takaware i te paenga whenua ki te kore e riro mai he whakaaetanga mō Brexit,.
Tata ki te 150,000 ngā waka i hangaia i tērā tau i te wheketere i Burnaston - he hanga i te Auris me te Avensis a Toyota - 90% o hokona atu ki te Uniana o Uropi.
"Ki āhau, ki te mīere a Piritana i te putanga i te EU i te pito o Poutūterangi ka tū te whakanaonga i tā mātou wheketere,", te kī a Marvin Cooke, te tumuaki whakahaere o Toyota i Burnaston.
Kua puta anō ngā mānukanuka o ētahi atu kaihanga waka o te UK mō te wehe mai i te EU me te kore whiwhi whakaaetanga mō te āhua o ngā tauhokohoko i waenga whenua, tae atu ki a Honda, BMW me Jaguar Land Rover.
Hei tauira, i kī a BMW ka kati tana wheketere Mini i Oxford mō te kotahi marama whai muri i a Brexit.
Ko ngā māharahara nui mō ngā āhuatanga e kīia ngā kaihanga waka he mōrea rārangi ratonga ki te tūpono kāore he whakaaetanga mō Brexit.
E whakahaerehia te rārangi whakanaonga a Toyota i runga i te tikanga "wā horo tonu", e taetae mai ai ngā wāhanga i ia 37 meneti mai i ngā kaiwhakarato i te UK me te EU mō ngā waka kua tonoa kia mahia.
Ki te wehe te UK i te EU me te kore whakaaetanga ā te 29 o Poutūterangi, ka pā pea ngā whakararutanga i te paenga, ā, ko te otinga atu hei tā te ahumahi ko ngā takamuri me te poto o ngā wāhanga.
Kua kore e taea e Toyota te pupuri i te rahinga rārangi taputapu mō te kotahi rā i tana wheketere Derbyshire, te kī a te kamupene, nō reira ka whakatūhia ngā whakanaonga.
E kīia ana a Mr Clark ko te mahere Chequers a Theresa May mō ngā hononga anamata me te EU "i āta whakaritea hei karo i aua tirotirotanga i te paenga."
"Me mātua whai whakaaetanga tātou. Kei te hiahia mātou i te whakaaetanga pai rawa e taea ai, hei tāku, kaua ko te angitu e kitea ana ināianei engari mō tātou ki te nanao atu ki tēnei whai wāhitanga," tana kī atu ki te whakaaturanga Today a BBC Radio 4.
"Ko ngā whakaaturanga kaua ā Toyota anake me ētahi atu kaiwhakanao me tino āhei mātou kia pēnei tonu te haere o ēnei rārangi ratonga tino angitu."
Kāore i taea e Toyota te ki e hia te roa e hikina ana aua whakanaonga, engari i te wā roa, ka heke te kaha whakataetae o te wheketere i te pikitanga o ngā utu, ā, taro rawa, ka whakakoretia ngā mahi.
I kī a Peter Tsouvallaris, kua 24 tau ia e mahi ana i Burnaston, ā, ko ia te kaiwhakarite a te uniana Unite i te wheketere, kei te tino māharahara ana mema: "Kua kite ahau ina ngaro ana ngā mahi e kore mō te hoki mai anō.
I kī tētahi kaikōrero kāwanatanga: "Kua whakatakotohia e mātou tētahi mahere tika, hāngai hoki mō tō mātou hononga anamata me te EU."
Ka hikina anō pea te hui a Trump me Rosenstein, te kī a te White House
Ka hikina anō pea te hui tūponotanga-nui me te rōia matua tuarua a Rod Rosenstein "mō te kotahi wiki", i te haere tonu o te whawhai mō te kaikōhari kōti matua a Brett Kavanaugh, te kī a te White House i te Rātapu.
Ko Rosenstein te kaitirotiro i ngā mahi a te rōia motuhake a Robert Mueller, kei te tūhura ia i te raweketanga a Rūhira i te pōtitanga, ngā hono i waenga i ngā kaiāwhina a Trump me Rūhia me te aukatinga pea i te ture e te perehitini.
Mēnā ka panaia e Trump te rōia matua tuarua, kāore rānei, ā, ka whakararu i te motuhaketanga o Mueller, te kōhimuhimu nui i Washington mō e hia marama.
I tēnei marama tonu, i pūrongo te New York Times i kōrero a Rosenstein mō te mau waea hei hopu i ngā kōrerorero me Trump me te whakaaro pea ki te whakakore i te perehitini mā te menemana 25.
I whakahē a Rosenstein i tēnei pūrongo.
Engari i tērā Mane i haere ia ki te White House, me te rērere o ngā whakapae kei te rihaina ia.
Engari, ka whakapuakina tētahi hui me Trump mō te Tāite, i Te Kotahitanga o Whenua o te Ao ia i Te Āporo Nui i taua wā.
I kī a Trump "kāore ia i te hiahia" pana i a Rosenstein engari ka hikina te hui kia kore ai e tukituki ki te whakawātanga a te komiti whakawā o te Senate i tuku whakaaturanga a Kavanaugh me tētahi o ngā wāhine i whakapae i a ia mō te whakaito, a Tākuta Christine Blasey Ford.
I te Paraire, i whakatauhia e Trump tētahi tūhuratanga kotahi wiki a te FBI ki ngā whakapae ki a Kavanaugh, e tōmuri atu anō te pōti a te Senate.
I runga te hekeretari pāpāho a Trump, a Sarah Sanders, i a Fox News i te Rātapu.
I te uitanga i a mō te hui me Rosenstein, i kī ia: "Kāore anō kia whakatauhia he rā mō tērā, tērā pea ka tū i tēnei wiki, ka hikina anō pea mō tērā wiki nā ērā āhuatanga katoa e pā ana ki te kōti matua.
Engari waiho mā te wā, ā, he rite tonu taku hiahia ki te whakamōhio haere i te hunga pāpāho."
Ka whakahē ētahi kairipoata i taua kōrero: Kāore anō kia whakahaerehia e Sanders tētahi kōrero whakamāramatanga mai i te 10 o Mahuru.
I pātai te kaihautū a Chris Wallace he aha i pērā ai.
I kī a Sanders ehara ko te kore e rata ki ngā kairīpoata pouaka whakaata "whakamanamana" te take he te iti rawa ngā wā tuku whakamārama, ahakoa tana kī: "Kāore ahau e whakahē i te kōrero tika he whakamanamana rātou."
Kātahi ka kī ia ka nui haere atu ngā kōrerorero i waenga i a Trump me te hunga pāpāho.
"He nui atu ngā wāhanga patapatai me te whakautu a te perehitini i ngā perehitini o mua atu i a ia," tana kī, me te kore tuku taunakitanga mō tēnei: "Kua tirohia e mātou aua tatau."
Ka haere tonu ngā kōrero whakamārama, te kī a Sanders, engari "ki te whai wā te hunga pāpāho ki te pātai tika atu ki te perehitini o Te Hononga o Amerika, he pai ake tērā i te kōrero ki ahau.
Ka ngana mātou kia nui ngā wā pērā, ā, kua kite koutou he maha ā mātou mahi pērā i ēnei wiki nei, ā, ka whakakapi tērā i ngā kōrero whakamārama ki te hunga pāpāho ina kōrero koe ki te perehitini o Te Hononga o Amerika."
Ka rite tonu te whakautuutu pātai a Trump ina wehe ia i te White House, e whai wāhi rānei ki ngā wāhanga tuwhera, ngā hui pānui me ngā manuhiri whai mana.
He tino rerekē ngā hui pānui takitahi.
I Te Āporo Nui i tēnei wiki i whakatauira mai pea te perehitini he aha i pērā mai, i tana whakaaturanga tene, korokē i ētahi wā i mua i ngā kairipoata i reira e huihui ana.
Ka tuhi te hekeretari hauora ki ngā kaimahi EU i NHS Scotland mō ngā māharahara mō Brexit
Kua tuhi atu te Hekeretari Hauora ki ngā kaimahi EU e mahi ana i NHS Scotland ki te whakapuaki i te mihi a te motu ki a rātou me te tono ki a rātou kia noho tonu mai i muri i te Brexit.
I tukuna e Jeane Freeman MSP tētahi reta i roto i te ono marama mai i te wehenga o te UK mai i te EU.
Kua pūmau kē te Kāwanatanga o Kotirana ki te utu i ngā tono kainoho mō ngā kirirarau o EU e mahi ana i roto i ngā ratonga tūmatanui kua whakawhitia.
I roto i tana reta, i tuhi a Ms Freeman: "I te raumati, e haere tonu ana ngā whakawhitiwhiti i waenga i te UK me te EU, e anga atu ana ki ngā whakatau e tūmanakohia ana i tēnei ngahuru.
Engari kei te nui haere ake atu ngā whakatikatika a te Kāwanatanga o te UK mō tētahi whakaritenga kore whakaaetanga.
E mōhio ana ahau he wā whakararuraru pea i a koe mō koutou katoa.
Koinei te mea i hiahia ahau ki te tārua ināianei ko te hira ki ahau o ngā mahi tautoko a tēnā kaimahi, a tēnā kaimahi, ahakoa nō hea rātou.
Heria mai ai e ngā hoa mahi nō te EU whānui, me tua atu hoki, i ngā wheako me ngā pūkenga hira e whakakaha ana me te whakapai ake i te ratonga hauora, e whiwhi painga ai ngā tūroro me ngā hapori e mahi nei mātou.
Ko Kotirana tō koutou tino kāinga, ka mutu e tino hiahia ana mātou kia noho mai koutou ki konei."
Ka Whiwhi Hāraparapara Ohotata a Christion Abercrombie Whai Muri i te Wharanga ki te Roro
I whiwhi hāparapara ohotata te kaiārai o Tennesse State Tigers a Christion Abercrombie whai muri i te wharanga ki te roro i te hinganga 31-27 i te Rāhoroi ki te Vanderbilt Commodores, hei tā Mike Organ o Tennessee.
I kī te kaiako matua o Tennessee State a Rod Reed ki ngā kairīpoata i pā mai i te wharanga i mua o te wā weherua.
"I haere mai ia ki te taha, ā, mea rawa ka hinga ki raro," te kī a Reed.
I tuku hāora ngā kaiwhakangungu me ngā kaimahi hauora ki a Abercombie i te taha i mua i te uta i a ia ki tētahi kauamo, ā, ka heria atu ia kia tirotirohia anō ia.
I kī atu tētahi āpiha nō Tennessee State ki a Chris Harris o WSMV i Nashville, Tennessee, i puta mai a Abercrombie i te hāparapara i te Vanderbilt Medical Center.
I kī hoki a Harris "kāore he kōrero anō mō te momo/whānuitanga o te wharanga", ā, kei te ngana a Tennessee State ki te rapu nōnahea i pā mai ai te wharanga.
Koinei te tau tākaro tuatahi o Abercrombie, he ākonga tau tuarua, me Tennessee State whai muri i te whakawhititanga mai i Illinois.
E rima ana tākaro katoa i te Rāhoroi i mua i te wehenga i te kēmu, ā, kua 18 katoa ana tākaro i tēne tau.
Ka nui ake te utu tāke tāpane a ngā kaihoko o tāwāhi ina hokona mai e rātou he kāinga i te UK
Ka nui ake te utu tāke tāpane a ngā kaihoko o tāwāhi ina hokona mai e rātou he kāinga i te UK, ā, ka whakamahia ngā moni tāpiri hei āwhina i te hunga kāinga kore i raro i ngā mahere hou a ngā Tory
Ka whakangūtia e tēnei āhuatanga te angitu o ngā mahi a Corbyn ki te kukume mai i ngā kaipōti rangatahi
Ka utaina te tāke tāpane ki te hunga kāore i te utu tāke i te UK
Ko te tūmanako a te Whare Tahua he £120 miriona i te tau ka riro mai - hei āwhina i te kore kāinga
Ka nui ake te utu tāke tāpane ki ngā kaihoko o tāwāhi ina hokona mai e rātou he kāinga i te UK, ā, ka whakamahia ngā moni tāpiri hei āwhina i te hunga kāinga kore, ka whakaputaina e Theresa May i tēnei rā.
Ko te whakaaro o ētahi mō tēnei whakaritenga he whakangū i te angitu o ngā mahi a Jeremy Corbyn ki te kukume mai i ngā kaipōti rangatahi me ngā kupu oati kia nui ake te wātea mai o ngā whare whaiutu me te whakahāngai i te hunga nui te moni whiwhi.
Ka utaina te tāke tāpane ki te hunga me ngā umanga kāore i te utu tāke i te UK, ā, ko ngā moni tāpiri ka ake ka whakapiki i ngā mahi a te Kāwanatanga ki te whakakore i te moe nauhea.
Ko te utu tāpiri - kei runga atu anō i te tāke tāpane onāianei, tae atu ki ngā rahinga nui ake i whakaurua mai i ngā tau e rua ki mua mō ngā kāinga tuarua me ngā whare reti - ka eke pea ki te toru ōrau.
Ko te tūmanako a te Whare Tahua atu ki te £120 miriona i te tau ka riro mai i tēnei.
Tata ki te 13 ōrau o ngā whare hōu i hangaia i Rānana ka hokona mai e ngā kainoho nō tāwāhi, e piki ana ngā utu, e uaua ake ai mō ngā kaihoko kāinga tuatahi ki te whiwhi kāinga.
Kāore he "tāone maha" i te maha ngā wāhi whairawa i te taiwhenua - otirā i te tāone matua - nā te maha o ngā kaihoko o tāwāhi e nui ake ana tō rātou wā i waho o te whenua.
Kua puta ake te kaupapahere hōu i ētahi wiki nei whai muri i te karanga a Boris Johnson mō tētahi tāke tāpare kia nui ake te hunga rangatahi e āwhinatia ana ki te whiwhi i tō rātou kāinga tuatahi.
I tuku whakapae ia ki ngā umanga hangahanga nui mō te noho teitei o ngā utu mā te hao i ngā whenua me te kore whakamahi, me te whakahau i a Mrs May ki te whakakore i ngā motunga mō ngā kāinga whaiutu hei whakatika i te "tāwai whare noho."
Kua whakapuakina e Mr Corbyn ngā hangahanga hou whare whakameremere e marohitia ana, tae atu ki ngā whakahaere reti me te whakamutu i ngā pananga "kore hē".
Kei te hiahia anō ia ki te tuku i ngā mana nui ake ki ngā kaunihera ki te waihanga whare hōu.
I kī a Mrs May: "I tērā tau i kī ahau ka tāpae i taku pirimiatanga ki te whakaora i te moemoeā o Piritana - kia pai ake te ora mō ia whakatipuranga hōu.
Arā, ko te whakatika i tā tātou mākete whare noho pakaru.
Ka noho tuwhera a Piritana i ngā wā katoa ki te hunga e hiahia ana ki te noho, mahi me te waihanga ao ki konei.
Engari, kāore i te tika mēnā he māmā mō te hunga kāore i te noho i te UK, me ngā kamupene o tāwāhi, te hoko whare hei kainoho Piritana pukumahi.
Mō te tino tokomaha kua tawhiti rawa te moemoeā o te hoko kāinga noho, ā, he tūturu rawa te āhuatanga whakaiti o te moe nauhea."
Jack Ross: "Ko taku wawata nui ko te whakahaere i a Kotirana"
I te kaiwhakahaere o Sunderland ko tana "tino wawata" ko te whakahaere i te kapa o Kotirana ā tōna wā.
Kei te rawe katoa ki te Kotimana, 42 ōna tau, te whakaora ake i te karapu Whakarua, kei te tūranga tuatoru rātou o League One, e toru ngā piro mai i te tūranga tuatahi.
I neke ia ki te Stadium of Light i tēnei raumati whai muri i te ārahi i a St Mirren kia hoki ki te Scottish Premiership i tērā tau.
"I hiahia ahau ki te tākaro mō taku whenua i ahau e tākaro ana.
I tākaro ahau mō te kapa tuarua ka mutu i reira," te kī atu a Ross ki a Sportsound a BBC Scotland.
"Engari, i pakeke mai ahau i te mātakitaki i a Kotirana i Hampden i te taha o tōku matua i ahau e tamariki, ā, koinei tētahi e kukume ana i ahau kia hoki mai rā anō.
Engari ka tae mai anake taua whai wāhitanga mēnā ka angitu taku whakahaere i te taumata karapu."
Ko ngā kaiwhakahaere i mua i a Ross i Sunderland ko Dick Advocaat, David Moyes, Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet me Paulo Di Canio.
I kī te kaiwhakahaere o Alloa Athletic o mua kāore ōna mātakutaku i a ia e whai ana i ngā toa i tētahi karapu nui, whai muri i ngā whakahē mai i a Barnsley me Ipswich Town.
"Ko te angitu mōku i tēnei wā 'mēnā ka taea e au tēnei karapu te whakahoki ki te Premier League?'
Nā te hanganga me ngā whakaurunga o tēnei karapu, ko tōna wāhi tika kei roto i te Premier League," tana kī.
"Ehara i te mahi māmā te tae mai ki konei, engari ka angitu anake ahau mēnā ka whakahokia e au te karapu ki reira."
E toru tau anake te roa o Ross i te ara whakahaere, whai muri i tētahi wā hei kaiwhakahaere kaiāwhina i Dumbarton me tētahi wā 15 marama i te rōpū kaiako o Hearts.
Kātahi ka āwhina ia i a Alloa ki te karo i te hekenga ki te taumata tuatoru, ā, i takahuri ia i a St Mirren mai i te heke atu ki ngā toa whakaihuwaka Championship i te tau o muri mai.
Ā, i kī a Ross kei te tino tau rawa atu ia ināianei tēnā i te wā e tākaro ana ia i Hartlepool, Falkirk, St Mirren me Hamilton Academical.
"Koirā pea te tino kuititanga," tana kōrero mō te ārahi i a Alloa.
"E tino whakapono ahau ko te whakahaere te mea tika ake mōku, tēnā i te tākaro.
Ka āhua rerekē te whakaaro i te mea i pai taku haere, i whiwhi oranga pai ahau, ā, i tae ki ētahi taumata pai.
Engari he uaua te tākaro.
He nui ngā mea me oti i a koe i ia wiki.
Kei te whai tonu ahau i tērā e pā ana ki ngā kōhuki me ngā taumahatanga o te mahi engari he tika ki ahau te whakahaere.
Mai rā anō taku hiahia ki te whakahaere, ā, kei te mahia e au ināianei, koinei te wā o ōku rā pakeke katoa i tino mauri tau rawa ahau."
Ka taea e koe te whakarongo ki te uiui katoa i Sportsound i te Rātapu, 30 o Mahuru, i Radio Scotland i waenga i te 12:00 me te 13:00 BST
Ko te wā tino tika mō tētahi paina ko te 5.30pm i te Rāhoroi, e ai ki tētahi rangahau
Kua piki ake ngā whiwhinga moni a ngā pāparakāuta o Piritana nā te hīrangi raumati engari kua nui atu ngā taumahatanga kua utaina ki ngā rārangi whare hoko kai.
I piki ngā hokonga o ngā pāparakāuta me ngā pā mā te 2.7 ōrau i te Hōngongoi - engari i heke ngā whiwhinga moni i ngā whare hoko kai mā te 4.8 ōrau, e ai ki ngā whika.
I kī a Peter Martin, o te umanga tohutohu pakihi a CGA, nā rātou i whakaemi ngā whika: "Nā te whiti haere tonu o te rā me ngā roa ake o te whāi wāhi o Ingarangi ki te Kapu o te Ao ki tērā e tūmanakohia ana i whai a Hōngongoi i tētahi tauira ōrite ki te marama o Pipiri, i te pikitanga o ngā pāparakāuta mā te 2.8 ōrau, engari ia i kaha ake te hahau i ngā whare hoko kai.
I hē kē atu te hekenga o te 1.8 ōrau i te whare hoko kai i te Pipiri i te Hōngongoi.
I kaha ake ngā pāparakāuta me ngā pā inu waipiro i ngā whare hoko kai.
I raru anō ngā pāparakāuta hoko kai i ngā rā paki, engari kāore i tino pērā rawa i ngā kaiwhakahaere whare hoko kai.
Te āhua nei i hiahia noa iho ngā tāngata ki te haere ki te inu.
Puta noa i ngā pāparakāuta me ngā pā i piki ngā hokonga inu mā te 6.6 ōrau mō te marama, ā, i heke ngā kai mā te toru ōrau."
I kī a Paul Newman, he kaitātari ngahau me te manaaki a RSM: "E haere tonu te ia i ēnei otinga mai i te mutunga o Paengawhāwhā.
Ka noho tonu te huarere me pānga o ngā huihuinga pāpori nui, tākaro rānei ngā āhuatanga nui rawa e pā ana ki ngā hokonga i te mākete i waho o te kāinga.
Ehara i te mea ohorere kei te uaua tonu ki ngā rōpū whare hoko kai, ahakoa rā ka tino mamae i te hekenga te 4.8 ōrau e ai ki te tau o mua, ā, me ngā pēhitanga haere to nu o ngā utu.
I tino hē te wā o te raumati wera roa mō ngā kaiwhakahaere hoko kai, ā, mā wā e tohu mēnā ka māmā ake i te Hereturikōkā i ngā pāmahana mātao ake."
Ko ngā hokonga tapeke puta noa i ngā pāparakāuta me ngā whare hoko kai, tae atu i ngā whakatūwheratanga hou, he 2.7 ōrau i te Hōngongoi, e whakaata ana i te hekenga o ngā whakaputanga o ngā momo.
E kohia ana, e tātarihia ana e te aroturuki hokonga ahumahi te Coffer Peach Tracker mō te rāngai pāparakāuta, pā me ngā whare hoko kai, ngā raraunga mahi mai i ngā rōpū whakahaere 47, me ngā huhuatanga tōpū neke atu i te £9 piriona, ā, koinei te paerewa ahumahi tūroa.
Kotahi te tamaiti i roto i te rima he huna pūkete pāpāho pāpori mai i ō rātou mātua
Kotahi te tamaiti i roto i te rima - ko ētahi he 11 tau te pakeke - he huna pūkete pāpāho pāpori mai i ō rātou mātua, kaiako hoki, e ai ki te rangahau
Kua kitea e tētahi rangahau o ngā ākonga kura tuarua 20,000 i te tipuranga o ngā whārangi "Insta meho"
Kua piki ngā mātakutaku i ēnei whakaaturanga kei te pōhitia ngā ihirangi hōkakatanga
Rua tekau ōrau o ngā ākonga i kī he pūkete "matua" tā rātou hei whakaatu ki ngā mātua
Kotahi te tamaiti i roto i te rima - ko ētahi he 11 tau te pakeke - kei te hanga pūkete pāpāho pāpori me te huna mai ō rātou mātua.
I kitea e tētahi rangahau o ngā ākonga kura tuarua 20,000 i te tere o te ipu o ngā pūkete "Insta meho" - e kōrero ana mō tētahi pae tuari whakaahua a Instagram.
Kua piki ngā mātakutaku i ēnei whakaaturanga kei te pōhitia ngā ihirangi hōkakatanga.
Rua tekau ōrau o ngā ākonga i kī he pūkete "matua" mā tā rātou hei whakaatu ki ngā mātua, me te whai i tētahi mā rātou ake.
I tūpono tētahi whaea ki te pae huna a tana tamāhine 13 tau, i reira ka kite i tētahi taiohi e whakahau ana i ētahi atu kia "pāwheratia ahau."
I kitea e te rangahau, nā Digital Awareness UK me te Headmasters" and Headmistresses" Conference (HMC) o ngā kura motuhake, 40 ōrau o ngā tamariki 11 ki te 18 tau e rua ā rātou pūkete, ā, haurua o rātou i whāki he pūkete huna ā rātou.
I kī te kaiārahi o te HMC a Mike Buchanan: "Ka nui te pōraruraru he tino maha ngā taiohi kua riro ō rātou whakaaro ki te waihanga wāhi tuihono e kore e kitea e ō rātou mātua me ngā kaiako."
Ka noho ko Eilidh Doyle hei "reo mō ngā kaipara" i runga i te poari o Scottish Athletics
Kua pōtihia a Eilidh Doyle ki te poari o Scottish Athletics hei whakataka whakahaere-kore i te hui ā-tau a te rōpū whakahaere.
Ko te Doyle te kaipara tauomaoma me te papa hākinakina whakarākei rawa o Kotirana, ā, i kī te tiamana a Ian Beattie he whai wāhitanga nui tēnei mō te hunga e ārahi ana i te hākinakina kia whiwhi painga mai i ōna wheako tino whānui i te taumata ā-ao i ngā tau tekau kua hipa.
"E tino whakautehia ana a Eilidh puta noa i te hapori kaipara o Kotirana, te UK me te ao, ā, e whakapono ana mātou ka tino whai painga a Kotirana i te heri mai i a koe ki te poari," te kī a Beattie.
I kī a Doyle: "Ka nui tōku hiahia ki te noho hei reo mō ngā kaipara, ā, ko te tūmanako ka taea e au te tino tautoko me te āwhina ki te ārahi i te hākinakina i Kotirana,"
Ko te Amerikana, i toa i te 200 mita me te 400 mita i Ngā Taumāhekeheke 1996 i Atlanta i roto i ana kōura Orimipia e whā, ā, he kaikōrero ia mā BBC ināianei, kua kore e hīkoi nā te pānga mai o te īkura roro transient ischemic.
I tuhi ia i runga Tīhau: “Kotahi marama i mua i pā te mate roro ikura ki a au.
Kāore e taea e au te hīkoi.
I kī mai ngā rata ā tōna wā ka mōhiotia mēnā ka hoki anō au ki te ora, ka pēhea rānei te āhua.
He mahi uaua engari kua hoki rawa au ki te ora, kua ako anō ki te hīkoi, ā, i tēnei rā e whakatūtū moruki ana!
He mihi nui mō ngā karere whakahauhau!"
Ko te pānui mapu ū e whakarite ana i ngā whaea ki ngā kau e whakawehewehe ana i te whakaaro tuihono
Kua whakawehewehe te kamupene mapu ū i te whakaaro tuihono ki te pānui e whakarite ana i ngā whaea whāngote pēpi ki ngā kau e mirakatia ana.
Hei tohu i te whakarewatanga o te mea e kīia nei ko te “mapu ū pūeru ngutu kau tuatahi o te ao,” i whakaputaina e te kamupene hangarau Elvie te pānui rūkahu i whakaohoohotia e te puoro ataata hei whakaatu i te wāteatanga e tukuna ana e te mapu hou ki ngā whaea kutētē.
Tokowhā ngā whaea tūturu e kanikani ana i roto i te whare witi e whakakapia ana ki te hei me te whakatangihia o te waiata e mau nei i ngā kupu pēnei: “Āe, ka miraka au i a au, engari kāore koe e kite i te whiore”, ā, “Mēnā kāore koe i aro mai ehara ēnei i te ū kararehe, ko aku ū.”
Ka haere tonu te huihuinga reo: “Mapua ki waho, mapua ki waho, e whāngai ana au i aua pēpi, mapua ki waho, mapua ki waho, E miraka ana au i aku wahine.”
Heoi anō, nā te pānui, kua tāngia ki te whārangi Facebook a te kamupene, i puta ai te tautohetohe tuihono.
E 77,000 ngā kitenga o te ataata, ā, he rau ngā pito kōrero, kua whiwhi te ataata ki ngā tauhohe rerekē a ngā kaititiro, ko ētahi e kī ana he whakakore i ngā “whakaweriweri’ o te ahumahi kau.
"He tino kino te whakataunga kia pānui i tēnei hua.
Pērā i a tātou me hapū rātou me te whakawhānau kia whakaputa i te miraka, engari ka tāhaetia ā rātou pēpi i te pahuretanga o ngā rā ruarua i muri mai i te whakawhānau,” te tuhi a tētahi.
Ka uru hakune te mapu ū Elvie ki roto ki te pari whāngote (Elvie/Whaea)
Ka kī tētahi atu: “He mārama te pāmamae mō te whaea me te pēpi.
Engari, āe, hei aha te whakamahi i a rātou hei pānui i te mapu ū mō ngā whaea e pupuri tonu ana i ā rātou pēpi?”
Ka tāpiri anō tētahi atu: “Kātahi te pānui kūare.”
Ka wawao ētahi atu i te pānui, me tētahi wahine e whāki ana he waiata “pukukata” ki a ia.
“Ki a au nei he whakaaro tipua tēnei.
Ka whiwhi au ki tētahi mēnā e whāngote tonu ana au.
Rite tonu au ki te kau i a au e mapu ana.
He āhua pōrangi tēnei pānui engari ka mōhio au koinā te āhua.
He hua tipua tēnei,” i tuhi tētahi.
Ka kī tētahi atu: “He pānui pārekareka tēnei e arotahi ana ki ngā whaea e mapu ai (i ētahi wā ki ō rātou wāhi mahi, wharepaku rānei) me te whakaaro he “kau” rātou.
Ehara tēnei i te pānui e whakamanahau ana, e whakawā ana rānei i te ahumahi kau.”
I te mutunga o te ataata ka whāki te rōpū wāhine i te kanikani rātou me ngā mapu hakune i kōpeketia ki ō rātou pari.
Ko te aroro hei kaupapa mō te whakamataaratanga i puta mai i te māramatanga he maha ngā wāhine e mapu-ū ai e whakaaro ana he ōrite rātou ki te kau.
Heoi anō he ngutu kau rawa te Mapu Elvie, kāore he waea, he pū rānei, ā, ka uru hakune ki roto i te pari whāngote, e whakawātea ana ngā wāhine ki te neke, hiki i ā rātou pēpi, me te whakaputa ki waho i a rātou e mapu ana.
I kī atu a Ana Balarin, hoa kaipakihi me te ECD ki Mother: “Nā te mea he hua whakawhana te Mapu Elvie i hiahiatia te whakarewatanga mumura, whakahorohoro hoki.
Nā te whakataurite i te wahine e kutētē and me ngā kau miraka i pīrangi mātou ki te whakaatu i te mapu ū me ngā wero katoa ki te tīwhiri, me te whakaatu i te ara ngahau, pākanga hoki, te aronga inati ki te wāteatanga e whakaputa ai te mapu hou.
Ehara tēnei i te wā tuatahi i uru te mapu Elvie ki ngā upoko.
I te wā o te Wiki Whakaatu Kākahu o Rānana, i kitea tētahi whaea ki ngā tamariki e rua ki runga i te arawhata ngeru mō te kaihoahoa Marta Jakubowski i a ia e whakamahi ana i te hua.
He Rau ngā Tamariki Manene i Māika te Nekehanga ki tētahi Puni Tēneti ki te Rohe
Kua koi te piki o te nama o ngā tamariki manene kua mauheretia ahakoa kāore i tino rerekē te whakawhitinga rohe, ko tētahi take nā ngā kōrero me ngā kaupapa here taumaha i whakaurua e te whakahaere o Trump kua uaua ake te whakanohonoho tamariki ki ngā kaitautoko.
I mua, i te nuinga o te wā ko ngā kaitautoko he manene kore puka, ā, kua mataku kei whakararuhia tō rātou āheinga ki te noho tonu ki te motu mā te hōkai whakamua ki te kokoraho i te tamaiti.
Ka piki te tūraru i te Pipiri, i te tauākītanga a ngā mana aka haumi me tuku ngā kaitautoko torohū me ērā atu mema pakeke o ō rātou kāinga i ngā makaurangi, ā, ka tiria ki ngā mana manene.
I tērā wiki, i taunaki a Matthew Albence, tētahi āpiha matua nō te Manene me te Whakauruhi Katimauhe, i mua i te Whakaminenga kua whakarau i ētahi taihana tāngata i tono kia tautoko i ngā tamariki kore kaitiaki.
I whakaaetia e te umanga e 70 ōrau o te hunga i whakarautia kāore i whai i ngā mauhanga taihara.
“Tata ki te 80 ōrau o ngā tāngata he kaitautoko, he tāngata rānei nō ngā kāinga o ngā tautoko, e noho turekore ana ki tēnei motu, ā, he wāhanga nui o ērā he manene taihara.
Nā reira e whai tonu ana mātou i aua tāngata,” te kī a Mita Albence.
E rapu ana kia tere ake te hātepe i ngā tamariki, i whakaputaina e ngā āpiha i ētahi tikanga hou e whakature ai kia puta ētahi i mua i te kōti i roto i te marama kotahi i muri i te mauheretanga, kaua ko te 60 rā, te tikanga i mua, e ai ki ngā kaimahi tāwharau.
He maha te hunga e puta mā te hui waea ataata, kaua e tae ā-tinana, ki te whakakuene i tō rātou kēhi mō te mana ā-ture ki tētahi kaiwhakawā manene.
Ko te hunga i whakatauria kāore e āhei ki te noho ka tere te terepu.
Ka roa rawa te herenga o ngā tamariki, e tinga ake ana te uru ki te mahara, te mate pāpōuri rānei, nā tēnei ka puta ngā whakarekereke, ngā whakamātau whakaputa rānei, e ai ki ngā kaimahi tāwharau me ngā pūrongo kua puta mai i te pūnaha i ngā marama tata.
Ka kī mai ngā kaiwawao he kaha ake aua āwangawanga ki te pokapū nui pērā i a Tornillo, e tinga ake ana kāore e kitea ngā tohu e takaoraora ana te tamaiti, nā tōna rahi.
Ka tāpiritia e rātou ko te nuku i ngā tamariki ki te tāone nui tēneti me te kore whai wā ki te whakareri i ā rātou mahamaha, ki te poroaki rānei ki ngā hoa e whakanui ake ai i te pāmamae e takaoraora ai aua tamariki.
Ka kī atu a Hiria ki ngā ‘taua noho’ nō Amerika, nō Wīwī, nō Tākei hoki kia maunu ināianei tonu.
E kōrero atu ana ki te Huinga Whānui o te UN, i tonoa e te Minita Pora Walid al-Moualem kia hoki mai ngā taurewa Hiria, ahakoa kua tae ki te tau tuawaru e haere ana te pakanga o taua motu.
I kī atu a Moualem, te pirimia tuarua hoki, ko ngā taua pora, e noho taihara ana ki te whenua o Hiria, me te whakataruna e whawhai ana ki te whakatuatea, ā, “ka meatia tikatia.”
“Me maunu rātou ināianei tonu me te kore heipūtanga,” tana kī ki te huinga.
Ka tohe a Moualem “kua tata oti te whawha ki te whakatuatea” ki Hiria, te wāhi neke atu i te 360,000 tāngata i mate i muri i te 2011, me ētahi atu miriona kua wehe atu i ō rātou kāinga.
I kī ia ka haere tonu te mahi a Tamakahi “e whawhai ana i tēnei pakanga tapu tae noa kia whakawāteatia ngā takiwā katoa o Hiria” o ngā rōpū whakatuatea me “tētahi whakatinanatanga pora taihara.”
E 2,000 ngā hōia nō Amerika ki Hiria, i te nuinga o te wā e whakangungu ana, e tohutohu ana hoki, i ngā taua Kōriti me ngā Arapa nō Hiria e mautohe ana i a Perehitini Bashar al-Assad.
Neke atu i te 1,000 ngā hōia nō Wīwī i runga i te whenua o taua motu kua kapi i te pakanga.
E pā ana ki ngā taurewa, i kī a Moualem he pai ngā āhuatanga kia hoki mai ai rātou, ā, ka uapare i “ētahi o ngā motu nō te uru” mō te “hōrapa mataku heahea” i kipa ai ngā taurewa ki noho tonu atu.
“Kua karanga mātou ki te hapori ā-ao me ngā whakahaere tiaki tangata ki te whakahaere i ēnei hokinga mai,” tana kī.
“E whakatōrangapū ana rātou i te take tāngata, kāore i tua atu.”
Kua whakatūpato a Amerika me te Uniana o Ūropi kāore e tukuna te āwhina whakahouhou mō Hiria āpā noa he whakaaetanga tōrangapū i waenganui i a Assad me te āpitihanga ki te whakaoti i te pakanga.
E kī ana ngā takawaenga o UN he whakaaetanga hou i waenganui i a Rūhia me Tākei ki te whakarite i te wāhi tauārai i te pā nui whakamutunga o ngā hauhau ki Idlib kua auaha te āheinga kia ahu whakamua ngā kōrerorero tōrangapū.
Ko te kaupapa o Rūhia-Tākei i kaupare i te whakaekenga tino nui e ngā taua Hiria e tautokohia ana e Rūhia ki te takiwā, he wāhi e noho ana ngā tāngata e toru miriona.
I āta whakamārama a Moualem he “aukatinga mārama” mō te whakaaetanga me te whakaputa i te wawata ko te mahi hōia ka whakapiro i ngā kairiri pakanga tapu tae atu ki ngā kairiri nō te Nusra Front kua tūhono ki Al-Qaeda, “e haepapatia ai”
Ko te wawata a te karere a te UN a Staffan de Mistura kia karanga i ngā hui tuatahi mō te komiti hou kei roto ngā mema kāwanatanga me te āpitihana kia te tuhi i te ture kāwanatanga mō muri i te pakanga mō Hiria hei ara ki ngā pōtitanga.
I whakatakoto a Moualem i ngā heipūtanga kia urua te kāwanatanga o Hiria ki te komiti, me te kī me herea te mahi a te paewhiri ki te “arotake i ngā atikara o te ture kāwanatanga o nāianei,” me te whakatūpato ki te raweketanga.
Te Take E Toa Ai a Tānapu i te Kaupeka Tuarua
I runga i taua whakakaupapatanga, ka toa a Mita Tānapu i te pōtitanga anō i te tau 2020 ki te kore e oti wawe tana perehitinitanga i te whakawātanga me te heitara, te wawata pea a ētahi kaimātakitaki rīpera.
Kāore e kore koinei “Te otinga tino nanawe o te perehitinitanga mau ake nei!”
I tēnei wā, kāore he tohu e ngenge haere ana ngā kaimātakitaki.
Mai i te tau 2014, ko ngā whakatauranga wā nunui neke atu i te huarua ki te 1.05 miriona ki CNN, ā, tata ki te tōtoru ki te 1.6 miriona ki MSNBC.
Ko te toharite o Fox News e 2.4 miriona ngā kaimātakitaki wā nunui, kua piki i te 1.7 miriona i ngā tau e whā ki mua, e ai ki a Nielsen, ā, ko “Te Hōtaka Rachel Maddow’ o MSNBC kua eke ki te tihi o ngā whakatauranga taura e 3.5 miriona ngā kaimātakitaki i ngā pō kawepūrongo nunui.
“He ahi tēnei e kukume mai ana i ngā tāngata nā te mea ehara tēnei i te mea e mārama ana tātou,” te kī a Neal Baer, te kaioma hōtaka o te whakaataata o ABC “Designated Survivor,” mō te hekeretari nō te rūnanga o te kāwanatanga ka tū hei perehitini i mua i te huaki i whakamōtī i te Kapitora.
Nell Scovell, he kaituhi pakeke i ngā whakaari pukuhohe me te kaituhi o “Just the Funny Parts: And a Few Hard Truths About Sneaking Into the Hollywood Boys" Club," kua whakaputa i te ariā kē.
Ka maumahara ia i te haerenga mā runga tekehī i mua i te pōtitanga i te tau 2016.
Ka kī mai te taraiwa ka pōti ia mō Mita Tānapu.
He aha ai? ka pātai ia.
“Ko tana kī, “Nā te mea ka whakakata ia i a au,”” ka kī mai a Miti Scovell ki a au.
He uaratanga whakangahau i roto i te aneatanga.
Kāore e kore, kāore e pērā ki tētahi atu mea i runga i te Pouaka Whakaata, ko ngā anga pūrākau e puta mai ana i Wahingitana ka whakarite i te anamata o Roe v. Wade, mēnā e āhei ana ngā whānau manene te whakaemi anō me te hauora o te ōhanga ā-ao.
Ko te kore aro he hāneanea e taea ai e ngā kaimātakitaki tino whai rawa.
Engari, he mea i tua atu i te kirirarau mōhio i a koe e tae atu ana ki te hāora tuaono e mātakitaki ana i te paewhiri mātanga e taupatupatu ana i te whakamahi a Bob Woodward i te “tuarongo hōhonu” hei mātāpuna mō tana pukapuka “Fear,” te hākete poma kirikau-otariti $15,000 a Paul  Manafort (“he kākahu whai whakahīhī mātotoru,” te kī a te Washington Post) me ngā hīraunga o ngā whakaaturanga ai a Stormy Daniels o te tinana, ā, o Mita Tānapu.
Ko au tētahi kāore e ōrite anō taku titiro ki a Super Mario.
“Ko tētahi mahi āna he whakarite ki tētahi hōtaka tūturu e whāngai ana ia i a koe ki tētahi mea ia pō,” te kī a Brent Montgomery, te tumu whakarae o Wheelhouse Entertainment me te kaihanga o "Pawn Stars," mō te hurihuri o ngā kaiwhakaari o te hōtaka Tānapu me ngā rerekētanga kakai ia rā (te whawhai ki te N.F.L, te whakamihi ki a Kim Jong-un).
Kāore e taea te mahue tētahi wāhanga kei mahue koe.
I taku taenga atu ki Mita Fleiss i tēnei wiki, he rā whiti e 80 tākiri i waho i tana kāinga i te takutai tūāraki o Kauai, engari kua uru kē ki te kāinga e mātakitaki ana i MSNBC i a ia e hopu ana i CNN.
Kāore e taea e ia te wehe atu, nā te mea kua reri a Brett Kavanaugh ki te noho ki te aroaro o te Komiti Kaiwhakawā a te Hīnota me te anamata o te Hupirīmi Kōti kāore anō kia whakaritea.
“Kei te maumahara i te wā e whakamahi ana mātou i ngā hōtaka pōrangi i ngā wā o mua me te kī a ngā tāngata, “Ko te tīmatanga o te otinga o te kaneketanga ā iwi o te Uru,””te kī mai a Mita Fleiss ki a au.
“Pēnei au he tūmomo kōrero whakakata, engari ko te āhua nei e tika ana rātou.”
Ko Amy Chozick, he kaituhi kaupapa wātea mō The Times e tuhi ana mō te pakihi, te tōrangapū me te hunga pāpāho, te kaituhi o te maharatanga “Chasing Hillary.”
He moni rāwaho e waipuke mai ai ki ngā whakataetae pōtitanga Whare tino tata
Ehara i te mea ohorere e kite ana te 17 o Pennsylvania i te waipuke ukauka, nā te tīaroaro anō i ngā takiwā whakakotahi i whakauru i ngā kainoho e rua ki te whakataetae kotahi mō te tūru ōrite.
Ko tēnei takiwā tapa tāone o Pittsburg i whakaritea anō inakuanei e whakauru i a Democrat Rep. Conor Lamb - i toa i tana tūru ki tētahi atu takiwā i te pōtitanga motuhake i tērā kōanga.
Kei te whakataetae a Lamb ki tētahi atu kainoho, Tūwehe Keith Rothfus, he māngai mō te takiwā 12 tawhito o Pennsylvania, e kaha inaki ana ki te 17 hou.
I whakaritea anō ngā mahere i muri i te whakataunga a te Hupirīmi Kōti o Pennsylvania ko ngā takiwā tawhito i raweke taiharatia hei tautoko i ngā Tūwehe.
Nā te whakataetae ki te 17 hou i tīmata te pakanga tahua whakamataaratanga i waenganui i ngā peka tahua o ngā pāti matua, te Komiti Whakakotahi Whakamataaratanga Manapori (DCCC) me te Komiti Whakakotahi Whakamataaratanga Tūwehe (NRCC).
Ka hau te rongo o Lamb i muri i te toanga tata ki te pōtitanga motuhake i tino mātakitakitia i te Poutūterangi mō te Takiwā Whakakotahi 18 o Pennsylvania.
Kua roa atu i te tekau tau te noho a tētahi tangata Tūwehe ki taua tūru, ā, ka toa a Perehitini Tānara Tānapu i ngā māka e 20.
E ai ki ngā mātanga tōrangapū he tata, engari kei mua ngā Manapori.
Ka Whakaaro Amerika ki te Hāmene i a Te Whakaora Mō te Tautoko i a Haina, Kātahi ka Taui
Ka kī ngā takawaenga kua āhukahuka kē te Whenua Tominika me Panama i a Peihinga, me te kore taututetute a Wahingitana.
He mahana te hui a Mita Tānapu ki a Perehitini Juan Carlos Varela nō Panama i te Pipiri o te tau 2017 me te whiwhi ki tētahi hōtera ki Panama tae noa ki te wā i peia atu te tima whakahaere o Trump Organization e ngā hoa kaipakihi.
Ka whakatau ngā āpiha nō te Tari Whenua Tōpū ki te whakahoki mai i ngā rangatira o ngā whakatakanga takawaenga o Amerika i Te Whakaora, i te Whenua Tominika me Panama mō “ngā whakataunga hou kia kaua e āhukahuka i a Taiwana,” te kī a Heather Nauert, te māngai mō te tari, i tētahi tauākī i te tīmatanga o tēnei marama.
Engari ko ngā hāmene i whakaaro noatia ki Te Whakaora, kua whiwhi, e ai ki te whakatau tata, $140 miriona āwhina nō Amerika i te tau 2017, tae ana ki te mana tarukino, te whakahaere me te tautoko ōhanga.
Ko ngā hāmene i marohitia, tae ana ki ngā tapahitanga o te āwhina tahua me ngā aukatinga kōkota heipū, ka tino pāmamae ki te motu nō Waenga Amerika me te kore mahi teitei me ngā pāpātanga kōhuru.
Ka haere ana ngā hui o roto, ka hiki ngā āpiha nō Amerika ki te Raki me Waenga Amerika i te hui matua i arotahitia ki te whakahaumaru me te tōnuitanga ōhanga hei whai i tētahi hui ōrite i tērā tau kua whakaarohia he ahu whakamua mō ngā whakapaunga kaha ki te aukati i ngā manene kia haere ki Amerika.
Engari tae atu ki waenga o Mahuru, kua whakamārama ngā āpiha whakahaere matua ka pīrangi rātou ki haere tonu te hui, nā reira i oti ai te whakaaro ki te hāmene i Te Whakaora.
Kua kīia ko te Perehitini Tuarua Mike Pence ka kōrero ki te hui, e whakaritea ana i tēnei wā mo waenga o Whiringa-ā-Nuku, hei tohu i te hira o te hui ki te whakahaere, te kī a ngā takawaenga.
Ā ka hoki māika ngā karere ki Te Whakaora, Panama me te Whenua Tominika me te kore hari i ngā karere taumaha, i ngā hāmene rānei nō Wahingitana
He māngai nō te Whare Mā mō Mita Bolton i whakapeka ki te kōrero mō ngā taipitopito o te taupatupatu i whakaaturia e ngā āpiha nō Amerika e toru, tae atu ki ngā takawaenga e rua, i whakaae ki te kōrero mō ngā whakataunga o roto i runga i te heipūtanga ka noho muna.
I whakaaetia aua kōrero e tētahi kaitātari o waho e tata ana ki te whakahaere, ā, i kōrero i runga i te heipūtanga ka noho muna.
Akona Hītori
Ko te hū hou e taka ai ko te pūrongo a te rōia motuhake Robert Mueller mō te āraitanga pea o te manatika, ināianei he nui te taunakitanga ki te mauhanga tūmatanui.
E ai ki ngā pūrongorongo ka huri a Mita Mueller i tana rangahau kia tirohia mēnā i mahi tahi te whakamataaratanga a Mita Tānapu me Rūhia ki tana huaki i ō tātou pōtitanga.
Mēnā ka whakarerekētia te āhua o Te Whakakotahi, ka noho haepapa a Mita Tānapu ki taua rōpū, i mua tata ake i tana putanga i mua i ngā kaipōti, ā, ā tōna wā pea ki mua i te hunga whakawā o ōna aropā.
He maha rawa aua mēnā, ā, kāore au i te kī kāore e kore ka hinga a Mita Tānapu - me ngā tāngata ōrite ki a ia i Ūropi.
He kōwhiringa mā tātou katoa i ngā taha e rua o te Ataranatiki e whakaaweawe i te roanga o te takaoraora.
I te tau 1938, kua reri ngā āpiha Tiamana ki te whakatū i te whananga ki Hitara, mēnā i ātete noa te Uru i a ia me te tautoko i ngā Tiekerowāka ki Mūnika.
I hinga tātou, ā, ka mahue te āheinga ki te karo i ngā tau tārukenga i whai atu.
Ko te ara o te hītori e kahuri i ngā wā panoni pēnei, ā, ko te hīkoi tē mutu o te manapori e tere ake ai, e pōturi iho ai rānei.
He āhua maha ngā wā panoni kei te aroaro o ngā tāngata o Amerika ināianei.
Ka aha tātou mēnā ka pana a Mita Tānapu i te Rōia Tianara Tuarua Rod Rosenstein, te tangata e whakahaere ana i te putanga o te rangahau a Mita Mueller?
Kei roto i te wai wera a Rosenstein mai i te wā i pūrongorongo tēnei pepa, i tērā tau, i marohi ia kia hopu muna i te perehitini me te whakapae kāore i te tau mō tana tūranga.
Ka kī a Mita Rosenstein ko te kōrero whakamārama a The Times he mākūware.
“Ka pēhea tā tātou urupare mēnā ehara te rangahau hou a te F.B.I i tonoa mō Brett Kavanaugh i te mea whakatutuki, tika rānei - mēnā rānei ka whakatūturutia ki te Hūpirimi Kōti  ahakoa ngā whakapae e taea ai te whakapono mō te pāwhera me te whakataki tito?
Ā ko te mea nui, ka pōti rānei tātou ki ngā kaupeka waenga mō te Whakakotahi e whakarite kia noho haepapa a Mita Tānapu?
Ki te rarahu tātou i aua whakamātautau, ka roa te hōtoke o te manapori.
Engari e whakapono ana au kāore tātou e rarahu, nā te akoranga i ako ai au i Prague.
Ko taku whaea he Tiu nō Tiekerowākia i tereputia ki Auschwitz e te tikanga whakahaere Nazi ōrite i noho ki taku kāinga takawaenga i tētahi wā.
I whakarauoratia ia, ka neke ki Amerika, ā, 60 tau i mua, i tuku i a au ki te tahu kānara Rā Tapu ki taua tēpu e mau nei i te swastika.
Mēnā koinā taku tuku ihotanga, ka pēhea te kore ngākau rorotu i roto i au mō tō tātou anamata?”
Ko Norman Eisen, he tāhake matua ki te Brookings Institution, ā, koia te heamana mō ngā Kirirarau mō te Haepapatanga me ngā Matatika ki Wahingitana, ā, koia te kaituhi a “The Last Palace: Europe's Turbulent Century in Five Lives and One Legendary House."
E ngākau rorotu a Graham Dorrans nō Rangers i mua i te whakataetae ki Rapid Vienna.
Ka whakamanuhiri a Rangers i a Rapid Vienna hei te Rāpare, e mōhio ana ko te toanga ki ngā tāngata nō Ateria, i muri i te ōrite hira i Peina ki Villarreal i te tīmatanga o tēnei marama, ka whakaputa rātou ki te tūranga kaha ki te puta i te Rōpū G o te Europa League.
Nā te whara pona i aukatia a Graham Dorrans i tana putanga tuatahi o te kaupeka āpānoa te ōrite 2-2 ki a Villarreal engari e whakapono ana ia ka taea e Rangers te whakamahi i taua otinga hei hūpana ki ngā mea hira ake.
“He māka pai mā mātou nā te mea he tīma pai a Villarreal,” te kī a te tangata e 31 ngā tau.
“I uru mātou ki te tākaro e whakapono ana ka riro tētahi mea i a mātou, ā, ka wehe me te māka.
Tērā pea e taea ai e mātou te tāhae i te mutunga, engari he otinga tika pea te ōrite.
He pai ake pea rātou i te haurua tuatahi, ā, ka puta mai mātou i te haurua tuarua, ko mātou te tīma pai ake.
Ko te Rāpare, he pō nui anō ki Ūropi.
Ko te tūmanako, ka riro i a mātou ngā māka e toru engari he tākaro uaua tēnā nā te mea e otinga pai tā rātou i tā rātou kēmu whakamutunga engari, ki te tautoko te mātoru i a mātou, ka mōhio au ka haere whakamua me te whiwhi ki te otinga pai.
He tau uaua tērā tau, hui katoa ko aku whara me ngā rerekētanga ki te karapu engari he āhua pai ngā piropiro o reira ināianei.
He pai te rōpū, ā, he pai rawa ki ngā tama i tēnei wā, he pai te whakangungu.
Ko te tūmanako, ka ahu whakamua ināianei, ka wareware i tērā kaupeka, ā, ka angitu.”
He moe whakatorouka tā te wāhine nā tēnei mataku penapena whakatā
Ahakoa he mārama rawa te whakaaro o ngā kaiwhakautu rangahau me pēhea rātou e tiaki, e torutoru noa iho rātou e kōrero ana mō te kaupapa nei ki ō rātou whanaunga.
Āhua haurua ngā tāngata i te rangahautanga Nationwide i kī e kōrero ana rātou ki ō rātou hoa rangatira mō te utu o te tiaki karioi.
E 10 ōrau anake i kī kua kōrero rātou ki ā rātou tamariki mō te kaupapa nei.
“E pīrangi ana ngā tāngata ki te tiaki i a rātou, engari kāore rātou e whakarite ana kia kōrero atu,” te kī a Holly Snyder, te perehitini tuarua o te pakihi inihua tauoranga Nationwide.
Me tīmata i konei.
Kōrero ki tō hoa rangatira me ngā tamariki: Kāore e taea e koe te whakareri i tō whānau ki te whakarato tiakitanga mēnā kāore koe e whakamōhio i ō wawata ki a rātou i mua noa atu i te wā.
Mahi tahi me tō kaitohutohu me tō whānau ki te kōrero ki hea, ā, pēhea e tiakina ai koe, nā te mea ko aua kōwhiri he tino kaupapa ki te mōhio he aha te utu.
Whakauru mai i tō kaitohutohu ahumoni. Ka āwhina tō kaitohutohu ki te whakarite i te ara ki te utu i aua utu.
Ko ō kōwhiri tahua mō te tiaki karioi ko te kaupapa here inihua tiaki karioi tawhito, tae atu ana ki te kaupapa here inihua tauoranga momorua hei tautoko i te whakakapi i ēnei utu, ko te inihua i a koe ake nā ō ake rawa - mēnā ka whai koe i te moni e tika ana.
Whakaritea ō puka ture: Aukatia ngā pakanga ture ki te ara kūiti.
Whakaritea te rīwhi tiaki hauora kia āhei koe ki te tautapa i te tangata pono ki te tirotiro i tō tiaki rata me te whakatūturu te tautuku a ngā mātanga i ō wawata mēnā kāore e taea e koe te kōrero.
Waihoki, me whakaaro i te mana rōia mō ō ahumoni.
Ka kōwhiri koe i tētahi tangata pono ki te whakatau i ngā whakataunga ahumoni me te whakatūturu te utunga o ō pire mēnā e mātengatenga ana koe.
Kaua e wareware i ngā taipitopito iti: Whakataruna he ohotata rata nā tō matua koroheke, ā, e haere ana ki te hōhipera.
Ka taea e koe te whakautu i ngā pātai mō ngā rongoā me ngā mate pāwera?
Whakaaturia aua taipitopito ki tētahi mahere tuhi kia reri ai koe.
“Ehara i te mea ko ngā ahumoni anake te kaupapa, engari ko wai ngā rata?” te pātai a Martin.
“He aha ngā rongoā?
Mā wai te kurī e tiaki?
Whakaritea tēnā mahere.”
I pupuhitia tētahi tangata i ngā wā maha ki te pū hau i Ilfracombe
Kua pupuhitia tētahi tangata i ngā wā maha ki te pū hau i a ia e hīkoi ana ki te kāinga i muri i te pō whakangahau.
Ko te kaupēhipēhi, e 40 ōna tau, i te takiwā Oxford Grove i Ilfracombe, Devon, i te wā ka pupuhia ki te tārāuma, puku me te ringa.
I whakaahua ngā āpiha i te puhanga, i mahia e tata ana ki te 02:30 BST, hei “mahinga tupurangi.”
Kāore te kaupēhipēhi i kite i tana kaituki.
Kāore ia e mate i ngā wharanga, ā, e inoi ana ngā pirihimana kia puta mai ngā kaiwhakaatu.
Ko ngā rū whenua me ngā tai āniwhaniwha ki Initonīhia.
Kāore e heke iho i te 384 tāngata i mate i te rū whenua kaha me te tai āniwhaniwha ki pā atu ki te tāone nui o Palu ki Initonīhia, te kī a ngā āpiha, me te kawatau ka piki te kōeke mate.
Nā te mea kua hinga ngā whakawhiti kōrero, kāore anō ngā āpiha whakaoranga e āhei ki te rongo i ētahi mōhiohio i te kāwanatanga kīngi o Donggala, he wāhi ki te raki o Palu e tata ake ana ki te poka pū o te rū whenua e 7.5 te kaha.
Kei Palu, neke atu i te 16,000 tāngata i whakawāteatia i muri i te pānga mai o te aituā.
Anei ētahi meka nui mō Palu me Donggala, ki te motu o Sulawesi:
Ko Palu te tāone matua o te porowini o Waenga Sulawesi, ko te wāhi ki te pito o tētahi whanga whāiti ki te tai hauāuru o te motu o Sulawesi, ko te whakatau tata o te taupori e 379,800 i te tau 2017.
I te whakanui te tāone nui i te huri tau 40 i te wā i pā mai te rū whenua me te tai āniwhaniwha.
Ko Donggala he kāwanatanga kīngi e whātoro atu ana i te 300 kiromita (180 māero) o te tapātai ki te marangai-mā-uru o te motu o Sulawesi.
Ko te kāwanatanga kīngi, he takiwā whakahaere i raro i te porowini, i whai i te taupori 299,200 i te tau 2017.
Ko te hī ika me te pāmu ngā tino pūtake o te ōhanga o te porowini o Waenga Sulawesi, he tino pūtake ki te takiwā takutai o Donggala.
Ko te huke konukōreko he mea nui ki te porowini, engari ka noho te nuinga ki Morowali, ki te takutai tauaro ki Sulawesi.
Ko Palu me Donggala i pā atu ki ngā tai āniwhaniwha i ētahi wā i te 100 tau kua pahure ake nei, e ai ki te Pokapū Whakamauru Aituā.
I te tau 1938, neke atu i te 200 tāngata i mate i te tai āniwhaniwha, ā, i mōtī ngā whare rau ki Donggala.
Tērā te tai āniwhaniwha i pā ki Donggala ki te uru i te tau 1996, e whakamate ana i te tokoiwa.
E noho ana a Initonīhia ki te wāhi rū o te Niao Ahi o Te Moana-nui-a-Kiwa, ā, he riterite te whakapā mai a ngā rū whenua.
Anei ētahi o ngā rū whenua matua me ngā tai āniwhaniwha i ngā tau nō tata ake nei.
2004: He rū whenua matua ki te tai hauāuru o te porowini o Aceh ki Initonīhia ki Sumatra ki te raki i te tau 26 o Hakihea i tīmata i te tai āniwhaniwha i pā ki ngā motu 14, e whakamate ana i ngā tāngata 226,000 huri noa te tapātai o te Moana o Īnia, neke atu i te haurua ki Aceh.
2005: He raupapa rū whenua i pā ki te tai hauāuru o Sumatra i te mutunga o Poutūterangi me te tīmatanga o Paengawhāwhā.
He rau te hunga i mate ki te Motu o Nias, i waho atu o Sumatra.
2006: I pā te rū whenua e 6.8 te kaha ki te tonga o Java, te motu whai taupori nunui o Initonīhia, e tīmata ana i te tai āniwhaniwha i tukia ki te tai tonga, e whakamate ana tata ki te 700 tāngata.
2009: He rū whenua e 7.6 te kaha i pātata ki te tāone nui o Padang, te tāone nui matua o te porowini o Sumatra ki te Uru.
Neke atu i te 1,100 tāngata i mate.
2010: He rū whenua e 7.5 te kaha i pā ki tētahi o ngā motu o Mentawai, i waho atu o Sumatra, e tīmata ana i te tai āniwhaniwha e 10 mita te rahi i whakamōtī ai i ngā pā taihana me te whakamate i ngā tāngata e tōtahi ki te 300.
2016: He rū whenua pāpaku i pā ki te kāwanatanga kīngi o Pidie Jaya ki Aceh, e whakaaweawe ana i te urupatu me te hopohopo i te maumaharatanga a ngā tāngata i te whakangaromanga o te rū whenua whakamate me te tai āniwhaniwha i te tau 2004.
Kāore tētahi tai āniwhaniwha i tīmatatia i tēnei wā, engari neke atu i te 100 i mate i ngā whare hinga.
2018: He rū whenua matua i pā ki te motu tāpoi o Lombok i Initonīhia, e whakamate ana neke atu i te 500 tāngata, ko te nuinga ki te taha tūāraki o te motu.
Ka turaki te rū whenua i ngā whare e hia mano me te waiho i ngā tāpoi mano me te kore ara whakaputa.
I Whakarautia te Tama Mātāmua a Sarah Palin mō Ngā Hāmene Taikaha Kāinga
Ko Track Palin, te tama mātāmua o te kāwana o mua mō Alaska me te kaitono perehitini tuarua Sarah Palin, kua whakarautia mō ngā hāmene taikaha.
Ko Palin, e 29, o Wasilla, Alaska, i whakarautia i runga i te pāihi mō te taikaha kāinga, te raweke ki te pūrongorongo taikaha kāinga me te ātete whakarau, e ai ki te pūrongo i tukuna i tēnei Rāhoroi e ngā Alaska State Troopers.
E ai ki te pūrongo pirihimana, i te wā i whakamātau tētahi hoa wahine ki te waea atu ki te pirihimana ki te pūrongorongo i ngā hara whakapae, i tangohia e ia te waea i a ia.
Ka mauheretia a Palin ki te Mat-Su Pretrial Facility, ā, e mauheretia ana ki te pukapuka here $500 tītengi, i pūrongorongo KTUU.
I puta ia ki te kōti i te Rāhoroi, me tana whakahua “Kāore i hara, tino” i te wā i pātaihia mō tana kī, i pūrongorongo ai te hononga.
E toru ngā kinonga Karaehe A, ko te tikanga ia ka mauheretia pea mō te wā kāore e iti iho i te tau, ā, ka whainatia e $250,000.
Kua hāmenetia hoki ki te kinonga Karaehe B, e taea ai te whiu o te rā kotahi ki te whare herehere me te whaina $2,000.
Ehara tēnei i te wā tuatahi kua tukuna ngā hāmene taihara ki a Palin.
I te Hakihea i te tau 2017, i whakapaetia i patu ia i tana matua, a Todd Palin.
Ka waea atu tana whaea, a Sarah Palin, ki te pirihimana ki te pūrongorongo i te huaki whakapae.
Kei mua tonu te kēhi i te Kōti o ngā Ika ā Whiro o Alaska.
I te Kohitātea o te tau 2016 i hāmenetia ia ki te huaki kāinga, te raweke ki te pūrongorongo o te taihara taikaha kāinga, me te whiwhi ki te rākau patu i a ia e haurangi ana e pā ana ki taua mahinga.
I whakapae tana hoa kōhine i meke ia i a ia ki te kanohi.
I whakahētia a Sarah Palin e ngā rōpū ika ā whiro i te tau 2016 i muri i tana tūhono i ngā whanonga taikaha a tana tama ki te PTSD e puta mai ana i tana whakaritenga mahi ki Irāki.
He tai āniwhaniwha rū whenua ki Initonīhia: he rau i mate
Kāore e iti iho i te 384 ngā tāngata i mate i muri i te rū whenua i pā te motu o Sulawesi ki Initonīhia i te Rāmere.
Ka tīmata te rū whenua e 7.5 te kaha i te tai āniwhaniwha me te turaki i ngā kāinga mano.
Kua hinga te hikohiko me ngā whatunga whakawhitiwhiti kōrero me te kawatau ka piki ngā kōeke mate i ngā ra e heke mai nei.
Kua pā te rū whenua ki waho paku atu i Sulawesi ki waenga, he wāhi ki te kārapu o te tāone nui matua o Initonīhia, Jakarta.
He ataata e huri haere ana i te pae pāpāho pāpori e whakaatu ana i te wā o te papātanga.
He rau ngā tāngata i whakaemitia mō te taurima tātahi ki te tāone nui o Palu, kātahi ka tukituki te tai āniwhaniwha ki te ākau.
E kimi ana ngā kaiwhakapae aka haumi i te hāmene whakamate mō te whakaarotanga huaki whakatuatea NYC
E kimi ana ngā kaiwhakapae aka haumi i Niu Ioka i te hāmene whakamate mō Sayfullo Saipov, te whakaarotanga ki te huaki whakatuatea ki te Tāone Nui o Niu Ioka i whakamate i ngā tāngata tokowaru - he hāmene onge kāore i whakamahia ki te wāhanga whenua mō te taihara aka haumi i muri i te tau 1953.
Ko Saipov, 30, e ai ki te whakapae, i whakamahi i te taraka retireti Home Depot ki te whakahaere i te huaki ki tētahi ara paihikara ki te Huanui ki te Taha Uru ki Lower Manhattan, e tītipi ana i ngā haere raro me te kaieke paihikara i mua i tana haere i te Whiringa-ā-nuku.
Hei parahau i te hāmene whakamate, me hāpono ngā kaiwhakapae i “takune” a Saipov ki te whakamate i ngā kaupēhipēhi tokowaru me te “takune” ki te whakawhiu i te whara tinana taumaha, e ai ki te pānui o te whakaaro ki te kimi i te hāmene whakamate, i tukuna ki te Takiwā Whakatetonga o Niu Ioka.
I roto i aua hāmene e rua te āheinga o te hāmene whakamate, e ai ki te puka kōti.
I ngā wiki i muri i te huaki, ka whakapā te huri nui aka haumi i te tuhinga whakapae e 22-tatau tae atu ana ki ngā hāmene kōhuru e waru hei tautoko i te pakihi taihara, he mea whakamahi i te nuinga o te wā e ngā kaiwhakapae aka haumi ki ngā kēhi taihara whakariterite, me tētahi hāmene mō te taikaha me te urupatu i ngā motokā.
I hiahia te huaki i te “tino whakamahere me te whakaaro tōmua,” te kī a ngā kaiwhakapae, e whakaahua ana i te āhuatanga o te whakamahi a Saipov hei “ahikauri, whakawiri me te hīkaka.”
"Nā Sayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov i whakaaweawe i te whara, pāmamae, me te korenga ki ngā whānau me ngā hoa o Diego Enrique Angelini rātou ko Nicholas Cleves, ko Ann-Laure Decadt, ko Darren Drake, ko Ariel Erlij, ko Hernan Ferruchi, ko Hernan Diego Mendoza, ko Alejandro Damian Pagnucco," te kī a te pānui o te whakaaro.
Tokorima ngā kaupēhipēhi he tāpoi nō Āketina.
He tekau tau i muri i te wā i hāmenetia e te Takiwā Whakatetonga o Niu Ioka i te kēhi hāmene whakamate.
Ko te whakapaenga hara, a Khalid Barnes, i whakaharaina mō te kōhuru i ngā kaiwhakarato taru kino engari i te mutunga iho ka hāmenetia ki te tauoranga ki te whare herehere i te Mahuru i te tau 2009.
Ko te wā whakamutunga i whakamahia ai te hāmene whakamate ki te kēhi aka haumi Niu Ioka ko te tau 1953 mō Julius rāua ko Ethel Rosenberg, he tokorua whakamoe i whakamatea i muri i te whakaharatanga o te kara ki te mahi i te mahi tūtei mō te Uniana Tawhito o Rūhia i te wā o te Pakanga Makariri i ngā tau e rua i mua.
Ka whakamatea ngā Rosenbergs e rua mā te tūru hikohiko i te 19 o Pipiri i te tau 1953.
Ko Saipov, he tangata taketake nō Uzbekistan, i whakaatu i te kore hinapōuri i ngā rā me ngā marama i muri i te huaki, e ai ki ngā puka kōti.
I kī ia ki ngā kaititiro he pai ki a ia ana mahi, te kī a ngā pirihimana.
I kī a Saipov ki ngā mana whakahaere i whakaohoohotia ia ki te whakamahi i te huaki i muri i te mātakitaki i ngā ataata ISIS i runga i tana waea, e ai ki te tuhinga whakapae.
I tono hoki ia ki te whakaatu i te kara ISIS ki tana rūma hōhipera, te kī a ngā pirihimana.
Kua kī ia e pā ana ki te tuhinga whakapae 22-tatau kāore ia i hara.
Ko David Patton, tētahi o ngā kaiwawao tūmatanui aka haumi hei kanohi mō Saipov, i kī he “mārama te matekiri” nō rātou ki te whakataunga a te kaiwhakapae.
“E whakaaro ana mātou ko te whakataunga ki te kimi i te hāmene whakamate, kaua ko te whakaae ki te kī hara ki te tauoranga ki te whare herehere me te kore āhei kia tukuna ka whakaroa noa i te taumahatanga o ēnei mahinga mō ngā tāngata katoa i pāngia,” te kī a Patton.
I pātai kē te tīma kaiwawao a Saipov ki ngā kaiwhakapae kia kaua e kimi i te hāmene whakamate.
E ai ki tētahi MP Tory me tuku a NIGEL FARAGE hei kaiwhakahaere whakaritenga Brexit.
I oati a Nigel Farage ki te ‘whakaoreore i te taua tāngata’ i tēnei rā i tētahi tautohe ki te hui Tory.
I kī te kaiārahi Ukip o mua me ‘rongo i te wera’ ngā kaitōrangapū i ngā Eurosceptics - i te wā i marohi tētahi o ngā MP a Theresa May me tuku ia hei kaiwhakahaere whakaritenga ki te EU.
Ko te kaiwhakanoho ki muri tē panoni ko Peter Bone i kī ki te hīkoi i Birmingham ‘kua puta kē atu’ te UK ināianei mēnā ko Mita Farage te Hekeretari Brexit.
Engari ko te wero i arotia e Mihi May i te whakakotahi anō i āna kapa kua tino whakawehewehea kua tārarotia e ngā Tē Panoni tautoko i te Noho tonu i uru ki tētahi tautohe motuhake ki Brexit i roto i te tāone nui.
E takaoraora ana te pirimia ki te whakamau tonu i te haere o tana mahere tau Chequers i waenganui i ngā huaki i ngā Brexiteers, ngā Remainers me te EU.
Ka whakanonoi ngā haumi ka haere tonu tana mahi ki te whakatūturu i te whakaaetanga me Brussels ahakoa te tino rara - me te uruhi i ngā Eurosceptics me Reipa ki te kōwhiri i waenganui i tana pūhera me te ‘aneatanga’.
Ka kī a Mita Bone ki te huihuinga Leave Means Leave ki Solihull i pīrangi ia ki te ‘whiu atu Chequers’.
Ka marohi ia me tuku a Mita Farage hei aropā me te hoatu ki a ia te mahi whakahaere i ngā whakaritenga ki Brussels.
‘Mēnā koia te kaiwhakahaere, kua puta kē atu tātou ināianei’, tana kī.
I tāpiri atu te MP nō Wellingborough: ‘Ka tū au ki te tautoko i te Brexit engari me whiu atu tātou i Chequers.’
Ka whakarite i tana mautohenga ki te EU, ka kī ia: ‘Kāore tātou i whawhai i ngā pakanga o te ao kia tū hei pononga.
E pīrangi ana tātou ki te hanga i ō tātou ake ture ki tō tātou ake motu.’
Ka pana a Mita Bone i ngā marohi kua panoni te whakaaro tūmatanui i muri i te pōtitanga i te tau 2016: ‘Ko te whakaaro kua panoni ngā tāngata o Peretānia i ō rātou hinengaro, ā, kua pīrangi ki te noho he rūkahu rawa.’
Ko te Tory Brexiteer a Andrea Jenkyns i reira i te hīkoi, e kōrero ana ki ngā kaikawe kōrero: ‘E kī noa ana au: E te Pirimia, whakarongo ki ngā tāngata.
He kiriweti a Chequers ki te tūmatanui whānui, kāore e pōtitia e te Āpitihana, he kiriweti ki tō tātou pāti me ā tātou kaiwhakahē e hīkoikoi nei i ngā tiriti me te whakamahi kia pōtitia ai tātou i te tuatahi.
Tēnā koa whakangaro atu Chequers me te tīmata ki te whakarongo.’
I roto i te karere koi ki Mihi May, ka tāpiri atu: ‘Ka mau tonu ngā pirimia ki ā rātou tūranga mēnā ka pupuri i ā rātou oati.’
Ka kī a Mita Farage ki te huihuinga me whakamahi kia ‘rangona te wera’ e ngā kaitōrangapū mēnā e tata ana rātou ki te whakamoho i te whakataunga i whakamahia i te whakataunga ā iwi i te tau 2016.
‘He take whakawhirinaki i waenganui i a tātou - ngā tāngata - me te karangatanga tōrangapū,’ tana kī.
‘E pīrangi ana rātou ki te whakamoho i Brexit, ā, kei konei tātou i tēnei rā ki te kī atu ‘kāore mātou e whakaae ki taua mahi a koutou.’
I roto i te karere ki te mātoru matangareka i tāpiritia e ia: ‘Kei te pīrangi au kia uruhi koutou i tō tātou karangatanga tōrangapū, e tata ana ki te whakamoho i Brexit, kia rongo i te wera.
`’E whakaoreore ana mātou i te taua tāngata o tēnei motu i hōmai i te toanga ki Brexit, ā, ka kore e whakatā tae noa ki te wā kua tū tātou hei Peretānia motuhake, tino rangatira, whakahīhī.’
I taua wā, i hīkoi tonu ngā Remainers i Birmingham i mua i te whakatū i te huihuinga rua hāora ki te poka pū o te tāone nui.
He torutoru ngā kaiwhakahē i pōwhiriwhiri i ngā kara Tories Against Brexit i muri i te whakarewatanga o te rōpū i tēnei mutunga wiki.
I taunu te aropā nō Reipa a Lord Adonis i te ngā Tē Panoni mō ngā take whakahaumaru i pā ki a rātou ki te taupā pāti i te tuwheratanga o te hui.
‘Koinei ngā tāngata e kī mai ana ki a tātou ka āhei rātou ki te whakarite i ngā pūnaha IT me ngā hangarau katoa mō Kānata te mea te mea, mō te rohenga waku kore, mō te hoko wātea me ngā rohenga kore ki Airani,’ ka tāpiritia e ia.
‘He pōhauhau rawa.
Kāore kau e Brexit pai,’ i tāpiritia e ia.
Kei te whakarite a Warren ki te ‘āta titiro’ ki te whakataetae hei perehitini
E kī ana a Sen. Elizabeth Warren ka “āta titiro ki te whakataetae hei perehitini” i muri i ngā pōtitanga hei te Whiringa-ā-rangi.
E pūrongorongo ana te Boston Globe i kōrero mai te Manapori nō Massachusetts mō tana anamata i roto i te hōro tāone ki te uru o Massachusetts i te Rāhoroi.
Ko Warren, he kaiwerowero i a Perehitini Tānara Tānapu, e whakataetae ana kia pōtitia anōtia ā te Whiringa-ā-rangi ki te GOP state Rep. Geoff Diehl, te heamana taurua o te whakamataaratanga 2016 o Tānapu.
Kei roto ia i te whakapae e whakataetae ia ki a Tānapu hei te tau 2020.
Ko te mahi i te ahiahi o te Rāhoroi i Holyoke te tūtakitanga 36 ki ana kaipōti mā te whakamahi i te anga hōro tāone i muri i te urunga o Tānapu ki tana tari.
Ka pātai tētahi i tae mai mēnā e whakaaro ana ia ki te whakataetae hei perehitini.
Kua whakautu a Warren kua tae te wā “kia haere ngā wāhine ki Wahingitana ki te whakatikatika i tō tātou kāwanatanga pakaru, tae atu ana ki te wahine ki te tihi.”
Kua whakarau tētahi i te matenga pupuhi o Sims nō LSU.
Kua tauākī ngā pirihimana nō Baton Rouge, La., i te Rāhoroi kua whakarautia tētahi whakaarotanga mō te matenga pupuhi o te kaitākaro poitūkohu a Wayde Sims i te Rāmere.
Kua tauākī te Tari Pirihimana o Baton Rouge i te whakarau o Dyteon Simpson, 20, i te hui kawepūrongo ET i te 11 a.m.
I whakaputaina e rātou tētahi ataata o te puhinga i te Rāmere, e inoi ana mō te āwhina ki te tautuhi i te tāne i kitea ai ki te kiriata.
Ko Sims, 20, i pupuhia, ā, i mate e tata ana ki te takiwā o te Southern University i te wā moata i te Rāmere.
“I tūngia a Wayde Sims ki te taotūtanga pakūnga pū ki te upoko, ā, ko te otinga i mate rawa atu ia,” te kī a te tumuaki pirihimana Murphy J. Paul ki te hunga pāpāho i te Rāhoroi, e ai ki 247sports.
Ka hōkai a Wayde ki te wawao i tana hoa, ā, ka pupuhia e Simpson.
I uiuia a Simpson me te whāki i reira ia, me te whiwhi ki te rākau o te riri, ā, ka whāki nāna a Wayde Sims i pupuhi.
Ka whakarautia a Simpson me te kore mahinga, ā, ka mau hereheretia ki te Tari Pirihimana o te Pāriha o East Baton Rouge.
He teina e 6-pūtu-6 i tipu ake ki Baton Rouge, i tākaro a Sims i roto i ngā kēmu e 32 me ngā tīmata 10 i tērā kaupeka, ā, ko ana toharite 17.4 meneti, 5.6 māka, ā, 2.9 turapa ia kēmu.
Te Grand Prix a Rūhia: Ka whakatata a Lewis Hamilton ki te taitara o te ao i muri i ngā whakahau tīma i hoatu i te toanga i runga i a Sebastian Vettel
Ka mārama i te wā i māraurau a Valtteri Bottas i mua i a Lewis Hamilton i te Rāhoroi ko te ngā whakahau tīma a Mercedes e whai wāhi nui ki te whakataetae.
Mai i te pou, he pai te tīmatanga a Bottas, ā, ka tata hinga a Hamilton i a ia i tana wawao i tana tūnga i ngā huringa tuatahi e rua me te tono i a Vettel ki te huaki i tana hoa tīma.
Ka uru a Vettel ki ngā kōruarua, ā, ka waiho i a Hamilton ki te uru ki te waka haere i te waero o te rōpū, ka pēnei he mea whakatau.
Ka uru te Mercedes ki te kōruarua i te huringa i mua me te puta i muri i Vettel, engari ka puta a Hamilton i muri i te mahi wira-ki-te-wira i kitea ai te taraiwa nō Ferrari e whakawātea manauhea i te roto me te tūraru i muri i te nekehanga huarua ki te wawao i te kokonga tuatoru.
Ka tīmata a Max Verstappen i te rārangi whakamutunga o te tukutuku, ā, kua tae ki te tuawhitu i te mutunga o te huringa tuatahi i tana huritau 21.
Ka ārahi ia i te wāhanga nui o te whakataetae me te mau tonu i ana taea hei heipū i te otinga tere me te pāhi i a Kimi Raikkonen mō te tuawhā.
Meāke ka uru ki ngā kōruarua i te huringa 44 engari kāore e taea te whakapiki i tana tere i ngā huringa waru e toe ana i te rironga o te tuawhā e Raikkonen.
He rā uaua nā te mea he mahi pārekareka tā Valtteri i te mutunga wiki katoa, ā, he tino tangata hūmārie i muri ki te whakahau kia waiho i a au kia pāhi.
He mahi whakaharahara tā te tīma kia whiwhi ki te tuatahi tuarua,” te kī a Hamilton.
He Kino Rawa Taua Reo Ā-Tinana
I taunu a Tānara Tānapu i a Senator Dianne Feinstein ki tētahi huihuinga i te Rāhoroi nā tana tohe kāore ia i tuku i te reta nā Christine Blasey Ford e whakapae ana kua pāwhara te tautapa Kōti Hupirīmi a Brett Kavanaugh.
E kōrero ana ki tētahi huihuinga i West Virginia, kāore te perehitini i tino anga ki te whakataki i hoatu e Ford i mua i te Komiti Kaiwhakawā a te Hīnata, e kī kē ana ko ngā mahi ki te Hīnata i whakaatu ai ko ētahi tāngata he “hākere me te maniheko me te rūpahu.”
“Ko te mea kotahi ka puta ā ko te mea ātaahua e haere ana i ngā rā torutoru kua pahure ake nei ki te Hīnata, ina kite koe i te riri, ina kite koe i ngā tāngata e riri ana, e hākere ana, e maniheko ana, e rūpahu ana.” tana kī.
“Ina titiro koe ki ngā tukunga me ngā turuturu me tā rātou kī “Ō, ehara i au tēnā.
Ehara i au tēnā.”
Maumahara?
Dianne Feinstein, nāu te turuturu?
Maumahara i tana whakautu...i turuturu koe i te puka - “Ō, Ō, he aha?
Ō, kāore.
Kāore au i turuturu.”
Nā, taihoa mō tētahi meneti.
I turuturu mātou...Kāore, kāore mātou i turuturu,” tana tāpiritanga, i te āhuatanga o te senator.
I tukuna ki a Feinstein te reta e whakarite ana i ngā whakapae a Ford ki a Kavanaugh i te Pipiri, ā, i turuturua i mua i te Mahuru - engari i whakakore a Feinstein i te kōrero i puta mai te turuturu i tana tari.
“Kāore au i huna i ngā whakapae a Dr. Ford, kāore au i turuturu i tana kōrero,” te kī a Feinstein ki te komiti, te pūrongorongo a The Hill.
“I pātai mai ia kia noho muna ā ka noho muna pēnā i tāna i pātai ai.”
Engari kāore tana whakakore i tau ki tā te perehitini, i kī i te huihuinga pō i te Rāhoroi: “Pēnei taku kōrero, he kino rawa taua reo ā-tinana.
Tērā pea ehara i a ia, engari koinā te reo ā-tinana kino rawa kua kite au.”
E whakahaere tonu ana tana wawao i te tautapa Kōti Hupirīmi, kua whakapaetia he hīanga mahimahi e ētahi wāhine tokotoru, i whakaaro te Perehitini e whakamahi ana ngā Manapori i ngā whakapae hei tautoko i ō rātou ake wawata.
“Kua pūtohe rātou ki te whakahoki mai i te mana ahakoa pēhea e whakahokia ai.
Ka kite koe i te hākere, te maniheko, ā, hei aha mā rātou ngā tāngata e pāmamaetia, ngā mea e takahia e rātou ki te whiwhi ki te mana me te whakahaere,” ka pūrongorongo a Mediaite te kī a te perehitini.
Rīki rangatira: Ngā Dundee Stars 5-3 Belfast Giants
I hahau a Patrick Dwyer i ngā piro e rua mō ngā Giants ki Dundee.
I whakapai ngā Dundee Stars i te hinganga i te Rīki rangatira i te Rāmere ki ngā Belfast Giants i te toanga i te kēmu whakahoki 5-3 ki Dundee i te Rāhoroi.
Ka puta ki mua i te piro-rua a Giants nā ngā hahau a Patrick Dwyer rāua ko Francis Beauvillier.
Ka whakaōrite a Mike Sullivan rāua ko Jordan Cownie i te tīma hau kāinga i mua i te whakahokinga o te noho ki mua a ngā Giants.
Ka whakaōrite a Francois Bouchard mō Dundee i mua i ngā piro e rua a Lukas Lundvald Nielsen hei whakamau i te toanga.
Ko te hinganga tuatoru ki te Rīki Rangatira i tēnei kaupeka mō ngā tāngata a Adam Keefe, i puta mai i muri kia toa i a Dundee 2-1 ki Belfast i te pō o te Rāmere.
Koinei te tūtakitanga tuawhā o te kaupeka i waenga i ngā tīma e rua, ka toa ngā Giants i ngā kēmu e toru i mua.
Ko te tuatahi a Dwyer i puta mai i te meneti tuawhā i te 3:35 i runga i te āwhina a Kendall McFaull, me āwhina a David Rutherford ki te huarua i te noho ki mua i ngā meneti e whā i muri mai.
I roto i te wā tīmatanga oreore, I whakahoki mai a Sullivan ki te kēmu i te 13:10 i mua i te urunga a Matt Marquardt hei kaiwhakarato mō te whakaōritenga a Cownie i te 15:16.
Ka whakarite a Dwyer i puta ngā Giants ki mua i te taenga ki te whakatā i te hahau i tana piro tuarua o te pō i te mutunga o te wāhanga tuatahi.
Ka whakakotahi anō te tīma hau kāinga, ā, ka whakaōritea anō e Bouchard nā te piro tākaro kaha i te 27:37.
I mahi tahi a Cownie rāua ko Charles Corcoran ki te āwhina i a Nielsen kia whakaputa a Dundee ki mua mō te wā tuatahi i te kēmu i te tata otinga o te wāhanga tuarua, ā, ka whakarite ia i te toanga nā te tuarima mō tana tima i te haurua o te wāhanga whakamutunga.
Ko ngā Giants, kua hinga i ngā kēmu e whā o ngā kēmu e rima i mua, ka tākaro ki Milton Keynes i te kāinga hei tērā kēmu hei te Rāmere.
Ka Mate te Kaiwhakahaere Huarahi Rererangi kia Whakatūturu te Putanga o Ngā Rau i Runga Waka Rererangi
Ko tētahi kaiwhakahaere huarahi rererangi i Initonīhia e whakamihia hei tuahangata i muri i tana matenga i a ia e whakatūturu ana ko te waka rererangi e kawe ana i ngā rau tāngata i wehe haumaru i te papa.
Neke atu i te 800 tāngata i mate, ā, he tokomaha e ngaro ana i muri i te pānga o te rū whenua matua ki te motu o Sulawesi i te Rāmere, e tīmata ana i te tai āniwhaniwha.
E muia ana te takiwā ki ngā rūmuri, ā, he tokomaha e hopukia ki te paketai i te tāone nui o Palu.
Engari ahakoa ana hoamahi e kāwhaki ana kia whakarauoratia ai rātou, kāore te tangata 21 tau, a Anthonius Gunawan Agung e whakaae kia wehe i tana tūranga i roto i te pourewa e pīoioi tūperepere ana ki te tauranga wakarererangi ki Mutiara Sis Al Jufri Airport Palu.
I noho tonu ia kia whakatūturu ko te Batik Air Flight 6321, i runga i te papa taunga i taua wā, āhei ki te rere haumaru ake.
Kātahi ia ka peke i te pourewa whakahaere huarahi rererangi i te wā i pōhēhē ia e turaki ana.
Tāria te wā ka mate ia ki te hōhipera.
Ko te kī a te māngai mō Air Navigation Indonesia, Yohannes Sirait, tērā pea i whakarauoratia ngā tauoranga rau e tana whakataunga, te pūrongorongo a ABC News nō Ahitereiria.
I whakarite mātou i te toparere i Balikpapan i Kalimantan ki te hari i a ia ki tētahi hōhipera nui ake ki tētahi atu tāone nui.
He mea whakarapa i ngaro ia i a mātou i te ata nei i mua i te taenga mai o te toparere ki Palu.
“Ka whati tō mātou manawa ki te rongo i tēnei,” i tāpiri ia.
I taua wā, e māharahara ana ngā mana ka tae te rahinga mate ki ngā mano me te kī a te umanga whakamauru aituā o te motu ko te tomonga ki ngā tāone o Donggala, Sigi me Boutong e kōpiria ana.
“E whakaarohia ana kei te piki tonu te rahinga i te mea he maha ngā tūpāpaku i raro i te paenga, ā, he tokomaha kāore e taea te whātoro atu,” te kī a te māngai mō te umanga a Sutopo Purwo Nugroho.
I eke ngā ngaru ki te ono mita i whakamōtī i Palu e whakahaere i te tāpuketanga maha i te Rātapu.
Ko ngā wakarererangi hōia, arumoni hoki, e mau mai ana i te āwhina me ngā whakaputunga.
Ka kī a Risa Kusuma, tētahi whaea 35 ngā tau ki a Sky News: “Ia meneti ka haria mai waka harihari tūroro i ngā tūpāpaku.
He uaua te kite i te wā māori mā.
Kua pāhua ngā mākete-iti i ngā wāhi katoa.”
Ko te kī a Jan Gelfand, te tumuaki o te Rīpeka Whero o te Ao ki Initonīhia ki CNN: “Kei te omaoma te Rīpeka Whero o Initonīhia ki te āwhina i ngā whakarauora engari kāore mātou he aha te mea e kitea ai e rātou i reira.
He parekura kē, engari ka kino kē atu pea.”

Ko te kamupene wakarererangi i tukia ki te muriwai i Micronesia e kī ana ināianei e ngaro ana tētahi tangata, i muri ki te kī i mua kua haumaru te whakatahinga o ngā kaieke me ngā kaitaurima 47 i te wakarererangi e torongi ana.
I kī a Air Niugini i tētahi wewete mai i te ahiahi o te Rāhoroi, kāore e taea e ia te kaute i te kaieke tāne.
Kei te mahi tahi te kamupene wakarererangi me ngā mana ā-rohe, hōhipera me ngā kaititiro kia kite i te tāne.

I whakatakoto tētahi kaitātari i te rārangi wā o te pō i tahuna oratia tētahi wahine.

E hāmene ana tētahi nana nō Niu Ioka i tētahi tokorua mō te panatanga whakahāwea i muri i te whiwhi ki te kupu tuhi nō te whaea e amuamu ana he “tangata mangu anō.”

“Kei te pīrangi au ki te whakaatu ki a rāua, kāore koe e mahi pērā,” tana kī ki te Post i te Rāmere, e tāpiri ana “Kei te mōhio au he whakatoihara.”

Ka ‘heke’ te nama o ngā tangata paheke i raro i a Kim
Ko te nama o ngā tangata paheke nō Kōrea ki te Raki ki Kōrea ki te Tonga i heke i te urunga mai a Kim Jong-un ki te mana whakahaere i ngā tau e whitu i mua, te kī a tētahi kaihanga ture nō Kōrea ki te Tonga.
Ko Park Byeong-seug, e taki ana i te raraunga nō te manatū whakakotahi o te Tonga, i kī 1,127 ngā paheke i tērā tau - hei whakaōrite ki 2,706 i te tau 2011.

Ki a Haina he manene turekore ngā tāngata paheke, kaua ko te taurewa, ā, he maha ngā wā ka whakahokia me te ringa kaha.
Ko te whanaungatanga i waenganui i te Raki me te Tonga - ko te āhua nei e whawhai tonu ana - kua piki i ngā marama tata.

Ka kīia a Brett Kavanaugh he “keka,” e Nancy Pelosi me te kī kāore e tau ki te whakarato ki te Hūpirimi Kōti.

I whakapono a Pelosi i whakatūturu te whakaaturanga a Kavanaugh kāore e taea e ia te whakarato ki te Hūpirimi Kōti, nā te mea i whakaatu tana ngākaukino ki ngā Manapori.
